                DIAGMODE        EQU          0
                DOS33B          EQU          1
                ULC             EQU          0                         ;1=ASM with lower case patch

                ;
                ;EQUATES REQD TO FIND THINGS IN APPLE II
                ;
                SETVID          EQU          $FE93
                SETKBD          EQU          $FE89
                PROMPT          EQU          $33                       ; PROMPT CHAR
                OUTSW           EQU          $36                       ; OUTPUT VECTOR SWITCH
                INSW            EQU          $38                       ; INPUT VECTOR SWITCH
                ZPGWRK          EQU          $40                       ; ZERO PAGE WORK CELL
                CNUM            EQU          $44                       ; CONVERTED NUMERIC
                LBUFF           EQU          $200                      ; LINE BUFFER
                MULT            EQU          $FB63                     ; MULT ROUTINE
                INPRT           EQU          $FE8B                     ; SET IN PORT
                OUTPRT          EQU          $FE95                     ; SET OUT PORT
                IBCHN           EQU          $E836                     ; BASIC RUN
                IBLMEM          EQU          $4A                       ; BASIC LOW MEM
                IBHMEM          EQU          $4C                       ; INTEGER BASIC HIMEM
                IBSOP           EQU          $CA                       ; INTEGER BASIC START OF CGM
                IBBRK           EQU          $E3E3                     ; BASIC BREAK
                IBGO            EQU          $E000                     ; BASIC ENTRY POINT
                IBCONT          EQU          $E003                     ; BASIC CONTINUE ENTRY POINT
                IBSOV           EQU          $CC                       ; BASIC START OF VARIABLES
                ASSOP           EQU          $67                       ; AS START OF PROGRAM
                ASEOP           EQU          $AF                       ; AS END OF PROGRAM
                ASEOP2          EQU          $69                       ; AS END-OF PGM 2
                ASHM1           EQU          $73                       ; AS HIGH MEM 1
                ASHM2           EQU          $6F                       ; AS HIGH MEM 2
                ASRNX           EQU          $D6                       ;AS RUN-ONLY FLAG
                ASONERR         EQU          $D8                       ;AS ON-ERR GOTO FLAG
                ASLMEM          EQU          ASSOP                     ; AS LOW MEM
                ASBRK1          EQU          $D865                     ; AS ROM BREAK
                ASBRK2          EQU          $1067                     ; AS RAM BREAK
                ASCNTU1         EQU          $D43C
                ASCNTU2         EQU          $C3C
                ASRSEQ1         EQU          $D4F2
                ASRSEQ2         EQU          $CF2
                AITSTL          EQU          $E000                     ; AS 1 IB TEST LOC
                ATSTV           EQU          $4C                       ; AS TEST VALUE
                ITSTV           EQU          $20                       ; IB TEST VALUE
                BOOTSL          EQU          $2E                       ; BOOT FROM SLOT
                ZPGFCB          EQU          $42                       ; ZERO PAGE WORK CELL
                MONRST          EQU          $FF65                     ;MONITOR RESET ENTRY
                MONBRK          EQU          $FA59                     ;MONITOR BREAK FUNCTION
                IORTS           EQU          $FF58                     ;KNOWN RTS IN MONITOR ROM
                HOME            EQU          $FC58
                PRINT           EQU          $FDED
                GETKEY          EQU          $FD0C
                INSDS2          EQU          $F88E
                LENGTH          EQU          $2F
                ZRSET           EQU          $3F2                      ;NEW MONITOR ROM RESET VECTOR
                PWCNST          EQU          $3F4                      ;NEW MONITOR ROM POWER UP CONSTANT
                ;;;                REP          40
                *
                *
                                ORG          ORIGIN
                *
                *
                ;;;                REP          40
                ;;;                PAGE
1b00 4c 84 1d   BEGIN           JMP          DBINIT
                ;
                DOSREL          EQU          *
                ;
                ;GET RELOCATION PARMS
                ;
                DR0             EQU          *
                LOC1            EQU          $26
1b03 a9 bf                      LDA          #$BF                      ; START AT BF00
1b05 85 41                      STA          ZPGWRK+1                  ; TO LOOK FOR
1b07 a2 00                      LDX          #0                        ; HIGH RAM
1b09 86 40                      STX          ZPGWRK
1b0b a0 00      DR0A            LDY          #0                        ; APPLE TEST
                DR1B            EQU          *
1b0d a1 40                      LDA          (ZPGWRK,X)
1b0f 85 26                      STA          LOC1
1b11 98         DR1             TYA
1b12 45 26                      EOR          LOC1
1b14 85 26                      STA          LOC1
1b16 98                         TYA
1b17 41 40                      EOR          (ZPGWRK,X)
1b19 81 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK,X)
1b1b c5 26                      CMP          LOC1
1b1d d0 05                      BNE          DR1A
1b1f c8                         INY
1b20 d0 ef                      BNE          DR1
1b22 f0 04                      BEQ          DR2                       ; BR IF TOOK
                DR1A            EQU          *
1b24 c6 41                      DEC          ZPGWRK+1                  ; NOT RAM
1b26 d0 e3                      BNE          DR0A                      ; TRY NEXT PAGE
                ;
                DR2             EQU          *
                ;
1b28 a5 41                      LDA          ZPGWRK+1                  ;BEGIN PATCH TO INSURE   *****
1b2a 29 df                      AND          #$DF                      ; PROPER HIGH MEMORY CHECK.
1b2c 85 43                      STA          ZPGFCB+1                  ;(DOS MASTER 3.1 CONTAINS
1b2e 86 42                      STX          ZPGFCB                    ; THIS ROUTINE STARTING AT LOCATION
1b30 a1 42                      LDA          (ZPGFCB,X)                ; $3540)
1b32 48                         PHA
1b33 85 26                      STA          LOC1                      ;SAVE TEST VALUE
1b35 98         DR2A            TYA                                    ;(FIRST TIME Y=0)
1b36 45 26                      EOR          LOC1                      ;TEST EACH (ALLEDGED) MEMORY BYTE
1b38 85 26                      STA          LOC1                      ; 256 TIMES TO DETERMINE IF
1b3a 98                         TYA                                    ; IT IS REALLY GOOD MEMORY AND
1b3b 41 40                      EOR          (ZPGWRK,X)                ; MIRRORED 8K LOWER IN RAM.
1b3d 81 42                      STA          (ZPGFCB,X)
1b3f c5 26                      CMP          LOC1                      ;DID IT PASS THIS TIME?
1b41 d0 09                      BNE          DR2B                      ; BYTE NOT MIRRORED, THEN GOOD MEMORY
1b43 c8                         INY                                    ;MAYBE IT WAS COINCIDENCE
1b44 d0 ef                      BNE          DR2A                      ;BRANCH UNLESS IT'S MATCHED 256 TIMES
1b46 a4 43                      LDY          ZPGFCB+1                  ;HIMEM IS 8K LOWER THAN WAS
1b48 68                         PLA                                    ;ORIGINALLY THOUGHT!
1b49 4c 51 1b                   JMP          DR2C
1b4c 68         DR2B            PLA                                    ;ORIGINAL HIMEM PROVED GOOD
1b4d 81 42                      STA          (ZPGFCB,X)                ;RESTORE BYTE ORIGINALLY MESSED WITH.
1b4f a4 41                      LDY          ZPGWRK+1                  ;END OF PATCH   *****
1b51 c8         DR2C            INY                                    ; NEW END OF DOS
1b52 8c 7d 1c                   STY          NEPAGE
1b55 38                         SEC
1b56 98                         TYA
1b57 ed 7e 1c                   SBC          DOSLNG                    ; MINUS DOS LENGTH
1b5a 8d 7c 1c                   STA          NSPAGE                    ; IS NEW START OF DOS
1b5d 38                         SEC
1b5e ed 7a 1c                   SBC          RSPAGE                    ; MINUS OLD DOS START
1b61 f0 9d                      BEQ          BEGIN                     ; (BREIF NO DELTA)
1b63 8d 7f 1c                   STA          DELTA                     ; IS DELTA
1b66 ad 7a 1c                   LDA          RSPAGE                    ; RESET START PAGE TO NORMAL
1b69 8d 0d 1d                   STA          ASTART+1
                ;
1b6c a9 1d                      LDA          #<DBINIT                  ; RESET PI RTN TO NORMAL
1b6e 8d 49 37                   STA          DI3+2
1b71 a9 84                      LDA          #>DBINIT
1b73 8d 48 37                   STA          DI3+1
                ;
                ;RELOCATE ADR TABLES
                ;
1b76 a2 00                      LDX          #0
1b78 86 40                      STX          ZPGWRK
                DR3             EQU          *
1b7a bd 29 1c                   LDA          ADRTAB+1,X
1b7d a8                         TAY
1b7e bd 2a 1c                   LDA          ADRTAB+2,X
1b81 85 41                      STA          ZPGWRK+1
1b83 4c 93 1b                   JMP          DR5
                ;
                DR4             EQU          *
1b86 18                         CLC
1b87 b1 40                      LDA          (ZPGWRK),Y
1b89 6d 7f 1c                   ADC          DELTA
1b8c 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y
1b8e c8                         INY
1b8f d0 02                      BNE          DR5
1b91 e6 41                      INC          ZPGWRK+1
1b93 c8         DR5             INY
1b94 d0 02                      BNE          DR6
1b96 e6 41                      INC          ZPGWRK+1
                ;
                DR6             EQU          *
1b98 a5 41                      LDA          ZPGWRK+1
1b9a dd 2c 1c                   CMP          ADRTAB+4,X
1b9d 90 e7                      BCC          DR4
1b9f 98                         TYA
1ba0 dd 2b 1c                   CMP          ADRTAB+3,X
1ba3 90 e1                      BCC          DR4
                ;
1ba5 8a                         TXA
1ba6 18                         CLC
1ba7 69 04                      ADC          #4
1ba9 aa                         TAX
1baa ec 28 1c                   CPX          ADRTAB
1bad 90 cb                      BCC          DR3
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;RELOCATE CODE
                ;
1baf a2 00                      LDX          #0
1bb1 8e 9c 33   DR7             STX          TEMP1
                ;
1bb4 bd 5a 1c                   LDA          CDETAB+1,X                ; GET A START OF CODE ADR
1bb7 85 40                      STA          ZPGWRK                    ; PUT IN ZPG
1bb9 bd 5b 1c                   LDA          CDETAB+2,X
1bbc 85 41                      STA          ZPGWRK+1
                ;
1bbe a2 00      DR8             LDX          #0
1bc0 a1 40                      LDA          (ZPGWRK,X)                ; GET OP CODE
1bc2 20 8e f8                   JSR          INSDS2                    ; GO FIND OUT HOW LONG
                ;
1bc5 a4 2f                      LDY          LENGTH                    ; GET HOW LONG
1bc7 c0 02                      CPY          #2                        ; IF IT AIN'T
1bc9 d0 11                      BNE          DR9                       ; 3 THEN DON'T RELOC
1bcb b1 40                      LDA          (ZPGWRK),Y                ; GET PAGE FROM INST
1bcd cd 7a 1c                   CMP          RSPAGE                    ; IF PAGE < REL START
1bd0 90 0a                      BCC          DR9                       ; THEN IGNOR
1bd2 cd 7b 1c                   CMP          REPAGE                    ; IF PAGE >= REL END
1bd5 b0 05                      BCS          DR9                       ; THEN IGNORE
1bd7 6d 7f 1c                   ADC          DELTA                     ; ELSE ADD DELTA
1bda 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y                ; TO RELOCATE
                ;
1bdc 38         DR9             SEC
1bdd a5 2f                      LDA          LENGTH                    ; ADD LENGTH
1bdf 65 40                      ADC          ZPGWRK                    ; TO PC
1be1 85 40                      STA          ZPGWRK
1be3 a9 00                      LDA          #0
1be5 65 41                      ADC          ZPGWRK+1
1be7 85 41                      STA          ZPGWRK+1
                ;
1be9 ae 9c 33                   LDX          TEMP1                     ; CHECK FOR END
1bec dd 5d 1c                   CMP          CDETAB+4,X                ; OF CODE SEGMENT
1bef 90 cd                      BCC          DR8                       ; BR NOT END
1bf1 a5 40                      LDA          ZPGWRK
1bf3 dd 5c 1c                   CMP          CDETAB+3,X
1bf6 90 c6                      BCC          DR8                       ; BR NOT END
                ;
1bf8 8a                         TXA
1bf9 18                         CLC
1bfa 69 04                      ADC          #4                        ; INCREMENT TABLE INDEX
1bfc aa                         TAX
1bfd ec 59 1c                   CPX          CDETAB                    ; DONE
1c00 90 af                      BCC          DR7                       ; BR IF NOT
                ;
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;MOVE TO RELOCATED CODE
                ;
1c02 a9 3f                      LDA          #<(ENDOFDOS-$80)
1c04 85 41                      STA          ZPGWRK+1                  ; ZPGWRK=FROM
1c06 ac 7d 1c                   LDY          NEPAGE
1c09 88                         DEY
1c0a 84 43                      STY          ZPGFCB+1                  ; ZPGFCB = TOO
1c0c a9 00                      LDA          #0
1c0e 85 40                      STA          ZPGWRK
1c10 85 42                      STA          ZPGFCB
1c12 a8                         TAY
                ;
1c13 b1 40      DR10            LDA          (ZPGWRK),Y                ; BYTE FROM
1c15 91 42                      STA          (ZPGFCB),Y                ; BYTE TO
1c17 c8                         INY                                    ; INCREMENT
1c18 d0 f9                      BNE          DR10                      ; BR NOT FULL PAGE
1c1a ce 80 1c                   DEC          DPGCNT                    ; DECREMENT PAGE CNT
1c1d f0 06                      BEQ          DR11                      ; BR IF DONE
1c1f c6 41                      DEC          ZPGWRK+1                  ; INC FROM PAGE
1c21 c6 43                      DEC          ZPGFCB+1                  ; INC TOO PAGE
1c23 d0 ee                      BNE          DR10                      ; MOVE PAGE
                ;
1c25 4c 54 1e   DR11            JMP          DBVECT+3                  ; DONE
                ;;;                PAGE
1c28 24         ADRTAB          DFB          9*4
1c29 00 1d                      DW           SAT1
1c2b 56 1d                      DW           EAT1
1c2d 58 1d                      DW           RUN
1c2f 5a 1d                      DW           RUN+2
1c31 64 1d                      DW           IBVT+2
1c33 66 1d                      DW           IBVT+4
1c35 6c 1d                      DW           AS1VT
1c37 70 1d                      DW           AS1VT+4
1c39 78 1d                      DW           AS2VT
1c3b 7c 1d                      DW           AS2VT+4
1c3d 7e 1d                      DW           AS2VT+6
1c3f 80 1d                      DW           AS2VT+8
1c41 c1 2a                      DW           SAT2
1c43 fd 2a                      DW           EAT2
1c45 e4 37                      DW           BAIOB
1c47 e8 37                      DW           ADOSLD+2
1c49 ee 37                      DW           IBDCTP
1c4b f0 37                      DW           IBDCTP+2
1c4d 00 00 00                   DFB          0,0,0,0
1c50 00
1c51 00 00 00                   DFB          0,0,0,0
1c54 00
1c55 00 00 00                   DFB          0,0,0,0
1c58 00
                CDETAB          EQU          *
1c59 20                         DFB          8*4
1c5a 84 1d                      DW           SC1
1c5c 84 28                      DW           EC1
1c5e fd 2a                      DW           SC2
1c60 97 33                      DW           EC2
1c62 5d 36                      DW           SC3
1c64 e0 37                      DW           EC3
1c66 56 3c                      DW           SWADR1
1c68 df 3c                      DW           EWADR1
1c6a 00 38                      DW           ASC1
1c6c 11 3a                      DW           AEC1
1c6e 69 3a                      DW           PSC1
1c70 94 3a                      DW           PEC1
1c72 00 3d                      DW           ASC2
1c74 a8 3f                      DW           AEC2
1c76 c8 3f                      DW           SDP1
1c78 ff 3f                      DW           EDP1
1c7a 1d         RSPAGE          DFB          <START
1c7b 40         REPAGE          DFB          <ENDOFDOS
                ;
1c7c 00         NSPAGE          DFB          0
1c7d 00         NEPAGE          DFB          0
                ;
1c7e 23         DOSLNG          DFB          <(ENDOFDOS-START)
                ;
1c7f 00         DELTA           DFB          0
1c80 23         DPGCNT          DFB          <(ENDOFDOS-START)

                HEREL           EQU          >*
                REMDR           EQU          256-HEREL
                                ORG          *+REMDR

                START           EQU          *
                SAT1            EQU          *
1d00 d3 1c      FTAB            DW           *-45                      ; START OF FTABS
1d02 81 1e      CINA            DW           CHRIN                     ; CHAR IN ADR
1d04 bd 1e      COUTA           DW           CHROUT                    ; CHAR OUT ADR
1d06 75 2a      FN1ADR          DW           FNAME1
1d08 93 2a      FN2ADR          DW           FNAME2

1d0c 00 1b      ASTART          DW           BEGIN                     ; CHANGED TO START BY RELOCATE
1d0e bb 35      CCBADR          DW           CCB

                OUTSVT          EQU          *                         ; CHAR OUTPUT STATE VECTOR TABLE
1d10 ea 1e                      DW           COS0-1

1d1c 70 1f                      DW           COS6-1
                ;COMMAND EXECUTION TABLE
                CMDETB          EQU          *

                EAT1            EQU          *

                ;NON-RELOCATING ADRS

                IBASVT          EQU          *
1d56 36 e8      CHAIN           DW           IBCHN
1d58 e5 24      RUN             DW           IBRUN
1d5a e3 e3      BREAK           DW           IBBRK
1d5c 00 e0      GO              DW           IBGO
1d5e 03 e0      CONT            DW           IBCONT                    ; BASIC CONT ENTRY POINT
1d60 00 00      ASEQ            DW           0
1d62 36 e8      IBVT            DW           IBCHN
1d64 e5 24                      DW           IBRUN
1d66 e3 e3                      DW           IBBRK
1d68 00 e0                      DW           IBGO
1d6a 03 e0                      DW           IBCONT
                IBVTL           EQU          *-IBVT
                ;
1d6c fc 24      AS1VT           DW           ASRUN1
1d6e fc 24                      DW           ASRUN1
1d70 65 d8                      DW           ASBRK1
1d72 00 e0                      DW           IBGO
1d74 3c d4                      DW           ASCNTU1
1d76 f2 d4                      DW           ASRSEQ1
                AS1VTL          EQU          *-AS1VT
                ;
1d78 06 25      AS2VT           DW           ASRUN2
1d7a 06 25                      DW           ASRUN2
1d7c 67 10                      DW           ASBRK2
1d7e 84 1d                      DW           DBINIT
1d80 3c 0c                      DW           ASCNTU2
1d82 f2 0c                      DW           ASRSEQ2
                AS2VTL          EQU          *-AS2VT
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;DOS BASIC INTERPRETER - INITIAL ENTRY
                ;
                SC1             EQU          *
                DBINIT          EQU          *
1d84 ad e9 37                   LDA          IBSLOT                    ; GET BOOT SLOT
1d87 4a                         LSR          A
1d88 4a                         LSR          A
1d89 4a                         LSR          A
1d8a 4a                         LSR          A
1d8b 8d 6a 2a                   STA          CS                        ; SET AS CUURENT SLOT
1d8e ad ea 37                   LDA          IBDRVN                    ; GET BOOT DRIVE NUMBER
1d91 8d 68 2a                   STA          CD                        ; SET AS CURRENT DRIVE
1d94 ad 00 e0                   LDA          AITSTL                    ; GET APPLESOFT/IB TEST
1d97 49 20                      EOR          #ITSTV                    ; IF AS THEN
1d99 d0 11                      BNE          IAS1                      ; GO TO AS INIT
                ;;ELSE INIT FOR IB
1d9b 8d b6 2a                   STA          ASIBSW                    ; SET SW FOR IB
1d9e a2 0a                      LDX          #IBVTL                    ; GET IB VT LENGTH
1da0 bd 61 1d   IIB1            LDA          IBVT-1,X                  ; MOVE IB ADDR
1da3 9d 55 1d                   STA          IBASVT-1,X
1da6 ca                         DEX
1da7 d0 f7                      BNE          IIB1
1da9 4c bc 1d                   JMP          INITAA
                ;
                IAS1            EQU          *
1dac a9 40                      LDA          #$40                      ; INDICATE ROM APPLESOFT
1dae 8d b6 2a                   STA          ASIBSW
1db1 a2 0c                      LDX          #AS1VTL
1db3 bd 6b 1d   IAS1A           LDA          AS1VT-1,X                 ; MOVE ROM AS ADRS
1db6 9d 55 1d                   STA          IBASVT-1,X
1db9 ca                         DEX
1dba d0 f7                      BNE          IAS1A
                ;
                INITAA          EQU          *
1dbc 38                         SEC                                    ; INDICATE INIT
1dbd b0 12                      BCS          INITA
1dbf ad b6 2a   DBRST           LDA          ASIBSW                    ;GET APPLESOFT/INITGER BASIC FLAG.
1dc2 d0 04                      BNE          INITA1                    ;BRANCH IF NOT INTIGER BASIC
1dc4 a9 20                      LDA          #ITSTV                    ;GET INTIGER TEST VALUE AND GO SET
1dc6 d0 05                      BNE          INITA2                    ; ROM SWITCH TO 'IB'. (BRANCH ALWAYS)
1dc8 0a         INITA1          ASL          A                         ;TEST FOR ROM APPLESOFT
1dc9 10 05                      BPL          INITA3                    ;BRANCH IF RAM VERSION
1dcb a9 4c                      LDA          #ATSTV                    ;GET APPLESOFT TEST VALUE AND GO SET
1dcd 20 b2 25   INITA2          JSR          SWTST                     ;GO SELECT PROPER ROM BASIC.
1dd0 18         INITA3          CLC                                    ; INDICATE RESET
                ;
                INITA           EQU          *
1dd1 08                         PHP                                    ; SAVE INIT/RESET
1dd2 20 51 28                   JSR          MVCSW                     ; GO MOVE CHAR SWITCH
1dd5 a9 00                      LDA          #0                        ; CLR MONITOR MODES
1dd7 8d 5e 2a                   STA          MONMOD
                ;
1dda 8d 52 2a                   STA          OSTATE                    ; CLEAR OUTSTATE AND EXECUTE STATE
1ddd 28                         PLP                                    ; GET INIT/RESET
1dde 6a                         ROR          A                         ; SHIFT CARRY TO MSB
1ddf 8d 51 2a                   STA          ISTATE                    ; SAVE INSTATE
1de2 30 03                      BMI          INITB                     ; BR IF INIT
1de4 6c 5e 1d                   JMP          (CONT)                    ; GO TO CONTINUE ENTRY
1de7 6c 5c 1d   INITB           JMP          (GO)                      ; GO TO GO ENTRY
                ;;;                PAGE
                INITC           EQU          *
1dea 0a                         ASL          A                         ; OF ISTATE NOT ON
1deb 10 19                      BPL          INITD                     ; THEN NOT RAM AS
1ded 8d b6 2a                   STA          ASIBSW                    ; SET RAM AS
1df0 a2 0c                      LDX          #AS2VTL
1df2 bd 77 1d   IAS2A           LDA          AS2VT-1,X                 ; MOVE RAM AS ADRS
1df5 9d 55 1d                   STA          IBASVT-1,X
1df8 ca                         DEX
1df9 d0 f7                      BNE          IAS2A

                SC1X            EQU          *

                CNF             EQU          *                         ; COMMAND NOT FOUND

                ;
                ; SYNTAX - FIGURE OUT WHAT WE GOT HERE

                SYNTAX          EQU          *

                SN10            EQU          *                         ; FILE NAMES NOT REQD

                ; SOPTS - LOOK FOR SYNTAX OPTIONS

                SOPTS           EQU          *

20e5 ad 5d 2a                   LDA          LBUFD                     ; SET PASS 1
                ;
20e8 20 a4 21   SP1             JSR          GNBC                      ; GO GET NON-BLANK CHAR
20eb d0 1f                      BNE          SP2                       ; BR IF NOT COMMA OR CR
20ed c9 8d                      CMP          #$8D                      ; IF CHAR IS COMMA
20ef d0 f7                      BNE          SP1                       ; THEN GO GET CHAR
                ;
20f1 ae 5f 2a                   LDX          CMDNO                     ; OPTIONS INPUT = I
20f4 ad 65 2a                   LDA          INOPTS                    ; ALLOW OPTS = A
20f7 1d 0a 29                   ORA          CMDSTB+1,X                ; IF (A OR I)
20fa 5d 0a 29                   EOR          CMDSTB+1,X                ; XOR A NOT = 0 THEN
20fd d0 93                      BNE          SERR1                     ; WE HAVE UNALLOWED OPTIONS
                ;
20ff ae 63 2a                   LDX          TEMP1A                    ; IF THIS IS PASS 2
2102 f0 76                      BEQ          CMDGO                     ; THEN DONE,
2104 8d 63 2a                   STA          TEMP1A                    ; ELSE SET PASS
2107 8e 5d 2a                   STX          LBUFD                     ; RESTORE LBUFD AND
210a d0 dc                      BNE          SP1                       ; GO DO PASS 2
                ;
210c a2 0a      SP2             LDX          #OPT1L                    ; COMPARE CHAR HAVE WITH
210e dd 40 29   SP3             CMP          OPTAB1-1,X                ; CHARS IN OPT TABLE
2111 f0 05                      BEQ          SP4                       ; IF FOUND CONTINUE,
2113 ca                         DEX
2114 d0 f8                      BNE          SP3                       ; IF NOT FOUND
2116 f0 b6      SERR2A          BEQ          SERR2                     ; THEN SYNTAX ERROR
                ;
2118 bd 4a 29   SP4             LDA          OPTAB2-1,X                ; IF CORRESPONDING OP TAB 2 IS
211b 30 47                      BMI          SP8                       ; MINUS THEN IT MONITOR BITS
211d 0d 65 2a                   ORA          INOPTS
2120 8d 65 2a                   STA          INOPTS
2123 ca                         DEX
                ;
2124 8e 64 2a                   STX          TEMP2A                    ; ELSE A NUMERIC MUST FOLLOW
2127 20 b9 21                   JSR          GETNUM                    ; FOLLOW
212a b0 a2                      BCS          SERR2
                ;
212c ad 64 2a                   LDA          TEMP2A                    ; GET IOTION NUMBER
212f 0a                         ASL          A                         ; MULT BY 4
2130 0a                         ASL          A
2131 a8                         TAY
                ;
2132 a5 45                      LDA          CNUM+1                    ; IF RESULT NUM HI IS
2134 d0 09                      BNE          SP5                       ; GT 0, THEN GT LOW RANGE
2136 a5 44                      LDA          CNUM                      ; TEST RESULT LOW
2138 d9 55 29                   CMP          OPTAB3,Y                  ; WITH LOW RANGE (LOW)
213b 90 8c                      BCC          SERR3                     ; BR IF RESULT < LR
213d a5 45                      LDA          CNUM+1
213f d9 58 29   SP5             CMP          OPTAB3+3,Y
2142 90 0b                      BCC          SP6                       ; BR IF LESS
2144 d0 83      SERR3A          BNE          SERR3                     ; BR IF GREATER
2146 a5 44                      LDA          CNUM
2148 d9 57 29                   CMP          OPTAB3+2,Y
214b 90 02                      BCC          SP6                       ; BR IF LESS
214d d0 f5                      BNE          SERR3A                    ; BR IF GREATER
                ;
214f ad 63 2a   SP6             LDA          TEMP1A                    ; IF PASS 1, THEN
2152 d0 94                      BNE          SP1                       ; DONT STORE RESULT
2154 98                         TYA
2155 4a                         LSR          A
2156 a8                         TAY
                ;
2157 a5 45                      LDA          CNUM+1                    ; STORE THE RESULT
2159 99 67 2a                   STA          CUROPT+1,Y
215c a5 44                      LDA          CNUM
215e 99 66 2a                   STA          CUROPT,Y
2161 4c e8 20   SP7             JMP          SP1                       ; GO FOR NEXT OPT
                ;
                SP8             EQU          *                         ; MONITOR REQ
2164 48                         PHA                                    ; SAVE TYPE REQ
2165 a9 80                      LDA          #CIO                      ; SET OPTION OF CIO
2167 0d 65 2a                   ORA          INOPTS
216a 8d 65 2a                   STA          INOPTS
216d 68                         PLA                                    ; RESTOERE REQ
216e 29 7f                      AND          #$7F                      ; CLEAR CIO
2170 0d 74 2a                   ORA          IMBITS                    ; OR WITH PREV IMBITS
2173 8d 74 2a                   STA          IMBITS
2176 d0 e9                      BNE          SP7                       ; GO FOR NEXT
                ;
2178 f0 9c                      BEQ          SERR2A                    ;BRANCH ALWAYS
                ;
217a 20 80 21   CMDGO           JSR          CMDGO1                    ; CMDGO - EXECUTE COMMAND
217d 4c 83 1f                   JMP          CERTN
                ;
                CMDGO1          EQU          *
2180 20 5b 27                   JSR          CLRSTS
2183 20 ae 21                   JSR          CLRCCB                    ; GO CLEAR CCB
                ECMD            EQU          *
2186 ad 5f 2a                   LDA          CMDNO                     ; COMMAND NO
2189 aa                         TAX                                    ; IS CMD EXEC TAB INDEX
218a bd 1f 1d                   LDA          CMDETB+1,X                ; GET CMD ADR
218d 48                         PHA                                    ; ONTO STACK
218e bd 1e 1d                   LDA          CMDETB,X
2191 48                         PHA
2192 60                         RTS                                    ; AND GOTO COMMAND
                
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; #   END OF FILE:  CMDSCAN

                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; GNXTC - GET NEXT CHAR
                ;
                GNXTC           EQU          *
2193 ae 5d 2a                   LDX          LBUFD
2196 bd 00 02                   LDA          LBUFF,X                   ; GET NEXT CHAR AND IF
2199 c9 8d                      CMP          #$8D                      ; IT IS A CR
219b f0 06                      BEQ          GNXTCR                    ; THEN RETURN WITHOUT
219d e8                         INX                                    ; INCR TO NEXT CHAR
219e 8e 5d 2a                   STX          LBUFD
21a1 c9 ac                      CMP          #','+$80                  ; TEST FOR COMMA
21a3 60         GNXTCR          RTS
                ;
                ; GNBC - GET NON BLANK CHAR
                ;
                GNBC            EQU          *
21a4 20 93 21                   JSR          GNXTC                     ; GO GET NEXT CHAR
21a7 f0 fa                      BEQ          GNXTCR                    ; BR IF COMMA OR CR
21a9 c9 a0                      CMP          #$A0                      ; IS IT BLANK
21ab f0 f7                      BEQ          GNBC                      ; BR IF BLANK
21ad 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;
                ; CLRCCB - CLEAR CCB
                ;
                CLRCCB          EQU          *
21ae a9 00                      LDA          #0
21b0 a0 16                      LDY          #CCBLEN                   ; CCBLENGTH
21b2 99 ba 35   CLC1            STA          CCB-1,Y                   ; CLEAR BYTE
21b5 88                         DEY
21b6 d0 fa                      BNE          CLC1
21b8 60                         RTS
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; GETNUM - CONVERT ASCII INPUT TO NUMERIC
                ;
                GETNUM          EQU          *
21b9 a9 00                      LDA          #0                        ; CLEAR WORK AREA
21bb 85 44                      STA          CNUM
21bd 85 45                      STA          CNUM+1
21bf 20 a4 21                   JSR          GNBC
21c2 08                         PHP
21c3 c9 a4                      CMP          #$A4
21c5 f0 3c                      BEQ          HEXNUM
21c7 28                         PLP
21c8 4c ce 21                   JMP          GN2A
                ;
21cb 20 a4 21   GN2             JSR          GNBC                      ; GET NEXT NON BLANK
                GN2A            EQU          *
21ce d0 06                      BNE          GN3                       ; BR NOT COMMA OR CR
21d0 a6 44                      LDX          CNUM                      ; X=RESULT LOW
21d2 a5 45                      LDA          CNUM+1                    ; Y=RESULT HI
21d4 18                         CLC
21d5 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;
21d6 38         GN3             SEC
21d7 e9 b0                      SBC          #$B0                      ; SUBTRACT ASCII 0
21d9 30 21                      BMI          GN4                       ; BR IF NOT NUM
21db c9 0a                      CMP          #10
21dd b0 1d                      BCS          GN4                       ; BR IF NOT NUM
21df 20 fe 21                   JSR          GN5                       ; OLD*2
21e2 65 44                      ADC          CNUM                      ; PLUS NEW
21e4 aa                         TAX
21e5 a9 00                      LDA          #0
21e7 65 45                      ADC          CNUM+1
21e9 a8                         TAY
21ea 20 fe 21                   JSR          GN5                       ; OLD*4
21ed 20 fe 21                   JSR          GN5                       ; OLD*8
21f0 8a                         TXA                                    ; OLD*8 + OLD*2 + NEW
21f1 65 44                      ADC          CNUM
21f3 85 44                      STA          CNUM                      ; =OLD*10 + NEW
21f5 98                         TYA
21f6 65 45                      ADC          CNUM+1
21f8 85 45                      STA          CNUM+1
21fa 90 cf                      BCC          GN2
                ;
                GN4             EQU          *
21fc 38                         SEC
21fd 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
                GN5             EQU          *
21fe 06 44                      ASL          CNUM                      ; CNUM * 2
2200 26 45                      ROL          CNUM+1
2202 60                         RTS
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                HEXNUM          EQU          *
2203 28                         PLP
                HN0             EQU          *
2204 20 a4 21                   JSR          GNBC                      ; GO GET CHAR
2207 f0 c5                      BEQ          GN2A                      ; BR IF CR OR COMMA
                ;
2209 38                         SEC
220a e9 b0                      SBC          #$B0                      ; CHAR - ASCII0
220c 30 ee                      BMI          GN4                       ; BR IF LT0
220e c9 0a                      CMP          #10                       ; IS IT LT10
2210 90 08                      BCC          HN1                       ; BR IF LT
2212 e9 07                      SBC          #$7                       ; SUB 7 FOR ASCII A
2214 30 e6                      BMI          GN4                       ; BR IF LT A
2216 c9 10                      CMP          #16                       ; TEST GT 15
2218 b0 e2                      BCS          GN4                       ; BR GT 15
221a a2 04      HN1             LDX          #4
221c 20 fe 21   HN2             JSR          GN5                       ; OLD*16
221f ca                         DEX                                    ;LOOP 4 TIMES ONLY
2220 d0 fa                      BNE          HN2
2222 05 44                      ORA          CNUM                      ; OR IN NEW
2224 85 44                      STA          CNUM                      ; SAVE NEW
2226 4c 04 22                   JMP          HN0                       ; GO FOR NEXT CHAR
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; EPR - EXECUTE PR#
                ;
                EPR             EQU          *
2229 a5 44                      LDA          CNUM                      ; GET PORT
222b 4c 95 fe                   JMP          OUTPRT                    ; GO DO IT
                ;
                ; EIN - EXECUTE IN#
                ;
                EIN             EQU          *
222e a5 44                      LDA          CNUM                      ; GET PORT
2230 4c 8b fe                   JMP          INPRT                     ; GO DO IT
                ;
                ; EMON - EXECUTE MONITOR CMD
                ;
                EMON            EQU          *
2233 ad 5e 2a                   LDA          MONMOD                    ; GET CURRENT BITS
2236 0d 74 2a                   ORA          IMBITS                    ; OR IN NEW BITS
2239 8d 5e 2a                   STA          MONMOD                    ; SET NEW MODE
223c 60                         RTS
                ;
                ; ENONON - EXECUTE NO MONITOR CMD
                ;
                ENOMON          EQU          *
223d 2c 74 2a                   BIT          IMBITS
2240 50 03                      BVC          ENM1
2242 20 c8 1f                   JSR          PRCRIF
                ENM1            EQU          *
2245 a9 70                      LDA          #$70
2247 4d 74 2a                   EOR          IMBITS                    ; INVERT INPUT BITS
224a 2d 5e 2a                   AND          MONMOD                    ; AND WITH CURRENT
224d 8d 5e 2a                   STA          MONMOD                    ; SET NEW MODE
2250 60                         RTS
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; EMAXF - EXECUTE MAX FILES
                ;
                EMAXF           EQU          *
2251 a9 00                      LDA          #0                        ; RESET EXECUTE
2253 8d b3 2a                   STA          ESTATE
2256 a5 44                      LDA          CNUM                      ; SAVE NEW NO FILES
2258 48                         PHA
2259 20 16 23                   JSR          CLALL                     ; GO CLOSE ALL FILES
225c 68                         PLA
225d 8d 57 2a                   STA          CNFTBS                    ; SET NEW NO FILE TBLS
2260 4c d4 27                   JMP          BLDFTB                    ; GO BUILD NEW ONES
                ;
                ; EDEL - DELETE A FILE
                ;
                EDEL            EQU          *
2263 a9 05                      LDA          #CRQDEL                   ; DELETE REQUEST
2265 20 aa 22                   JSR          OPEN                      ; GO OPEN
2268 20 64 27                   JSR          FILSRC                    ; FIND FILE
226b a0 00                      LDY          #0
226d 98                         TYA
226e 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y                ; RESET FN
2270 60                         RTS
                ;
                ; ELOCK - LOCK A FILE
                ;
                ELOCK           EQU          *
2271 a9 07                      LDA          #CRQLCK                   ; SET LOCK
2273 d0 02                      BNE          ELGO
                ;
                ; EUNLK - UNLOCK A FILE
                ;
                EUNLK           EQU          *
2275 a9 08                      LDA          #CRQUNL                   ; SET UNLOCK
                ELGO            EQU          *
2277 20 aa 22                   JSR          OPEN                      ; OPEN FILE & UNLOCK
227a 4c ea 22                   JMP          ECLOSE                    ; CLOSE IT
                ;
                ; EVAR - VERIFY A FILE
                ;
                EVAR            EQU          *
227d a9 0c                      LDA          #CRQVAR                   ; SET VARIFY
227f d0 f6                      BNE          ELGO
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; EREN - RENAME A FILE
                ;
                EREN            EQU          *
2281 ad 08 1d                   LDA          FN2ADR                    ; MOVE FILE NAME2
2284 8d bd 35                   STA          CCBFN2
2287 ad 09 1d                   LDA          FN2ADR+1
228a 8d be 35                   STA          CCBFN2+1
228d a9 09                      LDA          #CRQRNM
228f 8d 63 2a                   STA          TEMP1A                    ; SET RENAME
2292 20 c8 22                   JSR          EO3                       ; GO OPEN AND RENAME
2295 4c ea 22                   JMP          ECLOSE                    ; GO CLOSE
                ;
                ; EAPND - OPEN FILE FOR APPEND
                ;
                EAPND           EQU          *
2298 20 a3 22                   JSR          EOPEN                     ; GO OPEN
                AP1             EQU          *
229b 20 8c 26                   JSR          RBYTE                     ; READ A BYTE
229e d0 fb                      BNE          AP1                       ; BR IF NOT ZERO
                ;
22a0 4c 71 36                   JMP          BUMPER                    ; GO TO PATCH FOR APPEND FIX
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; EOPEN - OPEN A FILE
                ;
22a3 a9 00      EOPEN           LDA          #0                        ;FIX TYPE MISMATCH DETECTION
22a5 4c d5 23                   JMP          SV1                       ;(CALLS EOPN1)
22a8 a9 01      EOPN1           LDA          #CRQOPN
                OPEN            EQU          *
22aa 8d 63 2a                   STA          TEMP1A
22ad ad 6c 2a                   LDA          CL                        ; IF NO LENGTH ENTERED
22b0 d0 0a                      BNE          EO1                       ; THEN SET DEFAULT OF 1
22b2 ad 6d 2a                   LDA          CL+1
22b5 d0 05                      BNE          EO1
22b7 a9 01                      LDA          #1
22b9 8d 6c 2a                   STA          CL
                EO1             EQU          *
22bc ad 6c 2a                   LDA          CL                        ; MOVE REC LENGTH
22bf 8d bd 35                   STA          CCBRLN
22c2 ad 6d 2a                   LDA          CL+1
22c5 8d be 35                   STA          CCBRLN+1
                EO3             EQU          *
22c8 20 ea 22                   JSR          ECLOSE                    ; GO CLOSE IF OPEN
                EO4             EQU          *
22cb a5 45                      LDA          CNUM+1                    ; GET AVALL ENTRY
22cd d0 03                      BNE          EO5                       ; BR IF ONE AVAIL
22cf 4c c8 26                   JMP          ENFA                      ; DONE - NO FILES AVAIL
                EO5             EQU          *
22d2 85 41                      STA          ZPGWRK+1                  ; MOVE AVAIL SLOT TO ZPG
22d4 a5 44                      LDA          CNUM
22d6 85 40                      STA          ZPGWRK
                EO6             EQU          *
22d8 20 43 27                   JSR          MVFN1                     ; GO MOVE FILE NAME
22db 20 4e 27                   JSR          MVBUFP                    ; GO MOVE BUF PTRS
22de 20 1a 27                   JSR          OPNSUP                    ; GO SET UP OPEN
22e1 ad 63 2a                   LDA          TEMP1A                    ; SET OPEN REQ
22e4 8d bb 35                   STA          CCBREQ
22e7 4c a8 26                   JMP          DOSGO                     ; GO OPEN
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; ECLOSE - EXECUTE CLOSE FILE COMMAND
                ;
                ECLOSE          EQU          *
22ea ad 75 2a                   LDA          FNAME1
22ed c9 a0                      CMP          #$A0
22ef f0 25                      BEQ          CLALL
22f1 20 64 27                   JSR          FILSRC                    ; GO FIND FILE
22f4 b0 3a                      BCS          CL2                       ; BR IF NOT FOUND
22f6 20 fc 22                   JSR          CLOSE                     ; GO CLOSE
22f9 4c ea 22                   JMP          ECLOSE                    ; GO SEE IF ANY MORE OPEN
                ;
                ; CLOSE - CLOSE A FILE
                ;
                CLOSE           EQU          *
22fc 20 af 27                   JSR          TSTEXC
22ff d0 05                      BNE          CLX
2301 a9 00                      LDA          #0
2303 8d b3 2a                   STA          ESTATE
                CLX             EQU          *
2306 a0 00                      LDY          #0                        ; CLEAR 1ST FN
2308 98                         TYA                                    ; CHAR TO ZERO
2309 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y
230b 20 4e 27                   JSR          MVBUFP                    ; MOVE BUFFER PTRS
230e a9 02                      LDA          #CRQCLS                   ; SET CLOSE
2310 8d bb 35                   STA          CCBREQ
2313 4c a8 26                   JMP          DOSGO                     ; GO CLOSE
                ;
                ; CLALL - CLOSE ALL FILES
                ;
                CLALL           EQU          *
2316 20 92 27                   JSR          TSINIT                    ; GO INIT FILE SEARCH
2319 d0 05                      BNE          CL1
                CL0             EQU          *
231b 20 9a 27                   JSR          TSNXT                     ; NEXT ENTRY
231e f0 10                      BEQ          CL2                       ; BR IF NO MORE
                CL1             EQU          *
2320 20 af 27                   JSR          TSTEXC
2323 f0 f6                      BEQ          CL0
2325 20 aa 27                   JSR          TSTOPN                    ; GO TEST OPEN
2328 f0 f1                      BEQ          CL0                       ; BR NOT OPEN
232a 20 fc 22                   JSR          CLOSE                     ; GO CLOSE
232d 4c 16 23                   JMP          CLALL                     ; START OVER
2330 60         CL2             RTS                                    ; DONE

                ;
                ; EBSV - EXECUTE BINARY SAVE
                ;
                EBSV            EQU          *
2331 a9 09                      LDA          #ADR+L                    ; IF A&L
2333 2d 65 2a                   AND          INOPTS                    ; NOT GIVEN
2336 c9 09                      CMP          #ADR+L
2338 f0 03                      BEQ          EBSV1
233a 4c 00 20                   JMP          CNF                       ; THEN ERROR
                EBSV1           EQU          *
233d a9 04                      LDA          #4                        ; SET BINARY FILE
233f 20 d5 23                   JSR          SV1                       ; GO OPEN & TEST
2342 ad 73 2a                   LDA          CA+1                      ; OUTPUT ADR OF BLOCK
2345 ac 72 2a                   LDY          CA
2348 20 e0 23                   JSR          SV2
234b ad 6d 2a                   LDA          CL+1                      ; GO OPEN AND TEST
234e ac 6c 2a                   LDY          CL
2351 20 e0 23                   JSR          SV2                       ; OUTPUT LENGTH
2354 ad 73 2a                   LDA          CA+1                      ; GET ADR GIVEN
2357 ac 72 2a                   LDY          CA
235a 4c ff 23                   JMP          SV3                       ; OUTPUT BLOCK
                ;
                ; EBLD - EXECUTE BINARY LOAD
                ;
                EBLD            EQU          *
235d 20 a8 22                   JSR          EOPN1                     ;(CHANGED 11/1/78 FOR TYPE MISMATCH)
                EBLD2           EQU          *
2360 a9 7f                      LDA          #$7F
2362 2d c2 35                   AND          CCBFUC
2365 c9 04                      CMP          #4
2367 f0 03                      BEQ          EBLD3
2369 4c d0 26                   JMP          ETYP                      ;TYPE MISMATCH ERROR MESSAGE
                EBLD3           EQU          *
236c a9 04                      LDA          #4                        ; SET BINARY FILE
236e 20 d5 23                   JSR          SV1                       ; GO OPEN & TEST
2371 20 7a 24                   JSR          LD2                       ; GO GET ADR
2374 aa                         TAX
2375 ad 65 2a                   LDA          INOPTS
2378 29 01                      AND          #ADR                      ; IF ADR NOT GIVEN
237a d0 06                      BNE          EBLD1
237c 8e 72 2a                   STX          CA                        ; THEN USE ADR FROM FILE
237f 8c 73 2a                   STY          CA+1
                EBLD1           EQU          *
2382 20 7a 24                   JSR          LD2                       ; GET LENGTH
2385 ae 72 2a                   LDX          CA                        ; GET GIVEN ADR
2388 ac 73 2a                   LDY          CA+1
238b 4c 71 24                   JMP          LD3                       ; GO GET BLOCK
                ;
                ; EBRUN - EXECUTE BINARY RUN
                ;
238e 20 5d 23   EBRUN           JSR          EBLD                      ;DO A BINARY LOAD
2391 20 51 28                   JSR          MVCSW                     ; GO RESTORE CHAR I/O SW
2394 6c 72 2a                   JMP          (CA)                      ; GO EXEC THE STUFF
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; ESAVE - EXECUTE SAVE REQUEST
                ;
                ESAVE           EQU          *
2397 ad b6 2a                   LDA          ASIBSW                    ; IF IB THEN
239a f0 20                      BEQ          EIBSV                     ; GO TO IB SAVE
239c a5 d6                      LDA          ASRNX                     ;CANNOT DO AS SAVE WHEN RUN-ONLY PROG.
239e 10 03                      BPL          EASAV                     ;BRANCH IF OK TO SAVE, OTHERWISE
23a0 4c cc 26                   JMP          MFERR                     ;PRINT "PROGRAM TOO LARGE", THAT OUGHT TO GET 'EM.
23a3 a9 02      EASAV           LDA          #2                        ; GET APPLESOFT PGM
23a5 20 d5 23                   JSR          SV1                       ; GO OPEN AND TEST
                ;
23a8 38                         SEC                                    ; BLOCK LENGTH
23a9 a5 af                      LDA          ASEOP                     ; =EOP-SOP
23ab e5 67                      SBC          ASSOP
23ad a8                         TAY
23ae a5 b0                      LDA          ASEOP+1
23b0 e5 68                      SBC          ASSOP+1
23b2 20 e0 23                   JSR          SV2                       ; GO OUTPUT LENGTH
                ;
23b5 a5 68                      LDA          ASSOP+1                   ; BLOCK ADR
23b7 a4 67                      LDY          ASSOP                     ; =SOP
23b9 4c ff 23                   JMP          SV3                       ; GO OUTPUT BLOCK
                ;
                EIBSV           EQU          *
23bc a9 01                      LDA          #1                        ; SET IB PGM
23be 20 d5 23                   JSR          SV1                       ; GO OPEN AND TEST
                ;
23c1 38                         SEC                                    ; BLOCK LENGTH
23c2 a5 4c                      LDA          IBHMEM                    ; =HIMEM-SOP
23c4 e5 ca                      SBC          IBSOP
23c6 a8                         TAY
23c7 a5 4d                      LDA          IBHMEM+1
23c9 e5 cb                      SBC          IBSOP+1
23cb 20 e0 23                   JSR          SV2                       ; GO OUTPUT LENGTH
                ;
23ce a5 cb                      LDA          IBSOP+1                   ; BLOCK ADR
23d0 a4 ca                      LDY          IBSOP                     ; =SOP
23d2 4c ff 23                   JMP          SV3                       ; GO OUTPUT BLOCK
                ;
                SV1             EQU          *
                SV1A            EQU          *
23d5 8d c2 35                   STA          CCBFUC                    ; SET PGM TYPE
23d8 48                         PHA                                    ; SAVE PGM TYPE
23d9 20 a8 22                   JSR          EOPN1                     ; GO OPEN FILE  (CHGED 11/1/78)
23dc 68                         PLA                                    ; GET SAVE TYPE
23dd 4c c4 27                   JMP          TSTFUC                    ; GO CHECK
                ;
                SV2             EQU          *
23e0 8c c1 35                   STY          CCBBLN                    ; SET BLOCK LENGTH
23e3 8c c3 35                   STY          CCBDAT                    ; AND DATA BYTE
23e6 8d c2 35                   STA          CCBBLN+1

23eb 8d bb 35                   STA          CCBREQ
23ee a9 01                      LDA          #CRMNBT                   ; NEXT BYTE
23f0 8d bc 35                   STA          CCBRQM
23f3 20 a8 26                   JSR          DOSGO                     ; GO WRITE
23f6 ad c2 35                   LDA          CCBBLN+1                  ; OTHER BYTE TOO
23f9 8d c3 35                   STA          CCBDAT
23fc 4c a8 26                   JMP          DOSGO

23ff 8c c3 35   SV3             STY          CCBBBA                    ; SET BLOCK ADR
2402 8d c4 35                   STA          CCBBBA+1
2405 a9 02                      LDA          #CRMNBL                   ; INDICATE BLOCK I/O
2407 4c 86 36                   JMP          VPATCH                    ;VERIFY AFTER SAVE
240a 20 a8 26   GODOS           JSR          DOSGO                     ; GO DO IT
240d 4c ea 22                   JMP          ECLOSE                    ; CLOSE FILE
                ;;;                PAGE
2410 4c d0 26   NBPER           JMP          ERNU1
                ;
                ; ELOAD - EXECUTE LOAD REQUEST
                ;
                ELOAD           EQU          *
2413 20 16 23                   JSR          CLALL                     ; GO CLOSE ALL
2416 20 a8 22   ELOAD0          JSR          EOPN1                     ; OPEN FILE (CHGED 11/1/78)
                ;
                ELD1            EQU          *
2419 a9 23                      LDA          #$23                      ; STRIP UNRELATED STUFF
241b 2d c2 35                   AND          CCBFUC                    ; OUT OF FUC
241e f0 f0                      BEQ          NBPER                     ; BR IF ERROR
                ; ISOLOLATE IB & AS
                ELD2            EQU          *
2420 8d c2 35                   STA          CCBFUC                    ; SAVE IB/AS ONLY
2423 ad b6 2a                   LDA          ASIBSW                    ; IF IB THEN
2426 f0 28                      BEQ          EIBL                      ; GO TO IB LOAD
2428 a9 02                      LDA          #2
242a 20 b1 24                   JSR          LD1                       ; GO OPEN AND TEST
                ;
242d 20 7a 24                   JSR          LD2                       ; GO GET BLOCK LENGTH
                ;
2430 18                         CLC
2431 65 67                      ADC          ASSOP                     ; ADD BLOCK LENGTH TO SOP
2433 aa                         TAX
2434 98                         TYA
2435 65 68                      ADC          ASSOP+1
                ;
2437 c5 74                      CMP          ASHM1+1                   ; IF BL+SOP >= HMEM
2439 b0 70                      BCS          MFULL                     ; THEN WON'T FIT
                ;
                EASL1           EQU          *
243b 85 b0                      STA          ASEOP+1                   ; SET NEW EOP ADR
243d 85 6a                      STA          ASEOP2+1
243f 86 af                      STX          ASEOP
2441 86 69                      STX          ASEOP2
2443 a6 67                      LDX          ASSOP                     ; GET ADR WHERE TO LOAD
2445 a4 68                      LDY          ASSOP+1
2447 20 71 24                   JSR          LD3                       ; GO LOAD
244a 20 51 28                   JSR          MVCSW                     ;RESTORE I/O
244d 6c 60 1d                   JMP          (ASEQ)                    ;RELOC FOR THIS VERSION OF APPLSOFT
                ;
                EIBL            EQU          *
2450 a9 01                      LDA          #1                        ; SET IB PGM
2452 20 b1 24                   JSR          LD1                       ; GO OPEN AND TEST
                ;
2455 20 7a 24                   JSR          LD2                       ; GO GET BLOCK LENGTH
                ;
2458 38                         SEC                                    ; HMEM - BLOCK LENGTH
2459 a5 4c                      LDA          IBHMEM                    ; IS NEW SOP
245b ed 60 2a                   SBC          SVBL
245e aa                         TAX
245f a5 4d                      LDA          IBHMEM+1
2461 ed 61 2a                   SBC          SVBL+1
2464 90 45                      BCC          MFULL
2466 a8                         TAY
                ;
2467 c4 4b                      CPY          IBLMEM+1                  ; IF NEW SOP <= LMEM
2469 90 40                      BCC          MFULL
246b f0 3e                      BEQ          MFULL
246d 84 cb                      STY          IBSOP+1                   ; SET NEW SOP
246f 86 ca                      STX          IBSOP
                LD3             EQU          *
2471 8e c3 35                   STX          CCBBBA                    ; SET BLOCK ADR
2474 8c c4 35                   STY          CCBBBA+1
2477 4c 0a 24                   JMP          GODOS                     ; GET BLOCK & CLOSE
                ;
                LD2             EQU          *
247a ad 0a 1d                   LDA          SVBLA                     ; MOVE ADR OF WHERE
247d 8d c3 35                   STA          CCBBBA                    ; TO PUT DATA TO
2480 ad 0b 1d                   LDA          SVBLA+1                   ; CCBN
2483 8d c4 35                   STA          CCBBBA+1
2486 a9 00                      LDA          #0
2488 8d c2 35                   STA          CCBBLN+1                  ; READ INTO
248b a9 02                      LDA          #2
248d 8d c1 35                   STA          CCBBLN
2490 a9 03                      LDA          #CRQRD                    ; READ
2492 8d bb 35                   STA          CCBREQ
2495 a9 02                      LDA          #CRMNBL                   ; BLOCK
2497 8d bc 35                   STA          CCBRQM
249a 20 a8 26                   JSR          DOSGO
249d ad 61 2a                   LDA          SVBL+1
24a0 8d c2 35                   STA          CCBBLN+1
24a3 a8                         TAY
24a4 ad 60 2a                   LDA          SVBL
24a7 8d c1 35                   STA          CCBBLN
24aa 60                         RTS
                ;
                MFULL           EQU          *
24ab 20 ea 22                   JSR          ECLOSE                    ; GO CLOSE FILE
24ae 4c cc 26                   JMP          MFERR                     ; AND GIVE ERR MSG
                LD1             EQU          *
24b1 cd c2 35                   CMP          CCBFUC                    ; TEST TYPE
24b4 f0 1a                      BEQ          LD1C                      ; BR IF MATCH
24b6 ae 5f 2a                   LDX          CMDNO
24b9 8e 62 2a                   STX          SVCMD
24bc 4a                         LSR          A
24bd f0 03                      BEQ          LD1A                      ; BR IF PGM IS AS
24bf 4c 9e 25                   JMP          EINT                      ; GO FOR INTG BASIC
                ;
                LD1A            EQU          *
24c2 a2 1d                      LDX          #29                       ; SAVE FILE NAME
24c4 bd 75 2a   LD1B            LDA          FNAME1,X                  ; INCASE IS RAM APPLESOFT
24c7 9d 93 2a                   STA          FNAME2,X
24ca ca                         DEX
24cb 10 f7                      BPL          LD1B
24cd 4c 7a 25                   JMP          EAS                       ; GO FOR AS
                ;
24d0 60         LD1C            RTS
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; ERUN - EXECUTE RUN REQUEST
                ;
                ERUN            EQU          *
24d1 ad b6 2a                   LDA          ASIBSW                    ;IF APPLESOFT THEN RELOC FLAG SET
24d4 f0 03                      BEQ          ERUN0
24d6 8d b7 2a                   STA          RSTATE                    ;INDICATE APSFT RUN
24d9 20 13 24   ERUN0           JSR          ELOAD                     ; LOAD PGM
24dc 20 c8 1f   ERUN1           JSR          PRCRIF                    ;REENTRY POINT FOR ASFT RELOC
24df 20 51 28                   JSR          MVCSW                     ; GO RESTORE CHAR I/O SW
24e2 6c 58 1d                   JMP          (RUN)
                ;
                ; IBRUN - INT BASIC RUN
                ;
                IBRUN           EQU          *
24e5 a5 4a                      LDA          IBLMEM                    ; RESET START OF VARS
24e7 85 cc                      STA          IBSOV
24e9 a5 4b                      LDA          IBLMEM+1
24eb 85 cd                      STA          IBSOV+1
24ed 6c 56 1d                   JMP          (CHAIN)
                ;
                ; EHCAIN - EXECUTE CHAIN REQUEST
                ;
                ECHAIN          EQU          *
24f0 20 16 24                   JSR          ELOAD0                    ; LOAD PGM WITHOUT CLOSING READ FILES
24f3 20 c8 1f                   JSR          PRCRIF
24f6 20 51 28                   JSR          MVCSW                     ; GO RESTORE CHAR I/O SW
24f9 6c 56 1d                   JMP          (CHAIN)
24fc 20 65 d6   ASRUN1          JSR          $D665                     ; ROM
24ff 85 33                      STA          PROMPT                    ;INSURES APPLESOFT RUN DETECT (A=0)
2501 85 d8                      STA          ASONERR                   ;RESET APPLESOFT ONERR FLAG
2503 4c d2 d7                   JMP          $D7D2
2506 20 65 0e   ASRUN2          JSR          $E65                      ; RAM
2509 85 33                      STA          PROMPT                    ;INSURES APPLESOFT RUN DETECT (A=0)
250b 85 d8                      STA          ASONERR                   ;RESET APPLESOFT ONERR FLAG
250d 4c d4 0f                   JMP          $FD4

                ; #   END OF FILE:  XLODSAV
