                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; EWRITE - WRITE CMD EXECUTE
                ;
                EWRITE          EQU          *
2510 20 26 25                   JSR          RWPOSN                    ; GO POSITION FILE IF REQD
2513 a9 05                      LDA          #5
2515 8d 52 2a                   STA          OSTATE                    ; SET OSTATE=5
2518 4c 83 1f                   JMP          CERTN                     ; DONE
                ;
                ; EREAD - READ COMD EXECUTE
                ;
                EREAD           EQU          *
251b 20 26 25                   JSR          RWPOSN                    ; GO POSITION FILE IF REQD
251e a9 01                      LDA          #1
2520 8d 51 2a                   STA          ISTATE                    ; SET I STATE = DISK INPUT
2523 4c 83 1f                   JMP          CERTN                     ; DONE
                ;
                ; RWPOSN - POSTION FOR READ/ WRITE
                ;
                RWPOSN          EQU          *
2526 20 64 27                   JSR          FILSRC                    ; FIND THE FILE
2529 90 06                      BCC          RWP1                      ; BR IF FILE FOUND
252b 20 a3 22                   JSR          EOPEN                     ; GO OPEN FOR KLUTZ
252e 4c 34 25                   JMP          RWP2                      ; THEN SKIP NEXT LINE
                RWP1            EQU          *
2531 20 4e 27                   JSR          MVBUFP                    ; MOVE BUFF POINTERS
                RWP2            EQU          *
2534 ad 65 2a                   LDA          INOPTS                    ; GET IN OPTIONS
2537 29 06                      AND          #R+B                      ; WAS IT B OR R
2539 f0 13                      BEQ          RWPR                      ; BR IF NOT
253b a2 03                      LDX          #3
253d bd 6e 2a   RWP2A           LDA          CR,X                      ; MOVE REL REC
2540 9d bd 35                   STA          CCBRRN,X                  ; AND REL BYTE
2543 ca                         DEX
2544 10 f7                      BPL          RWP2A
                RWP3            EQU          *
2546 a9 0a                      LDA          #CRQPOS                   ; INDICATE POISTION REQUEST
2548 8d bb 35                   STA          CCBREQ
254b 20 a8 26                   JSR          DOSGO
254e 60         RWPR            RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;
                ; EINIT - EXECUTE INIT COMMAND
                ;
                EINIT           EQU          *
254f a9 40                      LDA          #V                        ; MUST HAVE
2551 2d 65 2a                   AND          INOPTS                    ; VOL OPTION
2554 f0 05                      BEQ          DFVOL                     ;GO SET DEFAULT VOLUME=254
2556 ad 66 2a                   LDA          CV                        ;CAN'T SPECIFY VOL=0
2559 d0 05                      BNE          EINITA
255b a9 fe      DFVOL           LDA          #$FE                      ;SET DEFAULT VOLUME NUMBER.
255d 8d 66 2a                   STA          CV
2560 ad 0d 1d   EINITA          LDA          ASTART+1
2563 8d bc 35                   STA          CCBBSA
2566 a9 0b                      LDA          #CRQFMT
2568 20 aa 22                   JSR          OPEN
256b 4c 97 23                   JMP          ESAVE
                ;
                ;
                ; ECAT - PRINT CATALOG
                ;
                ECAT            EQU          *
256e a9 06                      LDA          #CRQDIR
2570 20 aa 22                   JSR          OPEN                      ; GO PRETEND OPEN
2573 ad bf 35                   LDA          CCBVOL
2576 8d 66 2a                   STA          CV
2579 60                         RTS
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; EAS - EXECUTE APPLESOFT REQUEST
                ;
                EAS             EQU          *
257a a9 4c                      LDA          #ATSTV                    ; GET APPLESOFT TEST VALUE
257c 20 b2 25                   JSR          SWTST                     ; GO SWITCH AND TEST
257f f0 2e                      BEQ          GOINIT                    ; BR IF APPLESOFT
2581 a9 00                      LDA          #0
2583 8d b6 2a                   STA          ASIBSW
                ;
                EAS0            EQU          *
2586 a0 1e                      LDY          #30
2588 20 97 20                   JSR          CLRFNA
258b a2 09                      LDX          #FASBL
258d bd b7 2a   EAS1            LDA          FASB-1,X                  ; MOVE SYSTEM FILE NAME
2590 9d 74 2a                   STA          FNAME1-1,X
2593 ca                         DEX
2594 d0 f7                      BNE          EAS1
                ;
                EAS2            EQU          *
2596 a9 c0                      LDA          #$C0
2598 8d 51 2a                   STA          ISTATE                    ; FOR RAM APPLESOFT
259b 4c d1 24                   JMP          ERUN                      ; GO LOAD AND RUN
                ;
                ; EINT - EXECUTE INTEGER REQUEST
                ;
                EINT            EQU          *
259e a9 20                      LDA          #ITSTV                    ; GET IB TEST VALUE
25a0 20 b2 25                   JSR          SWTST                     ; GO SWITCH AND TEST
25a3 f0 05                      BEQ          GOINT                     ;BR IF INTIGER BASIC...
25a5 a9 01                      LDA          #1                        ;LANGUAGE NOT AVIALABLE, TOO BAD...
25a7 4c d2 26                   JMP          ERROR
25aa a9 00      GOINT           LDA          #0                        ;RESET RSTATE
25ac 8d b7 2a                   STA          RSTATE                    ; FOR NON APPLESOFT PROG.
                GOINIT          EQU          *
25af 4c 84 1d                   JMP          DBINIT                    ; GO INIT DOS
                SWTST           EQU          *
25b2 cd 00 e0                   CMP          AITSTL                    ; TEST CURRENT VALUE
25b5 f0 0e                      BEQ          SWTR
25b7 8d 80 c0                   STA          $C080                     ; TRY SWITCH 1
25ba cd 00 e0                   CMP          AITSTL                    ; TEST AGAIN
25bd f0 06                      BEQ          SWTR                      ; BR IF NOW SAME
25bf 8d 81 c0                   STA          $C081                     ; TRY SWITCH 2
25c2 cd 00 e0                   CMP          AITSTL                    ; TEST AND
25c5 60         SWTR            RTS                                    ; RETURN
                ;
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; EEXEC - EXECUTE EXEC CMD
                ;
                EEXEC           EQU          *
25c6 20 a3 22                   JSR          EOPEN                     ; OPEN FILE
25c9 ad 4f 2a                   LDA          CFTABA                    ; MOVE TABLE POINTERS
25cc 8d b4 2a                   STA          EFTABA
25cf ad 50 2a                   LDA          CFTABA+1
25d2 8d b5 2a                   STA          EFTABA+1
25d5 ad 75 2a                   LDA          FNAME1                    ; USE FILNAME
25d8 8d b3 2a                   STA          ESTATE                    ; SET EX STATE NON ZERO
25db d0 0e                      BNE          EXP2
                ;
                ;
                ; EPOS - EXECUTE POSITION
                ;
                EPOS            EQU          *
25dd 20 64 27                   JSR          FILSRC
25e0 90 06                      BCC          EXP1
25e2 20 a3 22                   JSR          EOPEN
25e5 4c eb 25                   JMP          EXP2
25e8 20 4e 27   EXP1            JSR          MVBUFP
                EXP2            EQU          *
25eb ad 65 2a                   LDA          INOPTS                    ; GET OPTIONS
25ee 29 04                      AND          #R                        ; TEST R
25f0 f0 1b                      BEQ          EX2                       ; BR NOT R
                ;
25f2 ad 6e 2a   EX0             LDA          CR                        ; IF CR NOT ZERO
25f5 d0 08                      BNE          EX1A                      ; THEN DECREMENT
25f7 ae 6f 2a                   LDX          CR+1
25fa f0 11                      BEQ          EX2
25fc ce 6f 2a                   DEC          CR+1
25ff ce 6e 2a   EX1A            DEC          CR
2602 20 8c 26   EX1             JSR          RBYTE                     ; AND READ A RCORD
2605 f0 38                      BEQ          ICFD4
2607 c9 8d                      CMP          #$8D                      ; UNTIL CR
2609 d0 f7                      BNE          EX1
260b f0 e5                      BEQ          EX0                       ; THEN TEST CR AGAIN
                ;
260d 60         EX2             RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; OCTD - OUTPUT A CHAR TO DISK
                ;
                OCTD            EQU          *
260e 20 5e 26                   JSR          TSTRUN                    ; GO TEST RUN
2611 b0 66                      BCS          ICFDB                     ;BRANCH IF NOT RUN MODE
2613 ad 5c 2a                   LDA          SVA                       ; CHAR IN SAVED ACU
2616 8d c3 35                   STA          CCBDAT                    ; PUT INTO CCBDATA AREA
2619 a9 04                      LDA          #CRQWR                    ; SET WRITE
261b 8d bb 35                   STA          CCBREQ
261e a9 01                      LDA          #CRMNBT                   ; SET NEXT BYTE
2620 8d bc 35                   STA          CCBRQM
2623 4c a8 26                   JMP          DOSGO                     ; GO WRITE BYTE
                ;
                ; INCFD - INPUT A CHAR FROM DISK
                ;
                ICFD            EQU          *
2626 20 5e 26                   JSR          TSTRUN                    ; GO TEST RUN
2629 b0 4e                      BCS          ICFDB                     ;BRANCH IF NOT RUN MODE
262b a9 06                      LDA          #6                        ; SET OUT STE = 6
                ICFD3           EQU          *
262d 8d 52 2a                   STA          OSTATE                    ; TO CATCH ECHO
2630 20 8c 26                   JSR          RBYTE
2633 d0 0f                      BNE          ICFD1                     ; BR IF NOT ZERO CHAR
                ICFD2           EQU          *
2635 20 fc 22                   JSR          CLOSE
2638 a9 03                      LDA          #3
263a cd 52 2a                   CMP          OSTATE
263d f0 ce                      BEQ          EX2
                ICFD4           EQU          *
263f a9 05                      LDA          #CREEOF
2641 4c d2 26                   JMP          ERROR                     ; GO TO ERROR
                ICFD1           EQU          *
2644 c9 e0                      CMP          #$E0                      ;CHECK FOR LOWER CASE
2646 90 02                      BCC          ICFNLC                    ;BRANCH IF NOT LOWER-CASE
2648 29 7f                      AND          #$7F                      ;STRIP HI BIT TO FOOL GETLINE
                ICFNLC          EQU          *
264a 8d 5c 2a                   STA          SVA                       ; PUT INTO SAVED ACU
264d ae 5a 2a                   LDX          SVX                       ; MUST CHECK LAST FOR LOWER CASE
2650 f0 09                      BEQ          ICFD0                     ;IGNORE IF FIRST CHAR.
2652 ca                         DEX
2653 bd 00 02                   LDA          LBUFF,X
2656 09 80                      ORA          #$80                      ;RESET HI BIT
2658 9d 00 02                   STA          LBUFF,X                   ; EVEN THOUGH IT MAY NOT NEED IT
                ICFD0           EQU          *
265b 4c b3 1f                   JMP          ORTN                      ; GO RESTORE REGS AND RTS
                ;
265e 48         TSTRUN          PHA
265f ad b6 2a                   LDA          ASIBSW                    ; GET AS/INT BASIC SWITCH
2662 f0 0e                      BEQ          TR1                       ; BR IF INT
2664 a6 76                      LDX          $76                       ;CHECK APPLESOFT RUN FLAG
2666 e8                         INX                                    ;(NOT RUN=0 AFTER INCREMENT)
2667 f0 0d                      BEQ          NOTRUN                    ;IF SAYS RUNNING MAKE SURE WITH PROMPT.
2669 a6 33                      LDX          PROMPT                    ;TEST APPLESOFT RUNNING.
266b e0 dd                      CPX          #']'+$80
266d f0 07                      BEQ          NOTRUN                    ; BR IF NOT RUN
266f 68         TR0             PLA
2670 18                         CLC                                    ;INDICATE PROGRAM RUNNING
2671 60                         RTS
                TR1             EQU          *
2672 a5 d9                      LDA          $D9                       ; GET INT RUN FLAG
2674 30 f9                      BMI          TR0                       ; BR IF RUN
2676 68         NOTRUN          PLA                                    ;INDICATE PROGRAM NOT RUNNING
2677 38                         SEC                                    ; WITH CARRY SET.
2678 60                         RTS
                ;
                ICFDB           EQU          *                         ; NOT RUN MODE
2679 20 fc 22                   JSR          CLOSE                     ; GO CLOSE FILE
267c 20 5b 27                   JSR          CLRSTS                    ; GO CLEAR STATES
267f 4c b3 1f                   JMP          ORTN
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; NXTEXC - NEXT EXECUTE CHAR
                ;
                NXTEXC          EQU          *
2682 20 9d 26                   JSR          MVEFTA
2685 20 4e 27                   JSR          MVBUFP                    ; GO MOVE PTRS
2688 a9 03                      LDA          #3
268a d0 a1                      BNE          ICFD3
                ;
                ; RBYTE - READ NEXT BYTE
                ;
                RBYTE           EQU          *
268c a9 03                      LDA          #CRQRD                    ; SET READ
268e 8d bb 35                   STA          CCBREQ
2691 a9 01                      LDA          #CRMNBT                   ; SET NEXT BYTE
2693 8d bc 35                   STA          CCBRQM
2696 20 a8 26                   JSR          DOSGO                     ; GO TO DOS
2699 ad c3 35                   LDA          CCBDAT                    ; GET THE DATA BYTE
269c 60                         RTS
                MVEFTA          EQU          *
269d ad b5 2a                   LDA          EFTABA+1                  ; MOVE TABLE ADR
26a0 85 41                      STA          ZPGWRK+1                  ; NO ZPG
26a2 ad b4 2a                   LDA          EFTABA
26a5 85 40                      STA          ZPGWRK
26a7 60                         RTS

                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; DOSGO - GOTO DOS
                ;
                DOSGO           EQU          *
26a8 20 06 2b                   JSR          DOSENT                    ; GO TO DOS
26ab 90 16                      BCC          DG3                       ; BR IF NOT ERROR
                ;
26ad ad c5 35                   LDA          CCBSTA                    ;GET RETURN CODE
26b0 c9 05                      CMP          #5
26b2 f0 03                      BEQ          YESEOF
26b4 4c 5e 36                   JMP          CLOSFILE                  ;NO. CLOSE & COMPLAIN
26b7 4c 92 36   YESEOF          JMP          EOFFIX                    ;MABYE FIX IT UP?
26ba ea                         NOP
                ***************************
                *
                * DOS 3.3  (REV B) PATCH
                *
                ***************************
                ;;;                DO           DOS33B
26bb 20 69 3a   DOSGO2A         JSR          MOVEOF                    ; MOVE END OF FILE PATCH
                ;;;                ELSE
                ;;;                NOP
                ;;;DOSGO2A         NOP
                ;;;                NOP
                ;;;                FIN
26be a2 00                      LDX          #0                        ; SET OTHER EIF
26c0 8e c3 35                   STX          CCBDAT                    ; DONE
26c3 60         DG3             RTS
                ;
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; ERROR ROUTINE
                ;
26c4 a9 0b      ESYNTX          LDA          #CREFLK+1
26c6 d0 0a                      BNE          ERROR
26c8 a9 0c      ENFA            LDA          #CREFLK+2
26ca d0 06                      BNE          ERROR
26cc a9 0e      MFERR           LDA          #CREFLK+4
26ce d0 02                      BNE          ERROR
                ETYP            EQU          *
26d0 a9 0d      ERNU1           LDA          #CREFLK+3
                ;
                ERROR           EQU          *
26d2 8d 5c 2a                   STA          SVA                       ; SAVE MSG NUMBER
26d5 20 e6 3f                   JSR          CLRSTS1                   ;PATCH TO CLR RSTATE TOO (WAS JSR CLRSTS)
26d8 ad b6 2a                   LDA          ASIBSW                    ; GET AS/IN BASIC SWITCH
26db f0 04                      BEQ          ERNAS                     ; BR IF NOT APPLESOFT
26dd a5 d8                      LDA          ASONERR                   ;GET AS ERR FLAG
26df 30 0e                      BMI          ERRTN                     ; BRT IF ON ERR IS GO
                ERNAS           EQU          *
26e1 a2 00                      LDX          #0
26e3 20 02 27                   JSR          EMPR                      ; GO OUTPUT
26e6 ae 5c 2a                   LDX          SVA                       ; GET SAVE MSG
26e9 20 02 27                   JSR          EMPR                      ; GO OUTPUT MSG
26ec 20 c8 1f                   JSR          PRCRIF                    ;OUTPUT A CARRAGE RETURN AFTER MESSAGE
26ef 20 51 28   ERRTN           JSR          MVCSW                     ; GO MOVE CHAR I/ SW
26f2 20 5e 26                   JSR          TSTRUN
26f5 ae 5c 2a                   LDX          SVA
26f8 a9 03                      LDA          #03
26fa b0 03                      BCS          ERRTN1                    ;DON'T GOTO BREAK HANDLER IF NOT RUNNING
26fc 6c 5a 1d                   JMP          (BREAK)
26ff 6c 5e 1d   ERRTN1          JMP          (CONT)                    ;REENTER CONT IF NOT RUN
                ;
                EMPR            EQU          *
2702 bd 3f 2a                   LDA          EMDTB,X                   ; GET ITS DISPL
2705 aa                         TAX                                    ; INTO X
                EMPR1           EQU          *
2706 8e 63 2a                   STX          TEMP1A                    ; SAVE DISPL
2709 bd 71 29                   LDA          EMSG,X                    ; GET MSG CHAR
270c 48                         PHA                                    ; SAVE CHAR
270d 09 80                      ORA          #$80                      ; SET MSB ON
270f 20 c5 1f                   JSR          ORTN1                     ; OUTPUT CHAR
2712 ae 63 2a                   LDX          TEMP1A                    ; GET INDEX
2715 e8                         INX                                    ; INCREMENT IT
2716 68                         PLA                                    ; RE-LOAD CHAR
2717 10 ed                      BPL          EMPR1                     ; BR IF MORE CHARS
2719 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; OPNSUP - OPEN SET UP
                ;
                OPNSUP          EQU          *
271a ad 66 2a                   LDA          CV                        ; VOLUME
271d 8d bf 35                   STA          CCBVOL
2720 ad 68 2a                   LDA          CD                        ; DRIVE
2723 8d c0 35                   STA          CCBDRV
2726 ad 6a 2a                   LDA          CS                        ; SLOT
2729 8d c1 35                   STA          CCBSLT
272c ad 06 1d                   LDA          FN1ADR                    ; FILENAME 1 ADR
272f 8d c3 35                   STA          CCBFN1
2732 ad 07 1d                   LDA          FN1ADR+1
2735 8d c4 35                   STA          CCBFN1+1
2738 a5 40                      LDA          ZPGWRK
273a 8d 4f 2a                   STA          CFTABA
273d a5 41                      LDA          ZPGWRK+1
273f 8d 50 2a                   STA          CFTABA+1
2742 60                         RTS
                ;
                ; MVFN1 - MOVE FILE NAME 1 TO FILE PTR
                ;
                MVFN1           EQU          *
2743 a0 1d                      LDY          #29
2745 b9 75 2a   MVFN1A          LDA          FNAME1,Y
2748 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y
274a 88                         DEY
274b 10 f8                      BPL          MVFN1A
274d 60                         RTS
                ;
                ; MVBUFP - MOVE BUFFER PTRS TO CCB
                ;
                MVBUFP          EQU          *
274e a0 1e                      LDY          #30
2750 b1 40      MVBP1           LDA          (ZPGWRK),Y
2752 99 a9 35                   STA          CCBFCB-30,Y
2755 c8                         INY
2756 c0 26                      CPY          #38
2758 d0 f6                      BNE          MVBP1
275a 60                         RTS
                ;
                ; CLRSTS - CLEAR STATES
                ;
                CLRSTS          EQU          *
275b a0 00                      LDY          #0
275d 8c 51 2a                   STY          ISTATE
2760 8c 52 2a                   STY          OSTATE
2763 60                         RTS
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; FILSRC - SEARCH FOR FILE NAME1
                ;
                FILSRC          EQU          *
2764 a9 00                      LDA          #0                        ; CLEAR SV AVAIL
2766 85 45                      STA          CNUM+1
                ;
2768 20 92 27                   JSR          TSINIT                    ; GO INIT SEARCH
276b 4c 73 27                   JMP          FLS1A
276e 20 9a 27   FLS1            JSR          TSNXT                     ; LOOK AT NEXT
2771 f0 1d                      BEQ          FLS4                      ; BR IF NO NEXT
                ;
2773 20 aa 27   FLS1A           JSR          TSTOPN                    ; GO TEST OPEN
2776 d0 0a                      BNE          FLS2                      ; BR IF OPEN
                ;
2778 a5 40                      LDA          ZPGWRK                    ; SAVE AVAIL ENTRY ADR
277a 85 44                      STA          CNUM
277c a5 41                      LDA          ZPGWRK+1
277e 85 45                      STA          CNUM+1
2780 d0 ec                      BNE          FLS1                      ; GO LOOK SOME MORE
                ;
2782 a0 1d      FLS2            LDY          #29                       ; FILE HAD 30 CHARS
2784 b1 40      FLS3            LDA          (ZPGWRK),Y                ; GET CHAR
2786 d9 75 2a                   CMP          FNAME1,Y                  ; TEST CHAR
2789 d0 e3                      BNE          FLS1                      ; BR NOT
278b 88                         DEY
278c 10 f6                      BPL          FLS3                      ; LOOK AT 30 CHARS
278e 18                         CLC                                    ; FOUND
278f 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;
2790 38         FLS4            SEC                                    ; NOT FOUND
2791 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; TSINIT - INITIALIZE FOR FTAB SEARCH
                ; TSNXT - GET NEXT FTAB ENTRY
                ;
                TSINIT          EQU          *
2792 ad 00 1d                   LDA          FTAB                      ; GET 1ST PTR ADR
2795 ae 01 1d                   LDX          FTAB+1
2798 d0 0a                      BNE          TSST
                TSNXT           EQU          *
279a a0 25                      LDY          #37                       ; GET LINK
279c b1 40                      LDA          (ZPGWRK),Y
279e f0 09                      BEQ          TSR                       ; BR IF NO LINK
                ;
27a0 aa                         TAX
27a1 88                         DEY
27a2 b1 40                      LDA          (ZPGWRK),Y
                TSST            EQU          *
27a4 86 41                      STX          ZPGWRK+1
27a6 85 40                      STA          ZPGWRK
27a8 8a                         TXA                                    ; SET NE CC
27a9 60         TSR             RTS                                    ; RTN
                ;
                ; TSTOPN - TST FOR OPEN FILE
                ;
                TSTOPN          EQU          *
27aa a0 00                      LDY          #0                        ; GET 1ST CHAR OF FN
27ac b1 40                      LDA          (ZPGWRK),Y
27ae 60                         RTS
                ;
                ; TSTEXC - TEST CURRENT FILE FOR EXECUTE
                ;
                TSTEXC          EQU          *
27af ad b3 2a                   LDA          ESTATE                    ; IF ESTATE = 0
27b2 f0 0e                      BEQ          TXC1                      ; THEN NO EXECUTE FILE
27b4 ad b4 2a                   LDA          EFTABA                    ; TEST CURRENT
27b7 c5 40                      CMP          ZPGWRK
27b9 d0 08                      BNE          TXC2                      ; IS NOT
27bb ad b5 2a                   LDA          EFTABA+1
27be c5 41                      CMP          ZPGWRK+1
27c0 f0 01                      BEQ          TXC2                      ; IS
27c2 ca         TXC1            DEX                                    ; IS NOT
27c3 60         TXC2            RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; TSTFUC - TEST FILE USE CODE FOR PGM
                ;
                TSTFUC          EQU          *
27c4 4d c2 35                   EOR          CCBFUC
27c7 f0 0a                      BEQ          TFUCR
27c9 29 7f                      AND          #$7F
27cb f0 06                      BEQ          TFUCR
27cd 20 ea 22                   JSR          ECLOSE                    ; GO CLOSE THE SOB
27d0 4c d0 26                   JMP          ERNU1
27d3 60         TFUCR           RTS
                
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; #   END OF FILE:  DOSGOER
                ; #   LINES      :  215
                ; #   CHARACTERS :  8197
                ; #   Formatter  :  Assembly Language Reformatter 1.0.2 (07 January 1998)
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; #   PROJECT  :  APPLE ][ DOS 3.3 C SOURCE CODE LISTING -- (C) APPLE COMPUTER INC. JULY 1983
                ; #   FILE NAME:  BLDFTAB
                ; ####################################################################################################
                
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; BLDFTB - BUILD FILE TABLES
                ; TABLE MAP:
                ; HIMEM,SOP
                ; SBUFF N (256)
                ; DBUFF N (256)
                ; FTB N (FCBLEN)
                ; HEADER N (38)
                ; .
                ; .
                ; SBUFF 1
                ; DBUFF 1
                ; FTB 1
                ; HEADER 1
                ; THIS PROGRAM
                ;
                ; HEADER MAP:
                ; FILENAME (30)
                ; FTB PTR (2)
                ; DBUF PTR (2)
                ; SBUF PTR (2)
                ; LINK (2)
                ;
                BLDFTB          EQU          *
27d4 38                         SEC
27d5 ad 00 1d                   LDA          FTAB                      ; START OF FTAB AREA
27d8 85 40                      STA          ZPGWRK                    ; IS 1ST FTB PTR
27da ad 01 1d                   LDA          FTAB+1                    ; HEADER
27dd 85 41                      STA          ZPGWRK+1
27df ad 57 2a                   LDA          CNFTBS                    ; MOVE NO FTABS
27e2 8d 63 2a                   STA          TEMP1A                    ; TO TEMP
                ;
27e5 a0 00      BFT1            LDY          #0
27e7 98                         TYA
27e8 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y                ; 1ST CHAR FN=0
27ea a0 1e                      LDY          #30                       ; INC Y TO FCB PTR
27ec 38                         SEC
27ed a5 40                      LDA          ZPGWRK                    ; END OF PTR HEADER
27ef e9 2d                      SBC          #FCBLEN                   ; MINUS FTAB LENGTH
27f1 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y                ; IS START OF FTB
27f3 48                         PHA                                    ; SAVE LOW ADR BYTE
27f4 a5 41                      LDA          ZPGWRK+1
27f6 e9 00                      SBC          #0
27f8 c8                         INY
27f9 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y
27fb aa                         TAX
27fc ca                         DEX                                    ; FTB ADR - 256
27fd 68                         PLA                                    ; IS ADR DIR BUFF
27fe 48                         PHA
27ff c8                         INY
2800 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y                ; SET DIR BUF PTR
2802 8a                         TXA
2803 c8                         INY
2804 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y
2806 aa                         TAX
2807 ca                         DEX                                    ; DIR BUFF - 256
2808 68                         PLA                                    ; IS SBUFF ADR
2809 48                         PHA
280a c8                         INY
280b 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y
280d c8                         INY
280e 8a                         TXA
280f 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y
                ;
2811 ce 63 2a                   DEC          TEMP1A                    ; DECREMENT TABLE INDEX
2814 f0 17                      BEQ          BFT2                      ; COUNT AND BR IF DONE
2816 aa                         TAX
2817 68                         PLA
2818 38                         SEC
2819 e9 26                      SBC          #38                       ; SBUFF ADR - 38
281b c8                         INY
281c 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y                ; IF ADR OF NEXT TAB
281e 48                         PHA                                    ; WHICH GOES INTO
281f 8a                         TXA                                    ; LINK
2820 e9 00                      SBC          #0
2822 c8                         INY
2823 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y
2825 85 41                      STA          ZPGWRK+1                  ; AND INTO ZPGWRK
2827 68                         PLA                                    ; FOR NEXT ENTRY
2828 85 40                      STA          ZPGWRK                    ; BUILD
282a 4c e5 27                   JMP          BFT1                      ; GO BUILD NEXT
                ;
                BFT2            EQU          *
282d 48                         PHA
282e a9 00                      LDA          #0                        ; SET LAST LINK
2830 c8                         INY                                    ; TO ZERO
2831 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y
2833 c8                         INY
2834 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y
                ;
2836 ad b6 2a                   LDA          ASIBSW                    ; IF IB THEN GO
2839 f0 0b                      BEQ          BFTIB
                ;
283b 68                         PLA                                    ; SET APPLESOFT
283c 85 74                      STA          ASHM1+1                   ; UPPER MEM LIMITS
283e 85 70                      STA          ASHM2+1
2840 68                         PLA
2841 85 73                      STA          ASHM1
2843 85 6f                      STA          ASHM2
2845 60                         RTS
                ;
                BFTIB           EQU          *
2846 68                         PLA                                    ; SET IB
2847 85 4d                      STA          IBHMEM+1                  ; UPPER MEM LIMITS
2849 85 cb                      STA          IBSOP+1
284b 68                         PLA
284c 85 4c                      STA          IBHMEM
284e 85 ca                      STA          IBSOP
2850 60                         RTS
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; MVISW - MOVE INPUT SWITCH
                ;
                MVCSW           EQU          *
2851 a5 39                      LDA          INSW+1
2853 cd 03 1d                   CMP          CINA+1
2856 f0 12                      BEQ          MVOSW
2858 8d 56 2a                   STA          SVINS+1
285b a5 38                      LDA          INSW                      ; SAVE CHAR IN SWITCH
285d 8d 55 2a                   STA          SVINS
                ;
2860 ad 02 1d                   LDA          CINA                      ; SET DFB CHAR IN ADR
2863 85 38                      STA          INSW
2865 ad 03 1d                   LDA          CINA+1
2868 85 39                      STA          INSW+1
                ;
                ;
                ; MVOSW - MOVE OUTPUT SWITCH
                ;
                MVOSW           EQU          *
286a a5 37                      LDA          OUTSW+1
286c cd 05 1d                   CMP          COUTA+1
286f f0 12                      BEQ          MVSRTN
2871 8d 54 2a                   STA          SVOUTS+1
2874 a5 36                      LDA          OUTSW                     ; SAVE CHAR OUT SWITCH
2876 8d 53 2a                   STA          SVOUTS
                ;
2879 ad 04 1d                   LDA          COUTA                     ; SET DFB CHAR OUT ADR
287c 85 36                      STA          OUTSW
287e ad 05 1d                   LDA          COUTA+1
2881 85 37                      STA          OUTSW+1
                MVSRTN          EQU          *
2883 60                         RTS

                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ; COMMAND SYNTAX OP EQUATES FOR SYNTAX BYTE ONE
                ;
                NPB             EQU          $80                       ; NO PARMS OK, COMMAND GOES TO BASIC
                NPE             EQU          $40                       ; NO PARMS OK, COMMAND TO EXECUTION RTN
                FN1             EQU          $20                       ; FILE NAME1 REGD
                FN2             EQU          $10                       ; FILE NAME2 REQD
                NUM1            EQU          $08                       ; NUMERIC 0-7 REGD
                NUM2            EQU          $04                       ; NUMERIC 1-10 REQD
                RNONLY          EQU          $02                       ; RUN TIME ONLY FLAG.
                CREFLG          EQU          $01                       ; FLAG TO INDICATE CMDS THAT MAY CREATE FILES
                ;
                ; COMMAND SYNTAX OP EQUATES FOR SYNTAX BYTE TWO
                ;
                V               EQU          $40                       ; VOLUME ALLOWED
                D               EQU          $20                       ; DRIVE ALLOWED
                S               EQU          $10                       ; SLOT ALLOWED
                L               EQU          $08                       ; LENGTH ALLOWED
                R               EQU          $04                       ; RECORD NUMBER ALLOWED
                B               EQU          $02                       ; BYTE NUMBER ALLOWED
                ADR             EQU          $01                       ; ADDRESS
                CIO             EQU          $80                       ; C,I, OR O ALLOWED
                ;
                ; COMMAND SYNTAX TABLE
                ; EACH COMMAND HAS TWO BYTE ENTRY
                ;
                CMDSTB          EQU          *
2909 21 70                      DFB          FN1+CREFLG,V+D+S          ; INIT
290b a0 70                      DFB          NPB+FN1,V+D+S             ; LOAD
290d a1 70                      DFB          NPB+FN1+CREFLG,V+D+S      ; SAVE
290f a0 70                      DFB          NPB+FN1,V+D+S             ; RUN
2911 20 70                      DFB          FN1,V+D+S                 ; CHAIN
2913 20 70                      DFB          FN1,V+D+S                 ; DELETE
2915 20 70                      DFB          FN1,V+D+S                 ; LOCK
2917 20 70                      DFB          FN1,V+D+S                 ; UNLOCK

                ; USERENT - DOS EXTERNAL ENTRY POINT (USER ENTRY)
                ; ENTRY PARM:
                ;  A= HIGH ADDRESS OF CCB
                ;  Y= LOW ADDRESS OF CCB
                ;  X= 0 IF CREATE DESIRED
                ;  X> 0 IF CREATE NOT DESIRED
                ; EXIT PARM:
                ;  CARRY CLEAR = OPERATION OK
                ;  CARRY SET = ERROR
                ;
                SC2             EQU          *

2b03 8e 5f 2a   USRCR           STX          CMDNO                     ;SET UP FOR CREATE CAPIBILITY

                ;
30db ad e5 35   LNB3            LDA          DCBCRS+1                  ; IS CURRENT REL SECTOR
30de cd df 35                   CMP          DCBDNF+1                  ; IN CURRENT DIRECTOR (HI LIMIT)
30e1 90 10                      BCC          LNB6                      ; BR IF IN THIS ONE
30e3 d0 08                      BNE          LNB4                      ; BR IF IN A NEXT DIR
30e5 ad e4 35                   LDA          DCBCRS
30e8 cd de 35                   CMP          DCBDNF
30eb 90 06                      BCC          LNB6                      ; BR IF IN THIS ONE
                ;REQD SECTOR IN A NEXT DIRECTORY
30ed 20 5e 2f   LNB4            JSR          RDFDIR                    ; GO READ NEXT FILE DIR
30f0 90 d7                      BCC          LNB2                      ; BR NXT AVAIL
30f2 60                         RTS                                    ; RETURN IF EOF DIR
                ;
                ;
                LNB6            EQU          *                         ; CALCULATE DISPL INTO DIR
30f3 38                         SEC
30f4 ad e4 35                   LDA          DCBCRS                    ; REQD REL SECTOR MINUS
30f7 ed dc 35                   SBC          DCBDFS
30fa 0a                         ASL          A                         ; TIMES 2
30fb 69 0c                      ADC          #FDENT                    ; PLUS DISPL TO 1ST
30fd a8                         TAY
30fe 20 0c 2f                   JSR          MVFCBD                    ; MOVE DIR ADR TO ZPG
3101 b1 42                      LDA          (ZPGFCB),Y                ; GET TRACK
3103 d0 0f                      BNE          LNB7                      ; BR IF NOT ZERO
3105 ad bb 35                   LDA          CCBREQ
3108 c9 04                      CMP          #CRQWR                    ; WRITE!
310a f0 02                      BEQ          LNB7A
310c 38                         SEC
310d 60                         RTS
310e 20 34 31   LNB7A           JSR          GNWSEC                    ; GO GET A NEW SECTOR
3111 4c 20 31                   JMP          LNBCON
3114 8d d6 35   LNB7            STA          DCBTRK                    ; SET TRK INTO DCB
3117 c8                         INY
3118 b1 42                      LDA          (ZPGFCB),Y                ; GET SECTOR
311a 8d d7 35                   STA          DCBSEC                    ; PUT INTO DCB
311d 20 dc 2f                   JSR          RDSECT                    ; GO READ SECTOR
3120 ad e4 35   LNBCON          LDA          DCBCRS                    ; MOVE CUR REL SECTOR
3123 8d e0 35                   STA          DCBCMS
3126 ad e5 35                   LDA          DCBCRS+1                  ; TO CUR MEM SECTOR
3129 8d e1 35                   STA          DCBCMS+1
                ;
                LNB8            EQU          *
312c 20 10 2f                   JSR          MVFCBS                    ; MOVE SECTOR BUFF ADR TO ZP
312f ac e6 35                   LDY          DCBCSB                    ; GET SECT BYTE
3132 18                         CLC                                    ; CARRY CLEAR = ALL OK
3133 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;
                GNWSEC          EQU          *                         ; NEED NEW SECTOR
3134 8c 9d 33                   STY          TEMP2                     ; SAVE DIR INDEX
3137 20 44 32                   JSR          GETSEC                    ; GET A SECTOR
313a ac 9d 33                   LDY          TEMP2
313d c8                         INY
313e 91 42                      STA          (ZPGFCB),Y                ; SET NEW SECTOR
3140 8d d7 35                   STA          DCBSEC
3143 88                         DEY
3144 ad f1 35                   LDA          DCBATK
3147 91 42                      STA          (ZPGFCB),Y                ; SET NEW TRACK
3149 8d d6 35                   STA          DCBTRK
                ;
314c 20 10 2f                   JSR          MVFCBS
314f 20 d6 37                   JSR          CLRSEC                    ; GO CLEAR SECTOR
                ;
                ;
3152 a9 c0                      LDA          #$C0                      ; INDICATE BOTH
3154 0d d5 35                   ORA          DCBWRF                    ; DIR AND SECTOR
3157 8d d5 35                   STA          DCBWRF                    ; MUST BE WRITTEN
315a 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;INCRRB - INCREMENT RELATIVE RECORD BYTE
                ;
                INCRRB          EQU          *
315b ae ea 35                   LDX          DCBCRR                    ; MOVE BYTE JUST READ OR WRITTEN
315e 8e bd 35                   STX          CCBRRN
3161 ae eb 35                   LDX          DCBCRR+1
3164 8e be 35                   STX          CCBRRN+1
3167 ae ec 35                   LDX          DCBCRB                    ; X=REL BYTE (LOW)
316a ac ed 35                   LDY          DCBCRB+1                  ; Y=REL BYTE HI
316d 8e bf 35                   STX          CCBBYT
3170 8c c0 35                   STY          CCBBYT+1
3173 e8                         INX                                    ; INC REL BYTE (LOW)
3174 d0 01                      BNE          INCR1                     ; BR IF NO CARRY
3176 c8                         INY                                    ; INC REL BYTE (HI)
                ;
3177 cc e9 35   INCR1           CPY          DCBRCL+1                  ; REL BYTE=REC LENGTH
317a d0 11                      BNE          INCR2                     ; BR IF NOT
317c ec e8 35                   CPX          DCBRCL                    ; TEST LOW BYTES
317f d0 0c                      BNE          INCR2
3181 a2 00                      LDX          #0
3183 a0 00                      LDY          #0                        ; RESET REL BYTE TO ZERO
3185 ee ea 35                   INC          DCBCRR                    ; AND INCR
3188 d0 03                      BNE          INCR2                     ; RELATIVE RECORD
318a ee eb 35                   INC          DCBCRR+1
                ;
318d 8e ec 35   INCR2           STX          DCBCRB                    ; SAVE NEW RELATIVE BYTE
3190 8c ed 35                   STY          DCBCRB+1
                ;
3193 60                         RTS
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;INCSCB - INCREMENT SECTOR BYTE
                ;
                INCSCB          EQU          *
3194 ee e6 35                   INC          DCBCSB                    ; INC SECTOR BYTE
3197 d0 08                      BNE          INCS2                     ; BR IF NOT FULL
3199 ee e4 35                   INC          DCBCRS                    ; AND INCR
319c d0 03                      BNE          INCS2                     ; RELATIVE SECTOR
319e ee e5 35                   INC          DCBCRS+1
                ;
                ;
                INCS2           EQU          *
31a1 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;MIBDA - MOVE AND INCREMENT CCBDAT
                ;
                MIBDA           EQU          *
31a2 ac c3 35                   LDY          CCBBBA                    ; Y=ADR LOW
31a5 ae c4 35                   LDX          CCBBBA+1                  ; X=ADR HI
31a8 84 42                      STY          ZPGFCB                    ; PUT ADR INTO ZPG
31aa 86 43                      STX          ZPGFCB+1
                ;
31ac ee c3 35                   INC          CCBBBA                    ; INC ADR LOW
31af d0 03                      BNE          MIB1                      ; BR IF NOT ZERO
31b1 ee c4 35                   INC          CCBBBA+1                  ; INC ADR HI
31b4 60         MIB1            RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;
                ;DTBLN - DECREMENT BLOCK LENGTH AND TEST ZERO
                ;
                DTBLN           EQU          *
31b5 ac c1 35                   LDY          CCBBLN                    ; GET LEN LOW
31b8 d0 08                      BNE          DTB1                      ; BR IF NOT ZERO
31ba ae c2 35                   LDX          CCBBLN+1                  ; GET LEN HI
31bd f0 07                      BEQ          DTB2                      ; BR IF LEN=0
31bf ce c2 35                   DEC          CCBBLN+1                  ; DEC LEN (HIGH)
31c2 ce c1 35   DTB1            DEC          CCBBLN                    ; DEC LEN (LOW)
31c5 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;
31c6 4c 7f 33   DTB2            JMP          GOODIO                    ; FINISHED BLOCK

                ;FNDFIL - FIND FILE NAME IN VOLUUME DIR
                ;
                FNDFIL          EQU          *
31c9 20 f7 2f                   JSR          RDVTOC                    ; GO GET VTOC
31cc ad c3 35                   LDA          CCBFN1                    ; MOVE FN PTR
31cf 85 42                      STA          ZPGFCB                    ; TO ZERO PAGE
31d1 ad c4 35                   LDA          CCBFN1+1
31d4 85 43                      STA          ZPGFCB+1
31d6 a9 01                      LDA          #1
31d8 8d 9d 33   FF1             STA          TEMP2
31db a9 00                      LDA          #0
31dd 8d d8 35                   STA          DCBVDR
31e0 18                         CLC
                FF2             EQU          *
31e1 ee d8 35                   INC          DCBVDR
31e4 20 11 30                   JSR          RDVDIR                    ; GO GET VDIR SECTOR
31e7 b0 51                      BCS          FF4A
31e9 a2 00                      LDX          #0                        ; SET FOR 1ST FILE
                ;
31eb 8e 9c 33   FF3             STX          TEMP1                     ; SAVE INDEX
31ee bd c6 34                   LDA          VDFILE,X                  ; GET FILE TRK
31f1 f0 1f                      BEQ          FF6                       ; BR IF LAST ENTRY
31f3 30 22                      BMI          FF7                       ; BR DELETED ENTRY
31f5 a0 00                      LDY          #0                        ; X=X+3
31f7 e8                         INX
31f8 e8                         INX
31f9 e8         FF4             INX
31fa b1 42                      LDA          (ZPGFCB),Y                ; GET FN CHAR
31fc dd c6 34                   CMP          VDFILE,X                  ; COMPARE TO ENTRY CHAR
31ff d0 0a                      BNE          FF5                       ; BR IF NOT SAME
3201 c8                         INY
3202 c0 1e                      CPY          #30                       ; ALL 30 CHARS
3204 d0 f3                      BNE          FF4                       ; BR IF NOT
3206 ae 9c 33                   LDX          TEMP1                     ; GET INDEX
3209 18                         CLC                                    ; FILE FOUND
320a 60                         RTS                                    ; RETURN
                ;
                FF5             EQU          *
320b 20 30 32                   JSR          VDINC
320e 90 db                      BCC          FF3
3210 b0 cf                      BCS          FF2
                ;
3212 ac 9d 33   FF6             LDY          TEMP2                     ; LOOKING FOR DELETED
3215 d0 c1                      BNE          FF1                       ; BR IF NOT (DO)
                ;
3217 ac 9d 33   FF7             LDY          TEMP2                     ; LOOKING FOR EMPTY
321a d0 ef                      BNE          FF5                       ; BR IF NOT
                ;
                MVFN            EQU          *
321c a0 00                      LDY          #0                        ; HAVE NEW ENTTRY
321e e8                         INX
321f e8                         INX
3220 e8         FF8             INX
3221 b1 42                      LDA          (ZPGFCB),Y                ; MOVE FILE NAME
3223 9d c6 34                   STA          VDFILE,X
3226 c8                         INY
3227 c0 1e                      CPY          #30
3229 d0 f5                      BNE          FF8
                ;
322b ae 9c 33                   LDX          TEMP1                     ; GET INDEX
322e 38                         SEC                                    ; SET NOT OLD
322f 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
                VDINC           EQU          *
3230 18                         CLC
3231 ad 9c 33                   LDA          TEMP1
3234 69 23                      ADC          #35
3236 aa                         TAX
3237 e0 f5                      CPX          #VDFLEN
3239 60                         RTS
                FF4A            EQU          *
323a a9 00                      LDA          #0
323c ac 9d 33                   LDY          TEMP2
323f d0 97                      BNE          FF1
3241 4c 77 33                   JMP          ERROR9
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;GETSEC - GET A SECTOR
                ;
                GETSEC          EQU          *
3244 ad f1 35                   LDA          DCBATK                    ; GET ALLOCATED TRK
3247 f0 21                      BEQ          GSS1                      ; BR IF NONE
                ;
                GS0             EQU          *
3249 ce f0 35                   DEC          DCBALS                    ; DECREMENT SECTOR NO
324c 30 17                      BMI          CS2                       ; BR IF NO SECTORS REM
                ;
324e 18                         CLC
324f a2 04                      LDX          #4                        ; 4 BYTE SHIFT
3251 3e f1 35   GS1             ROL          DCBABM-1,X                ; SHIFT BYTE LEFT
3254 ca                         DEX
3255 d0 fa                      BNE          GS1
3257 90 f0                      BCC          GS0                       ; BR IF NO SECTOR
                ;
3259 ee ee 35                   INC          DCBNSA
325c d0 03                      BNE          GS1A
325e ee ef 35                   INC          DCBNSA+1
                GS1A            EQU          *
3261 ad f0 35                   LDA          DCBALS                    ; GET ALLOCATED SECTOR
3264 60                         RTS                                    ; RETURN
                ;
3265 a9 00      CS2             LDA          #0                        ; CLEAR ALLOCATED
3267 8d f1 35                   STA          DCBATK                    ; TRK
                ;
326a a9 00      GSS1            LDA          #0                        ; SET SEARCH STATE=0
326c 8d 9e 33                   STA          TEMP3
326f 20 f7 2f                   JSR          RDVTOC                    ; GET VTOC
                ;
                GS2             EQU          *
3272 18                         CLC
3273 ad eb 33                   LDA          VALCA1                    ; GET LAST ALLOCATTED TRK
3276 6d ec 33                   ADC          VALCA2                    ; AD (+1) OR (-1)
3279 f0 09                      BEQ          GS3                       ; BR IF DECK TO ZERO
327b cd ef 33                   CMP          VNOTRK
327e 90 14                      BCC          GS5                       ; BR IF NOT AT OUTER LIMIT
3280 a9 ff                      LDA          #$FF                      ; SET (-1)
3282 d0 0a                      BNE          GS4
3284 ad 9e 33   GS3             LDA          TEMP3                     ; GET SEARCH STATE
3287 d0 37                      BNE          ERR9                      ; BR IF NOT ZERO
3289 a9 01                      LDA          #1                        ; SET (+1)
328b 8d 9e 33                   STA          TEMP3                     ; SET SEARCH STATE = 1
328e 8d ec 33   GS4             STA          VALCA2                    ; SET NEW (+1) OR -1)
3291 18                         CLC
3292 69 11                      ADC          #17                       ; ADD VTOC TRK NO
3294 8d eb 33   GS5             STA          VALCA1                    ; SET NEW LAST ALLOCATED
3297 8d f1 35                   STA          DCBATK                    ; PUT IN DCB
                ;
329a a8                         TAY                                    ; ALLOCATED TRACK
329b 0a                         ASL          A                         ; TIME 4
329c 0a                         ASL          A
329d a8                         TAY
329e a2 04                      LDX          #4
32a0 18                         CLC
32a1 b9 f6 33   GS6             LDA          VSECAL+3,Y                ; MOVE BIT MAP BYTE
32a4 9d f1 35                   STA          DCBABM-1,X
32a7 f0 06                      BEQ          GS7                       ; BR IF NO BITS ON
32a9 38                         SEC                                    ; SET HAVE A SECTOR
32aa a9 00                      LDA          #0                        ; CLEAR VTOC BYTE
32ac 99 f6 33                   STA          VSECAL+3,Y
32af 88         GS7             DEY
32b0 ca                         DEX
32b1 d0 ee                      BNE          GS6                       ; BR IF MORE TO MOVE
32b3 90 bd                      BCC          GS2
32b5 20 fb 2f                   JSR          WRVTOC                    ; GO WRITE VTOC
32b8 ad f0 33                   LDA          VNOSEC                    ; GET NO SECTORS
32bb 8d f0 35                   STA          DCBALS                    ; SET IN DCB SECTOR BYTE
32be d0 89                      BNE          GS0                       ; GO ALLOCATED SECTOR
32c0 4c 77 33   ERR9            JMP          ERROR9
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;FRETRK - FREE TRACK OF SECTORS
                ;
                FRETRK          EQU          *
32c3 ad f1 35                   LDA          DCBATK                    ; GET ALLOCATED TRACK
32c6 d0 01                      BNE          FT1                       ; BR IF NONE
32c8 60                         RTS                                    ; DONE
32c9 48         FT1             PHA
32ca 20 f7 2f                   JSR          RDVTOC                    ; GET VTOC
32cd ac f0 35                   LDY          DCBALS                    ; GET SECTOS
32d0 68                         PLA                                    ; GET TRACK
32d1 18                         CLC                                    ; SET FREE
32d2 20 dd 32                   JSR          FRESEC                    ; GO FREE
32d5 a9 00                      LDA          #0                        ; CLEAR ALLOCATED TRK
32d7 8d f1 35                   STA          DCBATK
32da 4c fb 2f                   JMP          WRVTOC                    ; WRITE VTOC
                ;
                ;FRESEC - FREE A SECTOR
                ;A=TRK, Y=SECTOR, C=ON/OFF
                ;
                FRESEC          EQU          *
32dd a2 fc      FS1             LDX          #252                      ; 4 BYTE SHIFT
32df 7e f6 34   FS2             ROR          DCBABM-252,X              ; SHIFT IN CARRY
32e2 e8                         INX                                    ; NEXT BYTE
32e3 d0 fa                      BNE          FS2                       ; BR IF NOT DONE
32e5 c8                         INY                                    ; INC SECTOR NO
32e6 cc f0 33                   CPY          VNOSEC                    ; NORMAL
32e9 d0 f2                      BNE          FS1                       ; BR IF NOT
                ;
32eb 0a                         ASL          A                         ; TRACK*4
32ec 0a                         ASL          A
32ed a8                         TAY
32ee f0 0f                      BEQ          FS4
32f0 a2 04                      LDX          #4
32f2 bd f1 35   FS3             LDA          DCBABM-1,X                ; GET BIT MAP BYTE
32f5 19 f6 33                   ORA          VSECAL+3,Y                ; OR WITH VTOC BM
32f8 99 f6 33                   STA          VSECAL+3,Y
32fb 88                         DEY
32fc ca                         DEX
32fd d0 f3                      BNE          FS3
32ff 60         FS4             RTS                                    ; DONE
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;LOCSEC - LOCATE SECTOR FOR RECORD I/O
                ;
                ;RELSEC = (REL REC * RECLEN + RELBYTE)/256
                ;SECBYT = REMAINDER
                ;
                LOCSEC          EQU          *
3300 ad bd 35                   LDA          CCBRRN                    ; RELATIVE RECORD NUMBER
3303 8d e6 35                   STA          DCBCSB                    ; TO CSB FOR MULT
3306 8d ea 35                   STA          DCBCRR                    ; AND CRR FOR SAVE
3309 ad be 35                   LDA          CCBRRN+1
330c 8d e4 35                   STA          DCBCRS
330f 8d eb 35                   STA          DCBCRR+1
3312 a9 00                      LDA          #0
3314 8d e5 35                   STA          DCBCRS+1                  ; HIGH CRS=0
3317 a0 10                      LDY          #16                       ; 16 BIT MULT
                ;
3319 aa         LS1             TAX                                    ; SAVE MS BYTE
331a ad e6 35                   LDA          DCBCSB
331d 4a                         LSR          A                         ; IF NO CARRY THEN NO PART PROD
331e b0 03                      BCS          LS1A
3320 8a                         TXA
3321 90 0e                      BCC          LS2
3323 18         LS1A            CLC
3324 ad e5 35                   LDA          DCBCRS+1                  ; FPORM PARTIAL PROD
3327 6d e8 35                   ADC          DCBRCL
332a 8d e5 35                   STA          DCBCRS+1
332d 8a                         TXA
332e 6d e9 35                   ADC          DCBRCL+1
                ;
3331 6a         LS2             ROR          A                         ; MULT BY 2
3332 6e e5 35                   ROR          DCBCRS+1
3335 6e e4 35                   ROR          DCBCRS
3338 6e e6 35                   ROR          DCBCSB
333b 88                         DEY                                    ; DEC BIT COUNT
333c d0 db                      BNE          LS1                       ; BR IF MORE BITS
                ;
                ;;;                DO           DOS33B
333e 18                         CLC                                    ; FOR FILE LENGTH > $7FFF BYTES
                ;;;                FIN
333f ad bf 35                   LDA          CCBBYT                    ; ADD REL BYTE RESULT
3342 8d ec 35                   STA          DCBCRB                    ; (SAVE REL BYTE)
3345 6d e6 35                   ADC          DCBCSB
3348 8d e6 35                   STA          DCBCSB
334b ad c0 35                   LDA          CCBBYT+1

3351 6d e4 35                   ADC          DCBCRS
3354 8d e4 35                   STA          DCBCRS
                ;;;                DO           DOS33B
3357 90 03                      BCC          DONTINC
3359 ee e5 35                   INC          DCBCRS+1
335c 60         DONTINC         RTS
335d 00 00                      DS           2,$00
                ;;;                ELSE
                ;;;                LDA          #0
                ;;;                ADC          DCBCRS+1
                ;;;                STA          DCBCRS+1
                ;;;                RTS
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                PAGE

3361 d0 22                      BNE          ERRORA

                ;
                VSECAL          EQU          *                         ; SECTOR ALLOCATION AREA
                ;SECTORS ALLOCATED BY BIT MAP
                ;4 BYTES OF BITS PER TRACK
                ;LEFT MOST BIT REPRESENTS SECTOR N
                ;WHERE N=NO SECTORS PER TRACK

                ;
                ;;;                PAGE
                                ORG          VTOC+256
                ;
                ;VOLUME DIRECTORY AREA
                ;
                VOLDIR          EQU          *
34bb 02         VDTCDE          DFB          2                         ; VOLUME DIRECTORY TYPE CODE
                VDLTRK          DS           1                         ; VD LINK TRACK
                VDLSEC          DS           1                         ; VD LINK SECTOR
                VDNF            DS           1                         ; VD NUMBER FILES THIS SECTOR
                VDSPAR          DS           7                         ; SPARES
                ;
                VDFILE          EQU          *                         ; FILE ALLOCATION AREA (7 FILES)
                ;EACH FILE:
                ;FILE DIR TRK
                ;FILE DIR SECTOR
                ;FILE USE CODE
                ;FILE NAME (30)
                ;FILE SECTOR COUNT (2)
                                ORG          VOLDIR+256
                VDEND           EQU          *
                VDLEN           EQU          *-VOLDIR
                VDFLEN          EQU          *-VDFILE

                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;COMMAND CONTROL BLOCK (CCB)
                ;
                CCB             EQU          *
                CCBREQ          DS           1                         ; USER REQUEST BYTE
                CRQNUL          EQU          0                         ; 0-NO REQUEST
                CRQOPN          EQU          1                         ; 1-OPEN FILE
                CRQCLS          EQU          2                         ; 2-CLOSE FILE
                CRQRD           EQU          3                         ; 3-READ DATA
                CRQWR           EQU          4                         ; WRITE DATA
                CRQDEL          EQU          5                         ; 5-DELETE FILE
                CRQDIR          EQU          6                         ; 6-READ DIRECTORY
                CRQLCK          EQU          7                         ; 7-LOCK FILE
                CRQUNL          EQU          8                         ; 8-UNLOCK FILE
                CRQRNM          EQU          9                         ; 9-RENAME
                CRQPOS          EQU          10                        ; 10-POSITION FILE
                CRQFMT          EQU          11                        ; 11-FORMAT
                CRQVAR          EQU          12                        ; 12 - VERIFY
                CRQMAX          EQU          13
                ;
                CCBBSA          EQU          *                         ; FORMAT - BOOT START ADR PAGE
                CCBRQM          DS           1                         ; RREQUEST MODIFIER BYTE
                CRMNUL          EQU          0                         ; NO MODIFIER
                CRMNBT          EQU          1                         ; R/W - 1 - NEXT BYTE
                CRMNBL          EQU          2                         ; R/W - 2 - NEXT BLOCK
                CRMSBT          EQU          3                         ; R/W - 3 - SPECIFC BYTE
                CRMSBL          EQU          4                         ; R/W - 4 - SPECIFIC BLOCK
                CRMMAX          EQU          5
                ;
                CCBRRN          EQU          *                         ; I/O - RELATIVE RECORD NUMBER
                CCBFN2          EQU          *                         ; RENAME - FILE NAME 2 PTR
                CCBRLN          DS           2                         ; OPEN - RECORD LENGTH
                ;
                CCBBYT          EQU          *                         ; I/O - RELATIVE BYTE NO (2 BYTES)
                CCBVOL          DS           1                         ; OPEN - VOL NO.
                CCBDRV          DS           1                         ; OPEN - DRIVE
                ;
                CCBBLN          EQU          *                         ; I/O - BLOCK LENGTH (2 BYTES)
                CCBSLT          DS           1                         ; OPEN - SLOT NO
                CCBFUC          DS           1                         ; OPEN - FILE USE CODE
                ;
                CCBFN1          EQU          *                         ; OPEN, DELETE, LOCK, UNLOCK, RENAME - FILENAME P
                CCBBBA          EQU          *                         ; BLOCKK I/O - BLOCK BUFFER PTR
                CCBDAT          DS           2                         ; BYTE I/O - DATA BYTE
                ;
                CCBSTA          DS           1                         ; RESULT STATUS
                CREFUN          EQU          1                         ; FCB UNALLOCATED
                CRERR           EQU          2                         ; CCB REQ RANGE ERR
                CREMRE          EQU          3                         ; REQ MOD RANGE ERR
                CREPRO          EQU          4                         ; WRITE PROTECT
                CREEOF          EQU          5                         ; END OF FILE ON READ
                CREFNF          EQU          6                         ; FILE NOT FOUND
                CREVMM          EQU          7                         ; VOL MIS MATCH
                CREIOE          EQU          8                         ; I/O ERR
                CRENSA          EQU          9                         ; NO SECTORS AVAILABLE
                CREFLK          EQU          10                        ; FILE LOCKED
                ;
                CCBSM           DS           1                         ; STATUS MODIFIER
                CCBFCB          DS           2                         ; FCB PTR
                CCBDBP          DS           2                         ; DIR BUF PTR
                CCBSBP          DS           2                         ; SECTOR BUF PTR
                CCBSPR          DS           4                         ; SPARE
                CCBLEN          EQU          *-CCB                     ; CCB LENGTH
                CFCBAD          EQU          CCBFCB
                CFCBDR          EQU          CCBDBP
                CFCBSB          EQU          CCBSBP
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;FILE CONTROL BLOCK (FCB) DEFINITION
                ;DCB - FILE DATA CONTROL BLOCK
                ;
                FCB             EQU          *
                ;
                ;DATA CONTROL BLOCK
                ;
                FCBDCB          EQU          *
                DCBFDT          DS           1                         ; 1ST FILE DIRECTORY TRACK
                DCBFDS          DS           1                         ; 1ST FILE DIRECTORY SECTOR
                DCBCDT          DS           1                         ; CURRENT FILE DIRECTORY TRACK
                DCBCDS          DS           1                         ; CURRENT FILE DIRECTORY SECTOR
                DCBWRF          DS           1                         ; WRITE REQD FLAG
                ;$80=WRITE FILE DIR
                ;$40=WRITE SECTOR DIR
                DCBTRK          DS           1                         ; SECTOR TRACK ADR
                DCBSEC          DS           1                         ; SECTOR ADR
                DCBVDR          DS           1                         ; VOL DIR REC
                DCBVDI          DS           1                         ; VOL DIR INDEX
                DCBDMS          DS           2                         ; MAX NO DIRECTORY SECTORS
                DCBDFS          DS           2                         ; CURRENT DIR 1ST REL SECTOR
                DCBDNF          DS           2                         ; REL SECTOR OF NXT DIR
                DCBCMS          DS           2                         ; SECTOR CURRENTLY IN MEMORY
                DCBSDL          DS           2                         ; SECTOR DATA LENGTH
                DCBCRS          DS           2                         ; CURRENT RELATIVE SECTOR
                DCBCSB          DS           2                         ; CURRENT SECTOR BYTE
                DCBRCL          DS           2                         ; RECORD LENGTH
                DCBCRR          DS           2                         ; CURRENT RELATIVE REC
                DCBCRB          DS           2                         ; CURRENT RELATIVE BYTE
                DCBNSA          DS           2                         ; NO SECTORS ALLOCATED
                ;
                DCBALS          DS           1                         ; ALLOCATION SECTOR BYTE
                DCBATK          DS           1                         ; ALLOCATION TRACK
                DCBABM          DS           4                         ; ALLOCATION TRACK SECTOR BIT MAP
                ;
                DCBFUC          DS           1                         ; FILE USE CODE
                DCBSLT          DS           1                         ; SLOT NUMBER
                DCBDRV          DS           1                         ; DRIVE NUMBER
                DCBVOL          DS           1                         ; VOLUME DRIVER
                DCBVTN          DS           1                         ; VTOC TRACK NUMBER
                ;
                DCBSPR          DS           3                         ; SPARES
                ;
                DCBLEN          EQU          *-FCBDCB                  ; DCB LENGTH
                FCBLEN          EQU          *-FCB                     ; FCB LENGTH
                ;

                ; #   END OF FILE:  FVCBUFS
                ; #   LINES      :  187
