                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR DOS BOOT'
                HERE3L          EQU          >*
                REMDR3          EQU          256-HERE3L
                                ORG          *+REMDR3
                TRK0LDR         EQU          *
                ;;;                DO           >TRK0LDR
                ;;;                ???                                    ;DELIBERATE ERROR IF NOT AT PAGE BOUNDARY
                ;;;                FIN
                ***************************
                *                         *
                * 16-SECTOR DOS BOOTSTRAP *
                *                         *
                *     RICK AURICCHIO      *
                *       10/10/79          *
                *                         *
                ***************************
                *                         *
                * THIS PROGRAM RESIDES IN *
                *  TRACK 0, SECTOR 0 OF A *
                *  DOS DISKETTE. ITS SOLE *
                *  PURPOSE IS TO READ THE *
                *  DOS LOADER PROGRAM IN  *
                *  FROM TRACK 0, SECTORS  *
                *  1-9. CONTROL IS THEN   *
                *  TRANSFERRED TO THAT    *
                *  PROGRAM.               *
                *                         *
                * NOTE: THE DOS LOADER    *
                *  CONTAINS THE ENTIRE    *
                *  SET OF 16-SECTOR CORE  *
                *  ROUTINES; THOSE CORE   *
                *  ROUTINES ARE USED TO   *
                *  LOAD THE REST OF THE   *
                *  DOS IMAGE INTO MEMORY. *
                *                         *
                ***************************
                POINTA          EQU          $26                       ;BUFFER POINTER
                BSLOT           EQU          $2B                       ;BOOT BSLOT
                BSECTR          EQU          $3D                       ;LAST BSECTR READ
                BTEMP           EQU          $3E                       ;ADDRESS BTEMP
                BRETRY          EQU          $5C                       ;OFFSET TO READER
                *
                MONINIT         EQU          $FB2F                     ;MONINIT SCREEN
                BHERE3          EQU          >*
                BOOTCNT         EQU          $800+BHERE3
3600 01                         DFB          01
                ;;;                PAGE
3601 a5 27                      LDA          POINTA+1                  ;WHERE DID BSECTR GET LOADED?
3603 c9 09                      CMP          #09                       ; (AT 0800)?
3605 d0 18                      BNE          READNEXT                  ;=>NO. WE'RE LOADING SOMETHING
                * WE'VE BEEN BOOTED. SET UP
                *  PARAMS FOR BOOT PROM SO
                *  THAT WE'LL READ IN TRACK 0,
                *  BSECTRS 00-09.
3607 a5 2b                      LDA          BSLOT                     ;GET BOOT BSLOT
3609 4a                         LSR          A                         ;CONVERT TO CX00
360a 4a                         LSR          A
360b 4a                         LSR          A
360c 4a                         LSR          A
360d 09 c0                      ORA          #$C0
360f 85 3f                      STA          BTEMP+1
3611 a9 5c                      LDA          #BRETRY                   ;PROM ROUTINE OFFSET
3613 85 3e                      STA          BTEMP
3615 18                         CLC                                    ;BUMP LOAD ADDRESS UP TO
3616 ad fe 08                   LDA          LOADADDR+1                ; LAST PAGE SO WE
3619 6d ff 08                   ADC          BGRPGC                    ;  CAN LOAD 'EM BACKWARDS...
361c 8d fe 08                   STA          LOADADDR+1
                * READ IN ANOTHER BSECTR FROM
                *  TRACK ZERO...
361f ae ff 08   READNEXT        LDX          BGRPGC
3622 30 15                      BMI          GOLOADER                  ;=>ALL DONE...EXECUTE IT!
3624 bd 4d 08                   LDA          TABLE,X                   ;GET PHYSICAL BSECTR NUMBER
3627 85 3d                      STA          BSECTR                    ; AND SET FOR BOOT PROM READ
3629 ce ff 08                   DEC          BGRPGC                    ;ONE LESS BELL TO ANSWER..
362c ad fe 08                   LDA          LOADADDR+1                ;GET LOAD ADDRESS
362f 85 27                      STA          POINTA+1                  ; FOR BSECTR READ
3631 ce fe 08                   DEC          LOADADDR+1                ;MOVE LOAD ADDRESS DOWN A PAGE
3634 a6 2b                      LDX          BSLOT                     ;RESTORE BSLOT NUMBER
3636 6c 3e 00                   JMP          (BTEMP)                   ;READ MORE OF TRACK 0
3639 ee fe 08   GOLOADER        INC          LOADADDR+1                ;ENTRY AT SECOND PAGE
363c ee fe 08                   INC          LOADADDR+1
363f 20 89 fe                   JSR          SETKBD                    ;CLEAR IN#X
3642 20 93 fe                   JSR          SETVID                    ; AND PR#X
3645 20 2f fb                   JSR          MONINIT                   ;MONINIT THE SCREEN PARAMS
3648 a6 2b                      LDX          BSLOT                     ;PASS BSLOT NBR TO LOADER
364a 6c fd 08                   JMP          (LOADADDR)                ;OFF TO LOOADER!
                * TABLE OF PHYSICAL BSECTR NUMBERS
                *  WHICH CORRESPOND TO THE LOGICAL
                *  BSECTRS 0-F ON TRACK ZERO...
                BHERE2          EQU          >*
                TABLE           EQU          $800+BHERE2
364d 00 0d 0b                   DFB          $00,13,11                 ;00->00,01->13,02->11
3650 09 07 05                   DFB          09,07,05                  ;03->09,04->07;05->05
3653 03 01 0e                   DFB          03,01,14                  ;06->03,07->01,08->14
3656 0c 0a 08                   DFB          12,10,08                  ;09->12,10->10,11->08
3659 06 04 02                   DFB          06,04,02,15               ;12->6,13->04,14->02,15->15
365c 0f
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;;;                REP          40
                * APPEND BUG PATCHES
                ****************************
                SC3             EQU          *
365d 00         EOFFLAG         DFB          0
                CLOSFILE        EQU          *
365e 20 64 27                   JSR          FILSRC                    ;FILE BUFFER FOUND?
3661 b0 08                      BCS          NOTFOUND                  ;=> NO, SO SKIP IT.
3663 a9 00                      LDA          #0                        ;YES, CLOSE IT
3665 a8                         TAY
3666 8d 5d 36                   STA          EOFFLAG
3669 91 40                      STA          (ZPGWRK),Y                ;RIGHT NOW
366b ad c5 35   NOTFOUND        LDA          CCBSTA                    ;ORIGINAL INSTRUCTION
366e 4c d2 26                   JMP          ERROR                     ;BACK TO ERROR HANDLER
                ****************************
                BUMPER          EQU          *
3671 ad 5d 36                   LDA          EOFFLAG                   ;SHOULD WE?
3674 f0 08                      BEQ          GOBACK                    ;=> NO
3676 ee bd 35                   INC          CCBRRN                    ;BUMP CCB RECORD NUMBER
3679 d0 03                      BNE          GOBACK
367b ee be 35                   INC          CCBRRN+1                  ;TO GET TO NEXT SECTOR
367e a9 00      GOBACK          LDA          #0
3680 8d 5d 36                   STA          EOFFLAG                   ;TURN FLAG OFF
3683 4c 84 3a                   JMP          FIXIT2                    ;Go to FIXIT2 as exit
                ;;;                REP          40
                VPATCH          EQU          *
3686 8d bc 35                   STA          CCBRQM                    ;ORIGINAL INSTRUCTION
3689 20 a8 26                   JSR          DOSGO                     ;GO SAVE
368c 20 ea 22                   JSR          ECLOSE                    ;CLOSE THE FILE
368f 4c 7d 22                   JMP          EVAR                      ;GO VERIFY IT AFTER SAVE
                ****************************
                EOFFIX          EQU          *
3692 a0 13                      LDY          #$13                      ;PEEK INTO THE FCB: IF
3694 b1 42      CHKFILE         LDA          (ZPGFCB),Y                ;DCBCRS,DCBCSB ARE ZEROS,
3696 d0 14                      BNE          FIXIT                     ; THEN WE HAVE EMPTY FILE
3698 c8                         INY
3699 c0 17                      CPY          #$17
369b d0 f7                      BNE          CHKFILE
369d a0 19                      LDY          #$19
369f b1 42      MOVE            LDA          (ZPGFCB),Y                ; DCBCRR,DCBCRB
36a1 99 a4 35                   STA          CCBRRN-$19,Y              ;INTO CCBRRN,CCBBYT
36a4 c8                         INY
36a5 c0 1d                      CPY          #$1D
36a7 d0 f6                      BNE          MOVE
36a9 4c bb 26   BACK            JMP          DOSGO2A                   ;NOW LET APPEND CONTINUE
                FIXIT           EQU          *
36ac a2 ff                      LDX          #$FF                      ;SET FLAG SO APPEND WILL
36ae 8e 5d 36                   STX          EOFFLAG                   ;KNOW TO CROSS SECTOR BOUNDARY
36b1 d0 f6                      BNE          BACK                      ;ALWAYS TAKEN
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;;;                REP          40
                * END OF BOOT PAGE DATA SETUP
                ;;;                REP          40
                *
                * FIXIT2 was developed to fix the wrap around
                * problem APPEND has when trying to APPEND to
                * a sequential file which is >255 sectors in length.
                *
                *                  Fix by
                *
                *              Fern Bachman
                *               Guil Banks
                *           September 28, 1982
                *
                * Fix to fix added to correctly APPEND to a sector
                * 255 bytes in length
                *
                *                    by
                *                Guil Banks
                *               July 11, 1983
                *
                ;;;                REP          30
                ;;;                SKP          1
                ;;;;FIXIT2          EQU          *
                ;;;;;                LDA          CCBRLN                    ;Current record length lo
                ;;;;;                STA          DCBCSB                    ;Current sector byte
                ;;;;;                STA          DCBCRR                    ;Current relative record
                ;;;;;                LDA          CCBRLN+1                  ;Do hi as well
                ;;;;;                STA          DCBCSB+1
                ;;;;;                STA          DCBCRR+1
                ;;;;;                STA          DCBCRS                    ;Set current relative sector
                ;;;;;                TSX
                ;;;;;                STX          ENTSTK
                ;;;;;                JMP          GOODIO
                ;;;                SKP          2
                ;;;                REP          30
                *
                *   Upper/Lower case patch
                *   for DOS 3.3C and BASIC
                *
                *            by
                *        Guil Banks
                *        Mark Houde
                *
                ;;;                REP          30
                *
                * This routine converts all characters
                * that are not between quotes to
                * upper case and returns them to the
                * input buffer ($200). This works with
                * DOS, Integer & Applesoft.
                *
                * Upon entry -
                *
                *              X Reg = 0
                *
                * Upon exit  -
                *
                *              Y Reg = $FF
                *              ACCUM = $8D
                *              X Reg = unknown
                *
                ;;;                REP          30
                ;;;                DO           ULC
                ;;;UPRCASE         EQU          *
                ;;;LUP1            LDA          LBUFF,X                   ;Get a char
                ;;;                CMP          #'"+$80                   ;Is it a quote?
                ;;;                BNE          CHK4UC                    ;=> if not
                ;;;LUP2            INX                                    ;Bump to next char
                ;;;                LDA          LBUFF,X                   ;Get it
                ;;;                CMP          #'"+$80                   ;Closing quote?
                ;;;                BEQ          NEXTCHR                   ;=> if so
                ;;;                CMP          #$8D                      ;End of line?
                ;;;                BNE          LUP2                      ;=> if not
                ;;;ULFINI          LDY          #$FF                      ;Do what DOS wants
                ;;;                STY          CMDNO
                ;;;                RTS                                    ;   & exit
                ;;;CHK4UC          EQU          *
                ;;;                CMP          #$E0                      ;Upper case?
                ;;;                BCC          CHK4CR                    ;=> if not
                ;;;                AND          #$DF                      ;Make upper case
                ;;;                STA          LBUFF,X                   ;   & restore
                ;;;CHK4CR          CMP          #$8D                      ;End of input?
                ;;;                BEQ          ULFINI                    ;=> if so
                ;;;NEXTCHR         INX                                    ;Bump to next char
                ;;;                BNE          LUP1                      ;=> always
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                SKP          1
                BHERE1          EQU          >*
36b3 00 00 00                   DS           $FD-BHERE1,0
36b6 00 00 00
36b9 00 00 00
36bc 00 00 00
36bf 00 00 00
36c2 00 00 00
36c5 00 00 00
36c8 00 00 00
36cb 00 00 00
36ce 00 00 00
36d1 00 00 00
36d4 00 00 00
36d7 00 00 00
36da 00 00 00
36dd 00 00 00
36e0 00 00 00
36e3 00 00 00
36e6 00 00 00
36e9 00 00 00
36ec 00 00 00
36ef 00 00 00
36f2 00 00 00
36f5 00 00 00
36f8 00 00 00
36fb 00 00
                * LOAD ADDRESS FOR CODE (PG BDY)
                * ENTRY AFTER BOOT IS AT LOADADDR+256 (SECOND PAGE LOADED)
                *
                BHERE4          EQU          >*
                LOADADDR        EQU          $800+BHERE4
36fd 00                         DFB          0
36fe 36         GRSPG           DFB          <TRK0LDR                  ;CONTAINS PAGE#-1 OF TRK 0, SEC 1 LOAD ADDRESS
                * LAST LOGICAL BSECTOR TO READ STARTING AT $00
                BHERE5          EQU          >*
                BGRPGC          EQU          $800+BHERE5
36ff 09         GRPGC           DFB          <(ENDOFDOS-TRK0LDR-$100)
                ********************
                ;;;                PAGE
                DOSLODR         EQU          *
                ;;;                DO           >DOSLODR
                ;;;                ???                                    ;ERROR IF NOT ON PAGE BOUNDARY
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                REP          40
                * FAST BOOT AT 2:1 INTERLEAVE
                * FOR 16-SECTOR DISKETTES
                ;;;                REP          40
3700 8e e9 37                   STX          IBSLOT                    ; SET BOOT SLOT
3703 8e f7 37                   STX          IBPSLT                    ; SET PREVIOUS SLOT
3706 a9 01                      LDA          #1                        ; SET PREV DRIVE
3708 8d f8 37                   STA          IBPDRV
370b 8d ea 37                   STA          IBDRVN
                ;
370e ad e0 37                   LDA          NDPGS                     ; COPY NO PAGES TO GET
3711 8d e1 37                   STA          BRWCNT
3714 a9 02                      LDA          #2
3716 8d ec 37                   STA          IBTRK                     ; SET TRACK 0
3719 a9 04                      LDA          #4                        ;ENDING SECTOR OF DOS IMAGE
371b 8d ed 37                   STA          IBSECT                    ;TO IOB
371e ac e7 37                   LDY          ADOSLD+1                  ;END PAGE OF DOS IMAGE
3721 88                         DEY                                    ;IS ONE LESS THAN
3722 8c f1 37                   STY          IBBUFP+1                  ;START OF DOSLDR+BOOT
                ;
3725 a9 01                      LDA          #IBCRTS                   ; SET READ
3727 8d f4 37                   STA          IBCMD
                ;
372a 8a                         TXA                                    ; SET PREV TRACK = 0
372b 4a                         LSR          A
372c 4a                         LSR          A
372d 4a                         LSR          A
372e 4a                         LSR          A
372f aa                         TAX
3730 a9 00                      LDA          #0
3732 9d f8 04                   STA          $4F8,X
3735 9d 78 04                   STA          $478,X
3738 20 93 37                   JSR          BOOTIO                    ; GO READ DOS
                ;
                ;DOSINT - INITIALIZE DOS
                ;
                DOSINT          EQU          *
373b a2 ff                      LDX          #$FF
373d 9a                         TXS
373e 8e eb 37                   STX          IBVOL
3741 4c c8 3f                   JMP          RCPATCH
3744 20 89 fe   RCBACK          JSR          SETKBD
                ;
3747 4c 03 1b   DI3             JMP          DOSREL                    ; GO TO POST INIT ROUTINE
                ;;;                PAGE
                WBOOT           EQU          *
374a ad e7 37                   LDA          ADOSLD+1
374d 38                         SEC
374e ed f1 37                   SBC          IBBUFP+1
3751 8d e1 37                   STA          BRWCNT                    ;COMPUT PAGE COUNT
3754 ad e7 37                   LDA          ADOSLD+1
3757 8d f1 37                   STA          IBBUFP+1                  ;BUFFER=LAST PAGE OF RWTS
375a ce f1 37                   DEC          IBBUFP+1
375d a9 02                      LDA          #2                        ;ENDING TRACK
375f 8d ec 37                   STA          IBTRK
3762 a9 04                      LDA          #4
3764 8d ed 37                   STA          IBSECT                    ;ENDING SECTOR
3767 a9 02                      LDA          #2
3769 8d f4 37                   STA          IBCMD                     ;COMMAND = WRITE
376c 20 93 37                   JSR          BOOTIO                    ;WRITE DOS IMAGE TRK 2,SEC 4
                *   ;           BACKWARDS TO TRK 0,SEC C
376f ad e7 37                   LDA          ADOSLD+1
3772 8d fe 36                   STA          GRSPG                     ;BOOTSTRAP LOAD ADDRESS
3775 18                         CLC
3776 69 09                      ADC          #9
3778 8d f1 37                   STA          IBBUFP+1                  ;BUFFER ADDRESS OF END OF BOOT
377b a9 0a                      LDA          #10
377d 8d e1 37                   STA          BRWCNT                    ;SECTOR COUNT TO WRITE
3780 38                         SEC
3781 e9 01                      SBC          #1
3783 8d ff 36                   STA          GRPGC                     ;BOOT LAST SECTOR #
3786 8d ed 37                   STA          IBSECT                    ;START AT END OF RWTS&BOOT
3789 20 93 37                   JSR          BOOTIO                    ;AND WRITE DOWN TO ZERO
378c 60                         RTS
378d 00 00 00                   DS           6,0                       ;FILL WITH BRKS
3790 00 00 00
                ;;;                PAGE
                BOOTIO          EQU          *
3793 ad e5 37                   LDA          BAIOB+1
3796 ac e4 37                   LDY          BAIOB
3799 20 b5 37                   JSR          DISKIO
                ;
379c ac ed 37                   LDY          IBSECT                    ; GET SECTOR
379f 88                         DEY                                    ; DECREMENT TO NEXT
37a0 10 07                      BPL          BIO1                      ;AT END OF TRACK?
37a2 a0 0f                      LDY          #15                       ;SET TO SECTOR 15
37a4 ea                         NOP
37a5 ea                         NOP
37a6 ce ec 37                   DEC          IBTRK
37a9 8c ed 37   BIO1            STY          IBSECT                    ; SET NEXT SECTOR
                ;
37ac ce f1 37                   DEC          IBBUFP+1                  ; DECREMENT BUFFER POINTER
37af ce e1 37                   DEC          BRWCNT                    ; DECREMENT PAGE COUNTER
37b2 d0 df                      BNE          BOOTIO                    ; BR IF NOT DONE
37b4 60                         RTS
                ;
                ;;;                PAGE
37b5 08         DISKIO          PHP                                    ;SAVE INTERUPT STATUS
37b6 78                         SEI                                    ;INHIBIT INTERUPT WHILE
37b7 20 00 3d                   JSR          RWTS                      ; ACCESSING DISK
37ba b0 03                      BCS          DSKERR                    ;MUST PASS BACK CARRY FLAG & INTERUPT
37bc 28                         PLP
37bd 18                         CLC
37be 60                         RTS
37bf 28         DSKERR          PLP                                    ;CARRY SET MEANS ERROR
37c0 38                         SEC
37c1 60                         RTS
37c2 ad bc 35   DLDSUP          LDA          CCBBSA                    ;SET UP FOR DOS LOADER
37c5 8d f1 37                   STA          IBBUFP+1                  ;START ADDRESS
37c8 a9 00                      LDA          #0
37ca 8d f0 37                   STA          IBBUFP
37cd ad f9 35                   LDA          DCBVOL                    ;INVERT VOLUME NUMBER
37d0 49 ff                      EOR          #$FF
37d2 8d eb 37                   STA          IBVOL
37d5 60                         RTS
                ;
37d6 a9 00      CLRSEC          LDA          #0                        ;CLEAR SECTOR
37d8 a8                         TAY
37d9 91 42      CS1             STA          (ZPGFCB),Y
37db c8                         INY
37dc d0 fb                      BNE          CS1
37de 60                         RTS
37df 00                         BRK
                EC3             EQU          *
37e0 1b         NDPGS           DFB          <(TRK0LDR-BEGIN)            ;CALC #PAGES IN DOS WITHOUT RWTS
37e1 00         BRWCNT          DFB          0                         ;WRK CTR FOR BOOTIO
37e2 0a                         DFB          $0A
37e3 1b                         DFB          $1B
37e4 e8 37      BAIOB           DW           IOB
37e6 00 36      ADOSLD          DW           TRK0LDR
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;IOB - INPUT / OUTPUT CONTROL BLOCK
                ;THE IOB IS USED FOR THE INTERFACE
                ;BETWEEN DOS AND THE DISK I/O ROUTINES
                ;
                IOB             EQU          *
37e8 01         IBTYPE          DFB          1                         ; IOB TYPE CODE
37e9 60         IBSLOT          DFB          6*16                      ; CONTROLLER SLOT NO.
37ea 01         IBDRVN          DFB          1                         ; DRIVE NUMBER
37eb 00         IBVOL           DFB          $00                       ; VOLUME NUMBER
37ec 00         IBTRK           DFB          0                         ; TRACK NUMBER
37ed 00         IBSECT          DFB          0                         ; SECTOR NUMBER
37ee fb 37      IBDCTP          DW           DCT
37f0 00 00      IBBUFP          DW           0                         ; POINTER TO BUFFER
37f2 00 01      IBDLEN          DW           256                       ; DATA LENGTH
37f4 00         IBCMD           DFB          0                         ; COMMAND
                IBCNUL          EQU          0                         ; 0-NULL COMMAND
                IBCRTS          EQU          1                         ; 1-READ TRACK, SECTOR
                IBCWTS          EQU          2                         ; 2-WRITE TRACK, SECTOR
                IBFMT           EQU          4                         ; 4-FORMAT DISK
                IBBOOT          EQU          8                         ; 8-WRITE BOOT
37f5 00         IBSTAT          DFB          0                         ; STATUS
                IBRERR          EQU          $80                       ; READ ERR
                IBDERR          EQU          $40                       ; DRIVE ERR
                IBVMME          EQU          $20                       ; VOLUME MISMATCH
                IBWPER          EQU          $10                       ; WRITE PROTECT ERROR
37f6 00         IBSMOD          DFB          0                         ; STATUS MODIFIER BYTE
37f7 60         IBPSLT          DFB          6*16                      ; PREVIOUS SLOT
37f8 01         IBPDRV          DFB          1                         ; PREVIOUS DRIVE
37f9 00 00      IBSPAR          DS           2,0                       ; IOB SPARES
37fb 00 01 ef   DCT             DFB          0,1,$EF,$D8
37fe d8
37ff 00                         DS           1,0                       ;FILL IN 3700 PAGE
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;
                ;FILE DIRECTORY DEFINITION
                ;
                ;;;                DSECT
                DSECT	EQU	*	;;;
                	ORG	0	;;;
                FILDIR          EQU          *
                FDUCDE          DS           1                         ; FILE USE CODE
                FDLTRK          DS           1                         ; LINK TO NEXT DIR TRACK
                FDLSEC          DS           1                         ; LINT TO NEXT DIR SECTOR
                FDNSA           DS           1                         ; NO SECTORS ALLOCATED
                FDLSDL          DS           1                         ; LAST SECTOR DATA LENGTH
                FDFRS           DS           2                         ; 1ST RELATIVE SECTOR IN THIS DIR
                FDSPAR          DS           5                         ; SPARES
                ;
                FDENT           DS           1                         ; START OF FILE ENTRIES (122)
                FDTRK           EQU          0                         ; TRACK
                FDSEC           EQU          1                         ; SECTOR
                ;
                FDLAST          EQU          FILDIR+256
                ;;;                DEND
                	ORG	DSECT	;;;

                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR CORE ROUTINES'
                ***************************
                *                         *
                *         DISC-II         *
                *     16-SECTOR FORMAT    *
                *      READ AND WRITE     *
                *       SUBROUTINES       *
                *                         *
                ***************************
                *                         *
                *                         *
                *     COPYRIGHT 1979      *
                *   APPLE COMPUTER INC.   *
                *                         *
                *   ALL RIGHTS RESERVED   *
                *                         *
                ***************************
                *                         *
                *      MAR 18, 1979       *
                *          WOZ            *
                *                         *
                ***************************
                ASC1            EQU          *                         ;TELL RELOCATOR WHERE CORE STARTS
                ;;;                PAGE
                ***************************
                *                         *
                *     CRITICAL TIMING     *
                *   REQUIRES PAGE BOUND   *
                *   CONSIDERATIONS FOR    *
                *      CODE AND DATA      *
                *                         *
                *     -----CODE-----      *
                *                         *
                *   VIRTUALLY THE ENTIRE  *
                *    'WRITE16' ROUTINE    *
                *      MUST NOT CROSS     *
                *     PAGE BOUNDARIES.    *
                *                         *
                *  THE WRITE16, READ16    *
                *  AND RDADR16 SUBRS      *
                *  WHICH MUST NOT CROSS   *
                *  PAGE BOUNDARIES ARE    *
                *  NOTED IN COMMENTS.     *
                *                         *
                *     -----DATA-----      *
                *                         *
                *  NBUF1 AND NBUF2 ARE    *
                *  256-BYTE AND 86-BYTE   *
                *  NIBL BUFFERS IN RAM.   *
                *  BOTH MUST BEGIN ON     *
                *  PAGE BOUNDARIES.       *
                *                         *
                *  NIBLIZING TABLE 'NIBL' *
                *  (64 BYTES) MAPS 6-BIT  *
                *  NIBLS INTO VALID 7-BIT *
                *  NIBLS.  THIS TABLE     *
                *  MUST NOT CROSS A PAGE  *
                *  BOUNDARY.              *
                *                         *
                *  DENIBLIZING TABLE      *
                *  'DNIBL' MAPS 7-BIT     *
                *  NIBLS INTO 6-BIT       *
                *  NIBLS.  IT MUST BEGIN  *
                *  ON A PAGE BOUNDARY,    *
                *  BUT ONLY DNIBL,$96 TO  *
                *  DNIBL,$FF ARE USED.    *
                *                         *
                ***************************
                ;;;                PAGE
                ***************************
                *                         *
                *         EQUATES         *
                *                         *
                ***************************
                *                         *
                *    ----PRENIBL16----    *
                *      AND POSTNB16       *
                *   (16-SECTOR FORMAT)    *
                *                         *
                ***************************
                BUF             EQU          $3E                       ;TWO BYTE POINTER.
                *
                * POINTS TO 256-BYTE
                * USER BUFFER ANYWHERE
                * IN MEMORY.  PRENIBL16
                * CONVERTS USER DATA
                * (IN BUF) INTO 6-BIT
                * NIBLS 00ABCDEF IN
                * NBUF1 AND NBUF2 PRIOR
                * TO 'WRITE'.  POSTNBL16
                * CONVERTS 6-BIT NIBLS
                * 00ABCDEF BACK TO USER
                * DATA IN BUF AFTER 'READ'.
                *
                T0              EQU          $26                       ;TEMP FOR POSTNBL16.
                ************************
                *                      *
                *    ----RDADR16----   *
                *                      *
                ************************
                COUNT           EQU          $26                       ;'MUST FIND' COUNT.
                LAST            EQU          $26                       ;'ODD BIT' NIBLS.
                CSUM            EQU          $27                       ;CHECKSUM BYTE.
                CSSTV           EQU          $2C                       ;FOUR BYTES,
                *       CHECKSUM, SECTOR, TRACK, AND VOLUME.
                *
                ************************
                *                      *
                *    ---WRITE16---     *
                *                      *
                *  USES NBUF1, NBUF2,  *
                *  AND 64-BYTE TABLE   *
                *       'NIBL'.        *
                *                      *
                ************************
                WTEMP           EQU          $26                       ;TEMP FOR DATA AT NBUF2,0.
                SLOTZ           EQU          $27                       ;SLOTNUM IN Z-PAG LOC.
                SLOTABS         EQU          $678                      ;SLOTNUM IN NON-ZPAG LOC.
                *
                ************************
                *                      *
                *     ----READ16---    *
                *  (16-SECTOR FORMAT)  *
                *                      *
                *   USES NBUF1,NBUF2.  *
                *  USES LAST 106 BYTES *
                *  OF A DATA PAGE FOR  *
                *  SIGNIFICANT BYTES   *
                *  OF DNIBL16 TABLE.   *
                *                      *
                ************************
                IDX             EQU          $26                       ;INDEX INTO (BUF).
                *
                ************************
                *                      *
                *    ---- SEEK ----    *
                *                      *
                ************************
                TRKCNT          EQU          $26                       ;HALFTRKS MOVED COUNT.
                PRIOR           EQU          $27                       ;PRIOR HALFTRACK.
                TRKN            EQU          $2A                       ;DESIRED TRACK.
                SLOTTEMP        EQU          $2B                       ;SLOT NUM TIMES $10.
                CURTRK          EQU          $478                      ;CURRENT TRACK ON ENTRY.
                *
                ************************
                *                      *
                *   ---- MSWAIT ----   *
                *                      *
                ************************
                MONTIMEL        EQU          $46                       ;MOTOR-ON TIME
                MONTIMEH        EQU          $47                       ;COUNTERS.
                *
                ************************
                *                      *
                *   ---- WRADR16 ----  *
                *                      *
                ************************
                AA              EQU          $3E                       ;TIMING CONSTANT
                NSECT           EQU          $3F                       ;SECTOR NUMBER
                NVOL            EQU          $41                       ;VOLUME NUMBER
                TRK             EQU          $44                       ;TRACK NUMBER
                *
                ************************
                *                      *
                *    DEVICE ADDRESS    *
                *     ASSIGNMENTS      *
                *                      *
                ************************
                PHASEOFF        EQU          $C080                     ;STEPPER PHASE OFF.
                PHASEON         EQU          $C081                     ;STEPPER PHASE ON.
                Q6L             EQU          $C08C                     ;Q7L,Q6L=READ
                Q6H             EQU          $C08D                     ;Q7L,Q6H=SENSE WPROT
                Q7L             EQU          $C08E                     ;Q7H,Q6L=WRITE
                Q7H             EQU          $C08F                     ;Q7H,Q6H=WRITE STORE

                ; #   END OF FILE:  COREQUS
                ; #   LINES      :  174
                ; #   CHARACTERS :  5595
                ; #   Formatter  :  Assembly Language Reformatter 1.0.2 (07 January 1998)
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; #   PROJECT  :  APPLE ][ DOS 3.3 C SOURCE CODE LISTING -- (C) APPLE COMPUTER INC. JULY 1983
                ; #   FILE NAME:  PRENIBL

                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR PRENIBLIZE'
                ****************************
                *                          *
                *    PRENIBLIZE SUBR       *
                *   (16-SECTOR FORMAT)     *
                *                          *
                ****************************
                *                          *
                *  CONVERTS 256 BYTES OF   *
                *  USER DATA IN (BUF),0    *
                *  TO (BUF),255 INTO 342   *
                *  6-BIT NIBLS (00ABCDEF)  *
                *  IN NBUF1 AND NBUF2.     *
                *                          *
                *    ---- ON ENTRY ----    *
                *                          *
                *  BUF IS 2-BYTE POINTER   *
                *    TO 256 BYTES OF USER  *
                *    DATA.                 *
                *                          *
                *    ---- ON EXIT -----    *
                *                          *
                *  A-REG UNCERTAIN.        *
                *  X-REG HOLDS $FF.        *
                *  Y-REG HOLDS $FF.        *
                *  CARRY SET.              *
                *                          *
                *  NBUF1 AND NBUF2 CONTAIN *
                *    6-BIT NIBLS OF FORM   *
                *    00ABCDEF.             *
                *                          *
                ****************************
3800 a2 00      PRENIB16        LDX          #$0                       ;START NBUF2 INDEX. CHANGED BY WOZ
3802 a0 02                      LDY          #2                        ;START USER BUF INDEX. CHANGED BY WOZ.
3804 88         PRENIB1         DEY                                    ;NEXT USER BYTE.
3805 b1 3e                      LDA          (BUF),Y
3807 4a                         LSR          A                         ;SHIFT TWO BITS OF
3808 3e 00 3c                   ROL          NBUF2,X                   ;CURRENT USER BYTE
380b 4a                         LSR          A                         ;INTO CURRENT NBUF2
380c 3e 00 3c                   ROL          NBUF2,X                   ;BYTE.
380f 99 00 3b                   STA          NBUF1,Y                   ;(6 BITS LEFT).
3812 e8                         INX                                    ;FROM 0 TO $55.
3813 e0 56                      CPX          #$56
3815 90 ed                      BCC          PRENIB1                   ;BR IF NO WRAPAROUND.
3817 a2 00                      LDX          #0                        ;RESET NBUF2 INDEX.
3819 98                         TYA                                    ;USER BUF INDEX.
381a d0 e8                      BNE          PRENIB1                   ;(DONE IF ZERO)
381c a2 55                      LDX          #$55                      ;NBUF2 IDX $55 TO 0.
381e bd 00 3c   PRENIB2         LDA          NBUF2,X
3821 29 3f                      AND          #$3F                      ;STRIP EACH BYTE
3823 9d 00 3c                   STA          NBUF2,X                   ;OF NBUF2 TO 6 BITS.
3826 ca                         DEX
3827 10 f5                      BPL          PRENIB2                   ;LOOP UNTIL X NEG.
3829 60                         RTS                                    ;RETURN.
                
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; #   END OF FILE:  PRENIBL
                ; #   LINES      :  54
                ; #   CHARACTERS :  2360
                ; #   Formatter  :  Assembly Language Reformatter 1.0.2 (07 January 1998)
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; #   PROJECT  :  APPLE ][ DOS 3.3 C SOURCE CODE LISTING -- (C) APPLE COMPUTER INC. JULY 1983
                ; #   FILE NAME:  WRITRTN

                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR WRITE'
                ************************
                *                      *
                *      WRITE SUBR      *
                *  (16-SECTOR FORMAT)  *
                *                      *
                ************************
                *                      *
                *   WRITES DATA FROM   *
                *    NBUF1 AND NBUF2   *
                *   CONVERTING 6-BIT   *
                *    TO 7-BIT NIBLS    *
                *   VIA 'NIBL' TABLE.  *
                *                      *
                *  FIRST NBUF2,        *
                *      HIGH TO LOW.    *
                *  THEN NBUF1,         *
                *      LOW TO HIGH.    *
                *                      *
                *  ---- ON ENTRY ----  *
                *                      *
                *   X-REG: SLOTNUM     *
                *        TIMES $10.    *
                *                      *
                *   NBUF1 AND NBUF2    *
                *    HOLD NIBLS FROM   *
                *    PRENIBL SUBR.     *
                *    (00ABCDEF)        *
                *                      *
                *  ---- ON EXIT -----  *
                *                      *
                *  CARRY SET IF ERROR. *
                *   (W PROT VIOLATION) *
                *                      *
                *  IF NO ERROR:        *
                *                      *
                *    A-REG UNCERTAIN.  *
                *    X-REG UNCHANGED.  *
                *    Y-REG HOLDS $00.  *
                *    CARRY CLEAR.      *
                *                      *
                *    SLOTABS, SLOTZ,   *
                *     AND WTEMP USED.  *
                *                      *
                *  ---- ASSUMES ----   *
                *                      *
                *  1 USEC CYCLE TIME   *
                *                      *
                ************************
382a 38         WRITE16         SEC                                    ;ANTICIPATE WPROT ERR.
382b 86 27                      STX          SLOTZ                     ;FOR ZERO PAGE ACCESS.
382d 8e 78 06                   STX          SLOTABS                   ;FOR NON-ZERO PAGE.
3830 bd 8d c0                   LDA          Q6H,X
3833 bd 8e c0                   LDA          Q7L,X                     ;SENSE WPROT FLAG.
3836 30 7c                      BMI          WEXIT                     ;IF HIGH, THEN ERR.
3838 ad 00 3c                   LDA          NBUF2
383b 85 26                      STA          WTEMP                     ;FOR ZERO-PAGE ACCESS.
383d a9 ff                      LDA          #$FF                      ;SYNC DATA.
383f 9d 8f c0                   STA          Q7H,X                     ;(5)  WRITE 1ST NIBL.
3842 1d 8c c0                   ORA          Q6L,X                     ;(4)
3845 48                         PHA                                    ;(3)
3846 68                         PLA                                    ;(4)  CRITICAL TIMING!
3847 ea                         NOP                                    ;(2)
3848 a0 04                      LDY          #4                        ;(2)  FOR 5 NIBLS.
384a 48         WSYNC           PHA                                    ;(3)  EXACT TIMING.
384b 68                         PLA                                    ;(4)  EXACT TIMING.
384c 20 b9 38                   JSR          WNIBL7                    ;(13,9,6)  WRITE SYNC.
384f 88                         DEY                                    ;(2)
3850 d0 f8                      BNE          WSYNC                     ;(2*)  MUST NOT CROSS PAGE!
3852 a9 d5                      LDA          #$D5                      ;(2)  1ST DATA MARK.
3854 20 b8 38                   JSR          WNIBL9                    ;(15,9,6)
3857 a9 aa                      LDA          #$AA                      ;(2)  2ND DATA MARK.
3859 20 b8 38                   JSR          WNIBL9                    ;(15,9,6)
385c a9 ad                      LDA          #$AD                      ;(2)  3RD DATA MARK.
385e 20 b8 38                   JSR          WNIBL9                    ;(15,9,6)
3861 98                         TYA                                    ;(2)  CLEAR CHKSUM.
3862 a0 56                      LDY          #$56                      ;(2)  NBUF2 INDEX.
3864 d0 03                      BNE          WDATA1                    ;(3)  ALWAYS.  NO PAGE CROSS!!
3866 b9 00 3c   WDATA0          LDA          NBUF2,Y                   ;(4)  PRIOR 6-BIT NIBL.
3869 59 ff 3b   WDATA1          EOR          NBUF2-1,Y                 ;(5)  XOR WITH CURRENT.
                *   (NBUF2 MUST BE ON PAGE BOUNDARY FOR TIMING!!)
386c aa                         TAX                                    ;(2)  INDEX TO 7-BIT NIBL.
386d bd 29 3a                   LDA          NIBL,X                    ;(4)  MUST NOT CROSS PAGE!
3870 a6 27                      LDX          SLOTZ                     ;(3)  CRITICAL TIMING!
3872 9d 8d c0                   STA          Q6H,X                     ;(5)  WRITE NIBL.
3875 bd 8c c0                   LDA          Q6L,X                     ;(4)
3878 88                         DEY                                    ;(2)  NEXT NIBL.
3879 d0 eb                      BNE          WDATA0                    ;(2*)  MUST NOT CROSS PAGE!
387b a5 26                      LDA          WTEMP                     ;(3)  PRIOR NIBL FROM BUF6.
387d ea                         NOP                                    ;(2)  CRITICAL TIMING.
387e 59 00 3b   WDATA2          EOR          NBUF1,Y                   ;(4)  XOR NBUF1 NIBL.
3881 aa                         TAX                                    ;(2)  INDEX TO 7-BIT NIBL.
3882 bd 29 3a                   LDA          NIBL,X                    ;(4)
3885 ae 78 06                   LDX          SLOTABS                   ;(4)  TIMING CRITICAL.
3888 9d 8d c0                   STA          Q6H,X                     ;(5)  WRITE NIBL.
388b bd 8c c0                   LDA          Q6L,X                     ;(4)
388e b9 00 3b                   LDA          NBUF1,Y                   ;(4)  PRIOR 6-BIT NIBL.
3891 c8                         INY                                    ;(2)  NEXT NBUF1 NIBL.
3892 d0 ea                      BNE          WDATA2                    ;(2*)  MUST NOT CROSS PAGE!
3894 aa                         TAX                                    ;(2)  LAST NIBL AS CHKSUM.
3895 bd 29 3a                   LDA          NIBL,X                    ;(4)  INDEX TO 7-BIT NIBL.
3898 a6 27                      LDX          SLOTZ                     ;(3)
389a 20 bb 38                   JSR          WNIBL                     ;(6,9,6)  WRITE CHKSUM.
389d a9 de                      LDA          #$DE                      ;(2)  DM4, BIT SLIP MARK.
389f 20 b8 38                   JSR          WNIBL9                    ;(15,9,6)    WRITE IT.
38a2 a9 aa                      LDA          #$AA                      ;(2)  DM5, BIT SLIP MARK.
38a4 20 b8 38                   JSR          WNIBL9                    ;(15,9,6)    WRITE IT.
38a7 a9 eb                      LDA          #$EB                      ;(2)  DM6, BIT SLIP MARK.
38a9 20 b8 38                   JSR          WNIBL9                    ;(15,9,6)    WRITE IT.
38ac a9 ff                      LDA          #$FF                      ;(2) TURN-OFF BYTE.
38ae 20 b8 38                   JSR          WNIBL9                    ;(15,9,9)  WRITE IT.
38b1 bd 8e c0                   LDA          Q7L,X                     ;OUT OF WRITE MODE.
38b4 bd 8c c0   WEXIT           LDA          Q6L,X                     ;TO READ MODE.
38b7 60                         RTS                                    ;RETURN FROM WRITE.
                *****************************
                *                           *
                *   7-BIT NIBL WRITE SUBRS  *
                *                           *
                *   A-REG OR'D PRIOR EXIT   *
                *       CARRY CLEARED       *
                *                           *
                *****************************
38b8 18         WNIBL9          CLC                                    ;(2)  9 CYCLES, THEN WRITE.
38b9 48         WNIBL7          PHA                                    ;(3)  7 CYCLES, THEN WRITE.
38ba 68                         PLA                                    ;(4)
38bb 9d 8d c0   WNIBL           STA          Q6H,X                     ;(5)  NIBL WRITE SUB.
38be 1d 8c c0                   ORA          Q6L,X                     ;(4)  CLOBBERS ACC, NOT CARRY.
38c1 60                         RTS
                
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; #   END OF FILE:  WRITRTN
                ; #   LINES      :  128
                ; #   CHARACTERS :  6272
                ; #   Formatter  :  Assembly Language Reformatter 1.0.2 (07 January 1998)
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; #   PROJECT  :  APPLE ][ DOS 3.3 C SOURCE CODE LISTING -- (C) APPLE COMPUTER INC. JULY 1983
                ; #   FILE NAME:  POSTNRD
                ; ####################################################################################################
                
                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR POSTNIBLIZE'
                ***************************
                *                         *
                *    POSTNIBLIZE SUBR     *
                *    16-SECTOR FORMAT     *
                *                         *
                ***************************
                *                         *
                *  CONVERTS 6-BIT NIBLS   *
                *  OF FORM 00ABCDEF IN    *
                *  NBUF1 AND NBUF2 INTO   *
                *  256 BYTES OF USER      *
                *  DATA IN BUF.           *
                *                         *
                *   ---- ON ENTRY ----    *
                *                         *
                *  X-REG: HOLDS SLOTNUM   *
                *            TIMES $10.   *
                *                         *
                *  BUF IS 2-BYTE POINTER  *
                *    TO 256 BYTES OF USER *
                *    DATA TO BE CONVERTED *
                *    TO 6-BIT NIBLS IN    *
                *    NBUF1 AND NBUF2      *
                *    PRIOR TO WRITE.      *
                *                         *
                *  T0 CONTAINS BYTE COUNT *
                *    CODE 0 = 256 BYTES   *
                *    CODE 1 =   1 BYTE    *
                *    CODE 2 =   2 BYTER   *
                *                         *
                *    CODE 255=255 BYTES   *
                *                         *
                *   ---- ON EXIT -----    *
                *                         *
                *  A-REG UNCERTAIN.       *
                *  Y-REG SAME AS T0.      *
                *  X-REG UNCERTAIN.       *
                *  CARRY SET.             *
                *                         *
                *  6-BIT NIBLS OF FORM    *
                *    00ABCDEF IN NBUF1    *
                *    AND NBUF2.           *
                *      (342 NIBLS)        *
                ***************************
38c2 a0 00      POSTNB16        LDY          #0                        ;USER DATA BUF IDX.
38c4 a2 56      POST1           LDX          #$56                      ;INIT NBUF2 INDEX.
38c6 ca         POST2           DEX                                    ;NBUF IDX $55 TO $0.
38c7 30 fb                      BMI          POST1                     ;WRAPAROUND IF NEG.
38c9 b9 00 3b                   LDA          NBUF1,Y
38cc 5e 00 3c                   LSR          NBUF2,X                   ;SHIFT 2 BITS FROM
38cf 2a                         ROL          A                         ;CURRENT NBUF2 NIBL
38d0 5e 00 3c                   LSR          NBUF2,X                   ;INTO CURRENT NBUF1
38d3 2a                         ROL          A                         ;NIBL.
38d4 91 3e                      STA          (BUF),Y                   ;BYTE OF USER DATA.
38d6 c8                         INY                                    ;NEXT USER BYTE.
38d7 c4 26                      CPY          T0                        ;DONE IF EQUAL T0.
38d9 d0 eb                      BNE          POST2
38db 60                         RTS                                    ;RETURN.
                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR READ'
                **************************
                *                        *
                *     READ SUBROUTINE    *
                *   (16-SECTOR FORMAT)   *
                *                        *
                **************************
                *                        *
                *    READS 6-BIT NIBLS   *
                *     (00ABCDEF) INTO    *
                *     NBUF1 AND NBUF2    *
                *    CONVERTING 7-BIT    *
                *     NIBLS TO 6-BIT     *
                *    VIA 'DNIBL' TABLE   *
                *                        *
                *  FIRST READS NBUF2     *
                *          HIGH TO LOW,  *
                *  THEN READS NBUF1      *
                *          LOW TO HIGH.  *
                *                        *
                *   ---- ON ENTRY ----   *
                *                        *
                *  X-REG: SLOTNUM        *
                *         TIMES $10.     *
                *                        *
                *  READ MODE (Q6L, Q7L)  *
                *                        *
                *   ---- ON EXIT -----   *
                *                        *
                *  CARRY SET IF ERROR.   *
                *                        *
                *  IF NO ERROR:          *
                *     A-REG HOLDS $AA.   *
                *     X-REG UNCHANGED.   *
                *     Y-REG HOLDS $00.   *
                *     CARRY CLEAR.       *
                *                        *
                *     NBUF1 AND NBUF2    *
                *       HOLD 6-BIT NIBLS *
                *       (00ABCDEF)       *
                *                        *
                *     USES TEMP 'IDX'.   *
                *                        *
                *   ---- CAUTION -----   *
                *                        *
                *        OBSERVE         *
                *    'NO PAGE CROSS'     *
                *      WARNINGS ON       *
                *    SOME BRANCHES!!     *
                *                        *
                *   ---- ASSUMES ----    *
                *                        *
                *   1 USEC CYCLE TIME    *
                *                        *
                **************************
38dc a0 20      READ16          LDY          #$20                      ;'MUST FIND' COUNT.
38de 88         RSYNC           DEY                                    ;IF CAN'T FIND MARKS
38df f0 61                      BEQ          RDERR                     ;THEN EXIT WITH CARRY SET.
38e1 bd 8c c0   READ1           LDA          Q6L,X                     ;READ NIBL.
38e4 10 fb                      BPL          READ1                     ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
38e6 49 d5      RSYNC1          EOR          #$D5                      ;DATA MARK 1?
38e8 d0 f4                      BNE          RSYNC                     ;LOOP IF NOT.
38ea ea                         NOP                                    ;DELAY BETWEEN NIBLS.
38eb bd 8c c0   READ2           LDA          Q6L,X
38ee 10 fb                      BPL          READ2                     ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
38f0 c9 aa                      CMP          #$AA                      ;DATA MARK 2?
38f2 d0 f2                      BNE          RSYNC1                    ;(IF NOT, IS IT DM1?)
38f4 a0 56                      LDY          #$56                      ;INIT NBUF2 INDEX.
                *              (ADDED NIBL DELAY)
38f6 bd 8c c0   READ3           LDA          Q6L,X
38f9 10 fb                      BPL          READ3                     ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
38fb c9 ad                      CMP          #$AD                      ;DATA MARK 3?
38fd d0 e7                      BNE          RSYNC1                    ;(IF NOT, IS IT DM1?)
                *         (CARRY SET IF DM3!)
38ff a9 00                      LDA          #$00                      ;INIT CHECKSUM.
3901 88         RDATA1          DEY
3902 84 26                      STY          IDX
3904 bc 8c c0   READ4           LDY          Q6L,X
3907 10 fb                      BPL          READ4                     ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
3909 59 00 3a                   EOR          DNIBL,Y                   ;XOR 6-BIT NIBL.
390c a4 26                      LDY          IDX
390e 99 00 3c                   STA          NBUF2,Y                   ;STORE IN NBUF2 PAGE.
3911 d0 ee                      BNE          RDATA1                    ;TAKEN IF Y-REG NONZERO.
3913 84 26      RDATA2          STY          IDX
3915 bc 8c c0   READ5           LDY          Q6L,X
3918 10 fb                      BPL          READ5                     ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
391a 59 00 3a                   EOR          DNIBL,Y                   ;XOR 6-BIT NIBL.
391d a4 26                      LDY          IDX
391f 99 00 3b                   STA          NBUF1,Y                   ;STORE IN NBUF1 PAGE.
3922 c8                         INY
3923 d0 ee                      BNE          RDATA2
3925 bc 8c c0   READ6           LDY          Q6L,X                     ;READ 7-BIT CSUM NIBL.
3928 10 fb                      BPL          READ6                     ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
392a d9 00 3a                   CMP          DNIBL,Y                   ;IF LAST NBUF1 NIBL NOT
392d d0 13                      BNE          RDERR                     ;EQUAL CHKSUM NIBL THEN ERR.
392f bd 8c c0   READ7           LDA          Q6L,X
3932 10 fb                      BPL          READ7                     ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
3934 c9 de                      CMP          #$DE                      ;FIRST BIT SLIP MARK?
3936 d0 0a                      BNE          RDERR                     ;(ERR IF NOT)
3938 ea                         NOP                                    ;DELAY BETWEEN NIBLS.
3939 bd 8c c0   READ8           LDA          Q6L,X
393c 10 fb                      BPL          READ8                     ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
393e c9 aa                      CMP          #$AA                      ;SECOND BIT SLIP MARK?
3940 f0 5c                      BEQ          RDEXIT                    ;(DONE IF IT IS)
3942 38         RDERR           SEC                                    ;INDICATE 'ERROR EXIT'.
3943 60                         RTS                                    ;RETURN FROM READ16 OR RDADR16.

                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR READ ADDRESS'
                ****************************
                *                          *
                *    READ ADDRESS FIELD    *
                *        SUBROUTINE        *
                *    (16-SECTOR FORMAT)    *
                *                          *
                ****************************
                *                          *
                *    READS VOLUME, TRACK   *
                *        AND SECTOR        *
                *                          *
                *   ---- ON ENTRY ----     *
                *                          *
                *  XREG: SLOTNUM TIMES $10 *
                *                          *
                *  READ MODE (Q6L, Q7L)    *
                *                          *
                *   ---- ON EXIT -----     *
                *                          *
                *  CARRY SET IF ERROR.     *
                *                          *
                *  IF NO ERROR:            *
                *    A-REG HOLDS $AA.      *
                *    Y-REG HOLDS $00.      *
                *    X-REG UNCHANGED.      *
                *    CARRY CLEAR.          *
                *                          *
                *    CSSTV HOLDS CHKSUM,   *
                *      SECTOR, TRACK, AND  *
                *      VOLUME READ.        *
                *                          *
                *    USES TEMPS COUNT,     *
                *      LAST, CSUM, AND     *
                *      4 BYTES AT CSSTV.   *
                *                          *
                *    ---- EXPECTS ----     *
                *                          *
                *   ORIGINAL 10-SECTOR     *
                *  NORMAL DENSITY NIBLS    *
                *   (4-BIT), ODD BITS,     *
                *   THEN EVEN.             *
                *                          *
                *    ---- CAUTION ----     *
                *                          *
                *         OBSERVE          *
                *    'NO PAGE CROSS'       *
                *      WARNINGS ON         *
                *    SOME BRANCHES!!       *
                *                          *
                *    ---- ASSUMES ----     *
                *                          *
                *    1 USEC CYCLE TIME     *
                *                          *
                ****************************
3944 a0 fc      RDADR16         LDY          #$FC
3946 84 26                      STY          COUNT                     ;'MUST FIND' COUNT.
3948 c8         RDASYN          INY
3949 d0 04                      BNE          RDA1                      ;LOW ORDER OF COUNT.
394b e6 26                      INC          COUNT                     ;(2K NIBLS TO FIND
394d f0 f3                      BEQ          RDERR                     ;ADR MARK, ELSE ERR)
394f bd 8c c0   RDA1            LDA          Q6L,X                     ;READ NIBL.
3952 10 fb                      BPL          RDA1                      ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
3954 c9 d5      RDASN1          CMP          #$D5                      ;ADR MARK 1?
3956 d0 f0                      BNE          RDASYN                    ;(LOOP IF NOT)
3958 ea                         NOP                                    ;ADDED NIBL DELAY.
3959 bd 8c c0   RDA2            LDA          Q6L,X
395c 10 fb                      BPL          RDA2                      ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
395e c9 aa                      CMP          #$AA                      ;ADR MARK 2?
3960 d0 f2                      BNE          RDASN1                    ;(IF NOT, IS IT AM1?)
3962 a0 03                      LDY          #$3                       ;INDEX FOR 4-BYTE READ.
                *            (ADDED NIBL DELAY)
3964 bd 8c c0   RDA3            LDA          Q6L,X
3967 10 fb                      BPL          RDA3                      ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
3969 c9 96                      CMP          #$96                      ;ADR MARK 3?
396b d0 e7                      BNE          RDASN1                    ;(IF NOT, IS IT AM1?)
                *        (LEAVES CARRY SET!)
396d a9 00                      LDA          #$0                       ;INIT CHECKSUM.
396f 85 27      RDAFLD          STA          CSUM
3971 bd 8c c0   RDA4            LDA          Q6L,X                     ;READ 'ODD BIT' NIBL.
3974 10 fb                      BPL          RDA4                      ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
3976 2a                         ROL          A                         ;ALIGN ODD BITS, '1' INTO LSB.
3977 85 26                      STA          LAST                      ;(SAVE THEM)
3979 bd 8c c0   RDA5            LDA          Q6L,X                     ;READ 'EVEN BIT' NIBL.
397c 10 fb                      BPL          RDA5                      ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
397e 25 26                      AND          LAST                      ;MERGE ODD AND EVEN BITS.
3980 99 2c 00                   STA          CSSTV,Y                   ;STORE DATA BYTE.
3983 45 27                      EOR          CSUM                      ;XOR CHECKSUM.
3985 88                         DEY
3986 10 e7                      BPL          RDAFLD                    ;LOOP ON 4 DATA BYTES.
3988 a8                         TAY                                    ;IF FINAL CHECKSUM
3989 d0 b7                      BNE          RDERR                     ;NONZERO, THEN ERROR.
398b bd 8c c0   RDA6            LDA          Q6L,X                     ;FIRST BIT-SLIP NIBL.
398e 10 fb                      BPL          RDA6                      ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
3990 c9 de                      CMP          #$DE
3992 d0 ae                      BNE          RDERR                     ;ERROR IF NONMATCH.
3994 ea                         NOP                                    ;DELAY BETWEEN NIBLS.
3995 bd 8c c0   RDA7            LDA          Q6L,X                     ;SECOND BIT-SLIP NIBL.
3998 10 fb                      BPL          RDA7                      ;*** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
399a c9 aa                      CMP          #$AA
399c d0 a4                      BNE          RDERR                     ;ERROR IF NONMATCH.
399e 18         RDEXIT          CLC                                    ;CLEAR CARRY ON
399f 60                         RTS                                    ;NORMAL READ EXITS.
                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR SEEK'
                **************************
                *                        *
                *  FAST SEEK SUBROUTINE  *
                *                        *
                **************************
                *                        *
                *   ---- ON ENTRY ----   *
                *                        *
                *  X-REG HOLDS SLOTNUM   *
                *         TIMES $10.     *
                *                        *
                *  A-REG HOLDS DESIRED   *
                *         HALFTRACK.     *
                *         (SINGLE PHASE) *
                *                        *
                *  CURTRK HOLDS CURRENT  *
                *          HALFTRACK.    *
                *                        *
                *   ---- ON EXIT -----   *
                *                        *
                *  A-REG UNCERTAIN.      *
                *  Y-REG UNCERTAIN.      *
                *  X-REG UNDISTURBED.    *
                *                        *
                *  CURTRK AND TRKN HOLD  *
                *      FINAL HALFTRACK.  *
                *                        *
                *  PRIOR HOLDS PRIOR     *
                *    HALFTRACK IF SEEK   *
                *    WAS REQUIRED.       *
                *                        *
                *  MONTIMEL AND MONTIMEH *
                *    ARE INCREMENTED BY  *
                *    THE NUMBER OF       *
                *    100 USEC QUANTUMS   *
                *    REQUIRED BY SEEK    *
                *    FOR MOTOR ON TIME   *
                *    OVERLAP.            *
                *                        *
                * --- VARIABLES USED --- *
                *                        *
                *  CURTRK, TRKN, COUNT,  *
                *    PRIOR, SLOTTEMP     *
                *    MONTIMEL, MONTIMEH  *
                *                        *
                **************************
39a0 86 2b      SEEK            STX          SLOTTEMP                  ;SAVE X-REG
39a2 85 2a                      STA          TRKN                      ;SAVE TARGET TRACK
39a4 cd 78 04                   CMP          CURTRK                    ;ON DESIRED TRACK?
39a7 f0 53                      BEQ          SEEKRTS                   ;YES, RETURN
39a9 a9 00                      LDA          #$0
39ab 85 26                      STA          TRKCNT                    ;HALFTRACK COUNT.
39ad ad 78 04   SEEK2           LDA          CURTRK                    ;SAVE CURTRK FOR
39b0 85 27                      STA          PRIOR                     ; DELAYED TURNOFF.
39b2 38                         SEC
39b3 e5 2a                      SBC          TRKN                      ;DELTA-TRACKS.
39b5 f0 33                      BEQ          SEEKEND                   ;BR IF CURTRK=DESTINATION
39b7 b0 07                      BCS          OUT                       ;(MOVE OUT, NOT IN)
39b9 49 ff                      EOR          #$FF                      ;CALC TRKS TO GO.
39bb ee 78 04                   INC          CURTRK                    ;INCR CURRENT TRACK (IN).
39be 90 05                      BCC          MINTST                    ;(ALWAYS TAKEN)
39c0 69 fe      OUT             ADC          #$FE                      ;CALC TRKS TO GO.
39c2 ce 78 04                   DEC          CURTRK                    ;DECR CURRENT TRACK (OUT).
39c5 c5 26      MINTST          CMP          TRKCNT
39c7 90 02                      BCC          MAXTST                    ;AND 'TRKS MOVED'.
39c9 a5 26                      LDA          TRKCNT
39cb c9 0c      MAXTST          CMP          #$C
39cd b0 01                      BCS          STEP2                     ;IF TRKCNT>$B LEAVE Y ALONE (Y=$B).
39cf a8         STEP            TAY                                    ;ELSE SET ACCELERATION INDEX IN Y
                STEP2           EQU          *
39d0 38                         SEC                                    ;CARRY SET=PHASE ON
39d1 20 ee 39                   JSR          SETPHASE                  ;PHASE ON
39d4 b9 11 3a                   LDA          ONTABLE,Y                 ;FOR 'ONTIME'.
39d7 20 00 3a                   JSR          MSWAIT                    ;(100 USEC INTERVALS)
                *
39da a5 27                      LDA          PRIOR
39dc 18                         CLC                                    ;CARRY CLEAR=PHASE OFF
39dd 20 f1 39                   JSR          CLRPHASE                  ;PHASE OFF
39e0 b9 1d 3a                   LDA          OFFTABLE,Y                ;THEN WAIT 'OFFTIME'.
39e3 20 00 3a                   JSR          MSWAIT                    ;(100 USEC INTERVALS)
39e6 e6 26                      INC          TRKCNT                    ;'TRACKS MOVED' COUNT.
39e8 d0 c3                      BNE          SEEK2                     ;(ALWAYS TAKEN)
                *
                SEEKEND         EQU          *                         ;END OF SEEKING
39ea 20 00 3a                   JSR          MSWAIT                    ;A=0: WAIT 25 MS SETTLE
39ed 18                         CLC                                    ; AND TURN OFF PHASE
                *
                * TURN HEAD STEPPER PHASE ON/OFF
                *
                SETPHASE        EQU          *
39ee ad 78 04                   LDA          CURTRK                    ;GET CURRENT PHASE
                CLRPHASE        EQU          *
39f1 29 03                      AND          #3                        ;MASK FOR 1 OF 4 PHASES
39f3 2a                         ROL          A                         ;DOUBLE FOR PHASE INDEX
39f4 05 2b                      ORA          SLOTTEMP
39f6 aa                         TAX
39f7 bd 80 c0                   LDA          PHASEOFF,X                ;FLIP THE PHASE
39fa a6 2b                      LDX          SLOTTEMP                  ;RESTORE X-REG
39fc 60         SEEKRTS         RTS                                    ;AND RETURN
                
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; #   END OF FILE:  RDADSEK
                ; #   LINES      :  203
                ; #   CHARACTERS :  8943
                ; #   Formatter  :  Assembly Language Reformatter 1.0.2 (07 January 1998)
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; ####################################################################################################
                ; #   PROJECT  :  APPLE ][ DOS 3.3 C SOURCE CODE LISTING -- (C) APPLE COMPUTER INC. JULY 1983
                ; #   FILE NAME:  MSWAITR
                ; ####################################################################################################
                
                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR MSWAIT'
                **************************
                *   MSWAIT SUBROUTINE    *
                **************************
                *                        *
                *  DELAYS A SPECIFIED    *
                *   NUMBER OF 100 USEC   *
                *   INTERVALS FOR MOTOR  *
                *   ON TIMING.           *
                *                        *
                *   ---- ON ENTRY ----   *
                *  A-REG: HOLDS NUMBER   *
                *        OF 100 USEC     *
                *        INTERVALS TO    *
                *        DELAY.          *
                *                        *
                *   ---- ON EXIT -----   *
                *  A-REG: HOLDS $00.     *
                *  X-REG: HOLDS $00.     *
                *  Y-REG: UNCHANGED.     *
                *  CARRY: SET.           *
                *                        *
                *  MONTIMEL, MONTIMEH    *
                *   ARE INCREMENTED ONCE *
                *   PER 100 USEC INTERVAL*
                *   FOR MOTON ON TIMING. *
                *   ---- ASSUMES ----    *
                *   1 USEC CYCLE TIME    *
                **************************
39fd 00 00 00                   DS           3,0                       ;AVOID PAGE BOUNDARY CROSSING...
3a00 a2 11      MSWAIT          LDX          #$11
3a02 ca         MSW1            DEX                                    ;DELAY 86 USEC.
3a03 d0 fd                      BNE          MSW1
3a05 e6 46                      INC          MONTIMEL
3a07 d0 02                      BNE          MSW2                      ;DOUBLE-BYTE
3a09 e6 47                      INC          MONTIMEH                  ;INCREMENT.
3a0b 38         MSW2            SEC
3a0c e9 01                      SBC          #$1                       ;DONE 'N' INTERVALS?
3a0e d0 f0                      BNE          MSWAIT                    ;(A-REG COUNTS)
3a10 60                         RTS
                AEC1            EQU          *                         ;TELL RELOCATOR WHERE CORE ENDS
                **************************
                *  PHASE ON-, OFF-TIME   *
                *   TABLES IN 100-USEC   *
                *   INTERVALS. (SEEK)    *
                **************************
3a11 01 30 28   ONTABLE         DFB          1,$30,$28
3a14 24 20 1e                   DFB          $24,$20,$1E
3a17 1d 1c 1c                   DFB          $1D,$1C,$1C
3a1a 1c 1c 1c                   DFB          $1C,$1C,$1C
3a1d 70 2c 26   OFFTABLE        DFB          $70,$2C,$26
3a20 22 1f 1e                   DFB          $22,$1F,$1E
3a23 1d 1c 1c                   DFB          $1D,$1C,$1C
3a26 1c 1c 1c                   DFB          $1C,$1C,$1C
                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR NYBBLE TABLES'
                ***************************
                *                         *
                *     6-BIT TO 7-BIT      *
                *  NIBL CONVERSION TABLE  *
                *                         *
                ***************************
                *                         *
                *   CODES WITH MORE THAN  *
                *   ONE PAIR OF ADJACENT  *
                *    ZEROES OR WITH NO    *
                *   ADJACENT ONES (EXCEPT *
                *     B7) ARE EXCLUDED.   *
                *                         *
                *  THIS TABLE MAY *NOT*   *
                *  CROSS A PAGE BOUNDARY! *
                *                         *
                ***************************
3a29 96 97 9a   NIBL            DFB          $96,$97,$9A
3a2c 9b 9d 9e                   DFB          $9B,$9D,$9E
3a2f 9f a6 a7                   DFB          $9F,$A6,$A7
3a32 ab ac ad                   DFB          $AB,$AC,$AD
3a35 ae af b2                   DFB          $AE,$AF,$B2
3a38 b3 b4 b5                   DFB          $B3,$B4,$B5
3a3b b6 b7 b9                   DFB          $B6,$B7,$B9
3a3e ba bb bc                   DFB          $BA,$BB,$BC
3a41 bd be bf                   DFB          $BD,$BE,$BF
3a44 cb cd ce                   DFB          $CB,$CD,$CE
3a47 cf d3 d6                   DFB          $CF,$D3,$D6
3a4a d7 d9 da                   DFB          $D7,$D9,$DA
3a4d db dc dd                   DFB          $DB,$DC,$DD
3a50 de df e5                   DFB          $DE,$DF,$E5
3a53 e6 e7 e9                   DFB          $E6,$E7,$E9
3a56 ea eb ec                   DFB          $EA,$EB,$EC
3a59 ed ee ef                   DFB          $ED,$EE,$EF
3a5c f2 f3 f4                   DFB          $F2,$F3,$F4
3a5f f5 f6 f7                   DFB          $F5,$F6,$F7
3a62 f9 fa fb                   DFB          $F9,$FA,$FB
3a65 fc fd fe                   DFB          $FC,$FD,$FE
3a68 ff                         DFB          $FF
                ;;;                PAGE
                ***************************
                *      7-BIT TO 6-BIT     *
                *     'DENIBLIZE' TABL    *
                *    (16-SECTOR FORMAT)   *
                *                         *
                *       VALID CODES       *
                *     $96 TO $FF ONLY.    *
                *                         *
                *                         *
                *   CODES WITH MORE THAN  *
                *   ONE PAIR OF ADJACENT  *
                *    ZEROES OR WITH NO    *
                *   ADJACENT ONES (EXCEPT *
                *    BIT 7) ARE EXCLUDED. *
                *                         *
                * THIS TABLE *MUST* BE    *
                * ALIGNED AT THE END OF   *
                * A PAGE IN MEMORY!!!     *
                ***************************
                XP              EQU          <*                        ;CURRENT PAGE ADDRESS
                DNIBL           EQU          256*XP                    ;DNIBL TABLE PAGE
                ;;;                PAGE
                ***********************************************
                *
                * GHOST APPEND BUG PATCH BY
                * BILL GRIMM
                *

                PSC1            EQU          *                         ;Tell relocater where to start
                MOVEOF          EQU          *

3a6e f0 05                      BEQ          GOON                      ; YES, RETURN TO CALLING ROUTINE

                ;;;                SKP          4

                FIXIT2          EQU          *
