                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR WRITE ADDRESS'
                ********************************
                *                              *
                *  WRITE ADR FIELD SUBROUTINE  *
                *      (16-SECTOR FORMAT)      *
                *  WRITES SPECIFIED NUMBER OF  *
                *  40-USEC (10-BIT) SELF-SYNC  *
                *  NIBLS, ADR FIELDS 16-SECTOR *
                *  START MARKS ($D5,$AA,$96),  *
                *  BODY (VOLUME, TRACK, SECTOR,*
                *  CHECKSUM), END FIELD MARKS, *
                *  AND THE WRITE TURN-OFF NIBL.*
                *                              *
                ********************************
                *                              *
                *   ------- ON ENTRY -------   *
                *                              *
                *  THE LOCATIONS VOLUME, TRK,  *
                *  AND NSECT MUST CONTAIN THE  *
                *  DESIRED VOLUME, TRACK, AND  *
                *  SECTOR VALUES DESIRED.      *
                *                              *
                *  THE PROPER DRIVE MUST BE    *
                *  ENABLED AND UP TO SPEED IN  *
                *  READ MODE (Q7L, Q6L).       *
                *                              *
                *  X-REG CONTAINS SLOTNUM      *
                *                    TIMES 16. *
                *                              *
                *  Y-REG CONTAINS NUMBER OF    *
                *    SELF-SYNC NIBLS DESIRED   *
                *    MINUS 1.                  *
                *      (0 FOR 256 NIBLS)       *
                *                              *
                ********************************
                *                              *
                *   ------- REQUIRES -------   *
                *                              *
                *         1 USEC CYCLE         *
                *                              *
                ********************************
                *                              *
                *   ------- CAUTION --------   *
                *                              *
                *  MOST OF THIS CODE IS TIME   *
                *  CRITICAL.  OBSERVE ALL      *
                *  'NO PAGE CROSS!' WARNINGS   *
                *  ON BRANCHES.                *
                *                              *
                ********************************
                SWADR1          EQU          *                         ;TELL RELOCATOR WHERE TO BEGIN
                *******************************
3c56 38         WADR16          SEC                                    ;ANTICIPATE WR PROT ERR.
3c57 bd 8d c0                   LDA          Q6H,X                     ;INTO 'WR PROT SENSE' MODE.
3c5a bd 8e c0                   LDA          Q7L,X                     ;SENSE IT (NEG=PROTECTED)
3c5d 30 5e                      BMI          WADRTS                    ;ERR EXIT IF PROTECTED.
3c5f a9 ff                      LDA          #$FF                      ;SELF-SYNC NIBL.
3c61 9d 8f c0                   STA          Q7H,X                     ;WRITE FIRST NIBL.
3c64 dd 8c c0                   CMP          Q6L,X                     ;(4) BACK TO WRITE MODE.
3c67 48                         PHA                                    ;(3) FOR DELAY.
3c68 68                         PLA                                    ;(4)
3c69 20 c3 3c   WSYNC1          JSR          WADRTS1                   ;(12) FOR 40-USEC NIBLS.
3c6c 20 c3 3c                   JSR          WADRTS1                   ;(12)
3c6f 9d 8d c0                   STA          Q6H,X                     ;(5) WRITE NIBL.
3c72 dd 8c c0                   CMP          Q6L,X                     ;(4) (BACK TO WRITE MODE)
3c75 ea                         NOP                                    ;(2) FOR DELAY.
3c76 88                         DEY                                    ;(2) NEXT OF 'N' NIBLS.
3c77 d0 f0                      BNE          WSYNC1                    ;(3) *** NO PAGE CROSS! ***
3c79 a9 d5                      LDA          #$D5                      ;(2) ADR MARK 1.
3c7b 20 d5 3c                   JSR          WNIBLB2                   ;(15,9,6) WRITE IT.
3c7e a9 aa                      LDA          #$AA                      ;(2) ADR MARK 2.
3c80 20 d5 3c                   JSR          WNIBLB2                   ;(15,9,6) WRITE IT.
3c83 a9 96                      LDA          #$96                      ;(2) 16-SECTOR ADR MARK 3.
3c85 20 d5 3c                   JSR          WNIBLB2                   ;(15,9,6) WRITE IT.
3c88 a5 41                      LDA          NVOL                      ;(3)
3c8a 20 c4 3c                   JSR          WBYTE                     ;(14,9,6) WRITE NVOL (ODD, THEN EVEN, BITS.)
3c8d a5 44                      LDA          TRK                       ;(3) WRITE TRACK NUMBER.
3c8f 20 c4 3c                   JSR          WBYTE                     ;(14,9,6) ODD, THEN EVEN, BITS)
3c92 a5 3f                      LDA          NSECT                     ;(3) WRITE SECTOR NUMBER.
3c94 20 c4 3c                   JSR          WBYTE                     ;(14,9,6) (ODD, THEN EVEN, BITS)
3c97 a5 41                      LDA          NVOL                      ;(3)
3c99 45 44                      EOR          TRK                       ;(3) FORM ADR FIELD CHECKSUM.
3c9b 45 3f                      EOR          NSECT                     ;(3)
3c9d 48                         PHA                                    ;(3) SAVE FOR EVEN BITS.
3c9e 4a                         LSR          A                         ;(2) ALIGHN ODD BITS.
3c9f 05 3e                      ORA          AA                        ;(3) SET CLOCK BITS.
                *    (PRECISE TIMING, 32 CYCLES PER NIBL)
3ca1 9d 8d c0                   STA          Q6H,X                     ;(5) WRITE CHECKSUM ODD BITS.
3ca4 bd 8c c0                   LDA          Q6L,X                     ;(4) BACK TO WRITE MODE.
3ca7 68                         PLA                                    ;(4) RECOVER FOR EVEN BITS.
3ca8 09 aa                      ORA          #$AA                      ;(2) SET CLOCK BITS.
3caa 20 d4 3c                   JSR          WNIBLA                    ;(17,9,6) WRITE THEM.
3cad a9 de                      LDA          #$DE                      ;(2) END MARK 1.
3caf 20 d5 3c                   JSR          WNIBLB2                   ;(15,9,6) WRITE IT.
3cb2 a9 aa                      LDA          #$AA                      ;(2) END MARK 2.
3cb4 20 d5 3c                   JSR          WNIBLB2                   ;(15,9,6) WRITE IT.
3cb7 a9 eb                      LDA          #$EB                      ;(2) END MARK 3.
3cb9 20 d5 3c                   JSR          WNIBLB2                   ;(15,9,6) 'WRITE TURN-OFF'
3cbc 18                         CLC                                    ;INDICATE NO WR PROT ERR.
3cbd bd 8e c0   WADRTS          LDA          Q7L,X                     ;OUT OF WRITE MODE.
3cc0 bd 8c c0                   LDA          Q6L,X                     ;TO READ MODE.
3cc3 60         WADRTS1         RTS                                    ;RETURN
3cc4 48         WBYTE           PHA                                    ;(3) PRESERVE FOR EVEN BITS.
3cc5 4a                         LSR          A                         ;(2) ALIGN ODD BITS.
3cc6 05 3e                      ORA          AA                        ;(3) SET CLOCK BITS.
3cc8 9d 8d c0                   STA          Q6H,X                     ;(5) WRITE NIBL.
3ccb dd 8c c0                   CMP          Q6L,X                     ;(4)
3cce 68                         PLA                                    ;(4) RECOVER FOR EVEN BITS.
3ccf ea                         NOP                                    ;(2)
3cd0 ea                         NOP                                    ;(2) FOR DELAY.
3cd1 ea                         NOP                                    ;(2)
3cd2 09 aa                      ORA          #$AA                      ;(2) SET CLOCK BITS.
3cd4 ea         WNIBLA          NOP                                    ;(2) (17,9,6) ENTRY.
3cd5 ea         WNIBLB2         NOP                                    ;(2) (15,9,6) ENTRY.
3cd6 48                         PHA                                    ;(3) FOR
3cd7 68                         PLA                                    ;(4) DELAY.
3cd8 9d 8d c0   WRNIBL          STA          Q6H,X                     ;(5) WRITE NIBL.
3cdb dd 8c c0                   CMP          Q6L,X                     ;(4)
3cde 60                         RTS                                    ;(6) RETURN.
                EWADR1          EQU          *                         ;TELL RELOCTR WHERE TO STOP
                XP2             EQU          <(*+255)                  ;H.O. ADDRESS NEXT PAGE
                XP2H            EQU          256*XP2                   ;NOW AS 16-BITS
3cdf 00 00 00                   DS           XP2H-*,0                  ;PAD OUT TO PAGE BOUNDARY..
3ce2 00 00 00
3ce5 00 00 00
3ce8 00 00 00
3ceb 00 00 00
3cee 00 00 00
3cf1 00 00 00
3cf4 00 00 00
3cf7 00 00 00
3cfa 00 00 00
3cfd 00 00 00

                ; #   END OF FILE:  WRITADR
                ; #   LINES      :  123
                ; #   CHARACTERS :  6714
                ; #   Formatter  :  Assembly Language Reformatter 1.0.2 (07 January 1998)

                ; #   FILE NAME:  RWTSONE

                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR RWTS'
                ****************************
                *         DISK II          *
                * READ/WRITE TRACK-SECTOR  *
                *                          *
                *   COPYRIGHT 1978 BY      *
                *  APPLE COMPUTER, INC.    *
                *                          *
                *  ALL RIGHTS RESERVED     *
                *                          *
                *      R. WIGGINTON        *
                *                          *
                *  MODIFIED: 07/13/79      *
                *     R. AURICCHIO         *
                *  ADDED WAIT-SEEK WHEN    *
                *   POWERING-UP MOTOR.     *
                *                          *
                *  MODIFIED: 10/25/79      *
                *     R. AURICCHIO         *
                *  ADDED DIAGMODE DISPLAYS *
                *   FOR ACTIVITY ANALYSIS. *
                ****************************
                ASC2            EQU          *                         ;TELL RELOCTR WHERE RWTS BEGINS
                *********************************
                MOTOROFF        EQU          $C088
                MOTORON         EQU          $C089
                DRV1EN          EQU          $C08A
                DRV2EN          EQU          $C08B
                ******************************
                * STATE MACHINE CONTROLS
                * Q6   Q7   FUNCTION
                * --   --   --------
                * LO   LO   READ
                * HI   LO   SENSE WRITE PROTECT
                * LO   HI   WRITE
                * HI   HI   WRITE LOAD
                ******************************
                DRV1TRK         EQU          $478
                DRV2TRK         EQU          $4F8
                IOBPL           EQU          $48
                IOBPH           EQU          $49
                SLOT            EQU          $5F8                      ;HOLDS SLOT NUM USED
                PTRSDEST        EQU          $3C
                DEVCTBL         EQU          PTRSDEST
                DRIVNO          EQU          $35
                MONTIME         EQU          $46
                SECT            EQU          CSSTV+1
                TRACK           EQU          CSSTV+2
                VOLUME          EQU          CSSTV+3
                MAXSEEKS        EQU          4                         ;MAX FOR SEEKCNT
                SEEKCNT         EQU          $4F8                      ;# RESEEKS BEFORE RECALIBRATE
                RETRYCNT        EQU          $578
                RECALCNT        EQU          $6F8                      ;# RECALIBRATES -1
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;*
                ;;;* DIAGMODE EQUATES...
                ;;;*
                ;;;SP              EQU          $A0                       ;SPACE (INDICATOR OFF)
                ;;;TD              EQU          4                         ;DISPL BETWEEN CHARS
                ;;;TC1             EQU          $1E                       ;^ - RWTS ACTIVE
                ;;;TL1             EQU          $07D0
                ;;;TC2             EQU          $0D                       ;M - MOTOR STARTUP
                ;;;TL2             EQU          TL1+TD
                ;;;TC3             EQU          $13                       ;S - SEEK IN PROGRESS
                ;;;TL3             EQU          TL2+TD
                ;;;TC4             EQU          $01                       ;A - READING ADDRESS
                ;;;TL4             EQU          TL3+TD
                ;;;TC5             EQU          $0C                       ;L - NOT DESIRED SECTOR (LATENCY)
                ;;;TL5             EQU          TL4+1
                ;;;TC6             EQU          $05                       ;E - ADDRESS ERROR
                ;;;TL6             EQU          TL5+1
                ;;;TC7             EQU          $10                       ;P - PRENIBBILIZING
                ;;;TL7             EQU          TL4+TD
                ;;;TC8             EQU          $17                       ;W - WRITING
                ;;;TL8             EQU          TL7+TD
                ;;;TC9             EQU          $12                       ;R - READING
                ;;;TL9             EQU          TL8+TD
                ;;;TC10            EQU          $05                       ;E - READ ERROR
                ;;;TL10            EQU          TL9+TD
                ;;;TC11            EQU          $0F                       ;O - POSTNIBBLIZING
                ;;;TL11            EQU          TL10+TD
                ;;;*
                ;;;SCOUNT          EQU          $2FE                      ;SECTORS-ACCESSED COUNT
                ;;;LCOUNT          EQU          $2FF                      ;LATENCY COUNT
                ;;;TL12            EQU          TL11+TD                   ;LATENCY POSITION
                ;;;                PAGE
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
                **************************
                *                        *
                *     READ/WRITE A       *
                *   TRACK AND SECTOR     *
                *                        *
                **************************
                *                        *
                *   ENTER WITH A & Y     *
                * REGISTERS POINTING TO  *
                * THE I/O CONTROL BLOCK  *
                * (THE 'IOB'). INSIDE    *
                * THE IOB:               *
                *                        *
                * IBTYPE: IOB TYPE CODE  *
                *       (SHOULD BE A 01) *
                *                        *
                * IBSLOT: CONTROLLER SLOT*
                *       NUMBER FOR THIS  *
                *       ACCESS.          *
                *                        *
                * IBDRVN: DRIVE NUMBER   *
                *       FOR THIS ACCESS  *
                *                        *
                * IBVOL: EXPECTED VOLUME *
                *      NUMBER. NOTE THAT *
                *      VOLUME 00 MATCHES *
                *      ANY VOLUME NUMBER *
                *                        *
                * IBTRK: TRACK TO USE    *
                *      THIS ACCESS       *
                *                        *
                * IBSECT: SECTOR NUMBER  *
                *       TO USE THIS TIME *
                *                        *
                * IBDCTP: POINTER TO THE *
                *       DEVICE CHARACTER-*
                *       ISTICS TABLE.    *
                *                        *
                * IBBUFP: POINTER TO THE *
                *       PLACE THE DATA IS*
                *       OR SHOULD BE.    *
                *                        *
                * IBDLEN: AMOUNT OF DATA *
                *       IN BYTES TO BE   *
                *       PROCESSED.       *
                *                        *
                * IBCMD: COMMAND CODE:   *
                *      0-> NULL COMMAND  *
                *      1-> READ SECTOR   *
                *      2-> WRITE SECTOR  *
                *      4-> FORMAT DISK   *
                *                        *
                * IBSTAT: ERROR CODE:    *
                *      0-> NO ERROR      *
                *    $10-> WRITE PROTECT *
                *    $20-> VOLUME ERROR  *
                *    $40-> DRIVE ERROR   *
                *    $80-> READ ERROR    *
                *                        *
                * IBSMOD: LOCATION TO    *
                *       RETURN THE VOLUME*
                *       NUMBER ACTUALLY  *
                *       FOUND.           *
                *                        *
                * IOBPSN: PREVIOUS SLOT  *
                *      NUMBER USED LAST  *
                *      ACCESS.           *
                *                        *
                * IOBPDN: PREVIOUS DRIVE *
                *      NUMBER USED LAST  *
                *      ACCESS.           *
                *                        *
                **************************
                *                        *
                * DEVICE CHARACTERISTICS *
                * TABLE DESCRIPTION:     *
                *                        *
                * DEVICE TYPE CODE       *
                *  (ZERO FOR DISK II)    *
                *                        *
                * NUMBER OF PHASES PER   *
                * TRACK (TWO FOR DISK II)*
                *                        *
                * MOTOR ON TIME IN 100   *
                * MICROSECOND INTERVALS  *
                * COMPLEMENTED. ($D8EF   *
                * FOR DISK II)           *
                *                        *
                **************************
                ;;;                PAGE
3d00 84 48      RWTS            STY          IOBPL                     ;UPON ENTRY, A&Y POINT AT THE
3d02 85 49                      STA          IOBPH                     ;I/O CONTROL BLOCK (IOB)
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDY          #TC1                      ;SAY WE'RE ACTIVE
                ;;;                STY          TL1
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3d04 a0 02                      LDY          #2                        ;SET RECALIBRATE
3d06 8c f8 06                   STY          RECALCNT                  ; COUNT
3d09 a0 04                      LDY          #MAXSEEKS                 ;SET RESEEK
3d0b 8c f8 04                   STY          SEEKCNT                   ; COUNT
3d0e a0 01                      LDY          #1                        ;GET SLOT # FOR THIS OPERATION
3d10 b1 48                      LDA          (IOBPL),Y
3d12 aa                         TAX
3d13 a0 0f                      LDY          #$0F                      ;DID HE CHANGE SLOTS?
3d15 d1 48                      CMP          (IOBPL),Y
3d17 f0 1b                      BEQ          SAMESLOT                  ;IF HE DIDN'T, GOOD FOR HIM!
                *
                * NOW ARE USING A DIFFERENT SLOT.
                * NOW WAIT FOR THIS DRIVE TO TURN OFF
                * TO SENSE MOTOR NOT SPINNING, DATA FROM DISK MUST
                * BE THE SAME FOR AT LEAST 96 MICROSECONDS
3d19 8a                         TXA                                    ;SAVE NEW SLOT #
3d1a 48                         PHA
3d1b b1 48                      LDA          (IOBPL),Y                 ;GET 'OLD SLOT NUMBER'
3d1d aa                         TAX
3d1e 68                         PLA
3d1f 48                         PHA                                    ;PUT BACK ON STACK
3d20 91 48                      STA          (IOBPL),Y                 ;SAVE 'NEW SLOT NUMBER'
3d22 bd 8e c0                   LDA          Q7L,X                     ;GO INTO READ MODE
3d25 a0 08      STILLON         LDY          #$08                      ;TO BE SURE, DATA MUST REMAIN
3d27 bd 8c c0                   LDA          Q6L,X                     ;STABLE FOR 96 MICROSECONDS
3d2a dd 8c c0   NOTSURE         CMP          Q6L,X                     ;DATA STILL CHANGING?
3d2d d0 f6                      BNE          STILLON                   ;IF SO, STILL SPINNING
3d2f 88                         DEY
3d30 d0 f8                      BNE          NOTSURE                   ;STABLE LONG ENOUGH? IF NOT, LOOP
                *
                * PREVIOUS SLOT'S DRIVE NOW OFF...
                *
3d32 68                         PLA                                    ;RESTORE NEW SLOT #
3d33 aa                         TAX
                *
                * NOW CHECK IF THE MOTOR IS ON, THEN START IT
                *
3d34 bd 8e c0   SAMESLOT        LDA          Q7L,X                     ;MAKE SURE IN READ MODE
3d37 bd 8c c0                   LDA          Q6L,X
3d3a a0 08                      LDY          #8                        ;WE MAY HAFTA CHECK SEVERAL TIMES TO BE SURE
                CHKIFON         EQU          *
3d3c bd 8c c0                   LDA          Q6L,X                     ;GET THE DATA
3d3f 48                         PHA                                    ;DELAY FOR DISK DATA TO CHANGE
3d40 68                         PLA
3d41 48                         PHA
3d42 68                         PLA
3d43 8e f8 05                   STX          SLOT
3d46 dd 8c c0                   CMP          Q6L,X                     ;CHECK RUNNING HERE
3d49 d0 03                      BNE          ITISON                    ;=>IT'S ON...
3d4b 88                         DEY                                    ;MAYBE WE DIDN'T CATCH IT
3d4c d0 ee                      BNE          CHKIFON                   ; SO WE'LL TRY AGAIN
                *
                ITISON          EQU          *
3d4e 08                         PHP                                    ;SAVE TEST RESULTS
3d4f bd 89 c0                   LDA          MOTORON,X                 ;TURN ON MOTOR REGARDLESS
3d52 a0 06                      LDY          #6                        ;MOVE OUT ALL POINTERS INTO ZPAGE
3d54 b1 48      PTRMOV          LDA          (IOBPL),Y
3d56 99 36 00                   STA          PTRSDEST-6,Y
3d59 c8                         INY
3d5a c0 0a                      CPY          #$0A                      ;MOVED ALL POINTERS?
3d5c d0 f6                      BNE          PTRMOV
3d5e a0 03                      LDY          #3                        ;SET UP THE
3d60 b1 3c                      LDA          (DEVCTBL),Y               ; MOTOR-ON TIME
3d62 85 47                      STA          MONTIME+1
3d64 a0 02                      LDY          #2                        ;NOW GET PARAMS
3d66 b1 48                      LDA          (IOBPL),Y                 ;DETERMINE DRIVE ONE OR TWO
3d68 a0 10                      LDY          #$10                      ;SAME DRIVE USED BEFORE?
3d6a d1 48                      CMP          (IOBPL),Y
3d6c f0 06                      BEQ          OK                        ;IF SO, DON'T NECESSARILY WAIT FOR MOTOR
3d6e 91 48                      STA          (IOBPL),Y                 ;NOW USING THIS DRIVE
3d70 28                         PLP                                    ;TELL HIM MOTOR WAS OFF
3d71 a0 00                      LDY          #$00                      ;SET ZERO FLAG
3d73 08                         PHP
3d74 6a         OK              ROR          A                         ;BY GOING INTO THE CARRY
3d75 90 05                      BCC          SD1                       ;SELECT DRIVE 2 !
3d77 bd 8a c0                   LDA          DRV1EN,X                  ;ASSUME DRIVE 1 TO HIT
3d7a b0 03                      BCS          DRVSEL                    ;IF WRONG, ENABLE DRIVE 2 INSTEAD
3d7c bd 8b c0   SD1             LDA          DRV2EN,X
                DRVSEL          EQU          *
3d7f 66 35                      ROR          DRIVNO                    ;SAVE SELECTED DRIVE
                *
                * DRIVE SELECTED. IF MOTORING-UP,
                *  WAIT BEFORE SEEKING...
                *
3d81 28                         PLP                                    ;WAS THE MOTOR
3d82 08                         PHP                                    ; PREVIOUSLY OFF?
3d83 d0 0b                      BNE          NOWAIT                    ;=>NO, FORGET WAITING.
3d85 a0 07                      LDY          #7                        ;YES, DELAY 150 MS
3d87 20 00 3a   SEEKW           JSR          MSWAIT
3d8a 88                         DEY
3d8b d0 fa                      BNE          SEEKW
3d8d ae f8 05                   LDX          SLOT                      ;RESTORE SLOT NUMBER
                *
                NOWAIT          EQU          *
                *
                * SEEK TO DESIRED TRACK...
                *
3d90 a0 04                      LDY          #4                        ;SET TO IOBTRK
3d92 b1 48                      LDA          (IOBPL),Y                 ;GET DESIRED TRACK
3d94 20 5a 3e                   JSR          MYSEEK                    ;SEEK!
                *
                * SEE IF MOTOR WAS ALREADY SPINNING.
                *
3d97 28                         PLP                                    ;WAS MOTOR ON?
3d98 d0 11                      BNE          TRYTRK                    ;IF SO, DON'T DELAY, GET IT TODAY!
                *
                *  WAIT FOR MOTOR SPEED TO COME UP.
                *
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDY          #TC2                      ;SAY 'MOTOR COMING ON'
                ;;;                STY          TL2
                ;;;                LDY          #0                        ;CLEAR SECTOR AND
                ;;;                STY          SCOUNT                    ; LATENCY COUNTERS
                ;;;                STY          LCOUNT
                ;;;                LDY          #SP                       ;SHUT OFF THE
                ;;;                STY          TL12                      ; LATENCY INDICATOR
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3d9a a4 47                      LDY          MONTIME+1                 ;IF MOTORTIME IS POSITIVE,
3d9c 10 0d                      BPL          MOTORUP                   ; THEN SEEK WASTED ENUFF TIME FOR US
3d9e a0 12      MOTOF           LDY          #$12                      ;DELAY 100 USEC PER COUNT
3da0 88         CONWAIT         DEY
3da1 d0 fd                      BNE          CONWAIT
3da3 e6 46                      INC          MONTIME
3da5 d0 f7                      BNE          MOTOF
3da7 e6 47                      INC          MONTIME+1
3da9 d0 f3                      BNE          MOTOF                     ;COUNT UP TO $0000
                MOTORUP         EQU          *
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDY          #SP                       ;SAY 'MOTOR RUNNING'
                ;;;                STY          TL2
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON

                *
                * DISK IS NOW UP TO SPEED: READ IT!
                * NOW CHECK: IF IT IS NOT THE FORMAT DISK COMMAND,
                *  LOCATE THE CORRECT SECTOR FOR THIS OPERATION.
                *
                TRYTRK          EQU          *
3dab a0 0c                      LDY          #$0C
3dad b1 48                      LDA          (IOBPL),Y                 ;GET COMMAND CODE #
3daf f0 5a                      BEQ          GALLDONE                  ;IF NULL COMMAND, GO HOME TO BED.
3db1 c9 04                      CMP          #$04                      ;FORMAT THE DISK?
3db3 f0 58                      BEQ          FORMDSK                   ;ALLRIGHT,ALLRIGHT, I WILL...
3db5 6a                         ROR          A                         ;SET CARRY=1 FOR READ, 0 FOR WRITE
3db6 08                         PHP                                    ;AND SAVE THAT
3db7 b0 03                      BCS          TRYTRK2                   ;MUST PRENIBBLIZE FOR WRITE.
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDY          #TC7                      ;SAY 'PRENIBBLIZING'
                ;;;                STY          TL7
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3db9 20 00 38                   JSR          PRENIB16
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDY          #SP                       ;PRENIB FINISHED
                ;;;                STY          TL7
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3dbc a0 30      TRYTRK2         LDY          #$30                      ;ONLY 48 RETRIES OF ANY KIND.
3dbe 8c 78 05                   STY          RETRYCNT
3dc1 ae f8 05   TRYADR          LDX          SLOT                      ;GET SLOT NUM INTO X-REG
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #TC4                      ;SAY 'READING ADDRESS'
                ;;;                STA          TL4
                ;;;                LDA          #SP                       ;SAY 'NO ADDRESS ERROR' (YET)
                ;;;                STA          TL6
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3dc4 20 44 39                   JSR          RDADR16                   ;READ NEXT ADDRESS FIELD
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #SP                       ;ADDRESS-READ DONE
                ;;;                STA          TL4
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3dc7 90 24                      BCC          RDRIGHT                   ;IF READ IT RIGHT, HURRAH!
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #TC6                      ;SAY 'ADDRESS ERROR'
                ;;;                STA          TL6
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3dc9 ce 78 05   TRYADR2         DEC          RETRYCNT                  ;ANOTHER MISTAEK!!
3dcc 10 f3                      BPL          TRYADR                    ; WELL, LET IT GO THIS TIME.,
                *
                * RRRRRECALIBRATE !!!!
                *
                RECAL           EQU          *
3dce ad 78 04                   LDA          CURTRK
3dd1 48                         PHA                                    ;SAVE TRACK WE REALLY WANT
3dd2 a9 60                      LDA          #$60                      ;RECALIBRATE ALL OVER AGAIN!
3dd4 20 95 3e                   JSR          SETTRK                    ;PRETEND TO BE ON TRACK 96
3dd7 ce f8 06                   DEC          RECALCNT                  ;ONCE TOO MANY??
3dda f0 28                      BEQ          DRVERR                    ;TRIED TO RECALIBRATE TOO MANY TIMES, ERROR!
3ddc a9 04                      LDA          #MAXSEEKS                 ;RESET THE
3dde 8d f8 04                   STA          SEEKCNT                   ; SEEK COUNTER
3de1 a9 00                      LDA          #$00
3de3 20 5a 3e                   JSR          MYSEEK                    ;MOVE TO TRACK 00
3de6 68                         PLA
3de7 20 5a 3e   RESEEK          JSR          MYSEEK                    ;GO TO CORRECT TRACK THIS TIME!
3dea 4c bc 3d                   JMP          TRYTRK2                   ;LOOP BACK, TRY AGAIN ON THIS TRACK
                *
                * HAVE NOW READ AN ADDRESS FIELD CORRECTLY.
                * MAKE SURE THIS IS THE TRACK, SECTOR, AND VOLUME DESIRED.
                *
3ded a4 2e      RDRIGHT         LDY          TRACK                     ;ON THE RIGHT TRACK?
3def cc 78 04                   CPY          CURTRK
3df2 f0 1c                      BEQ          RTTRK                     ;IF SO, GOOD
                * NO, DRIVE WAS ON A DIFFERENT TRACK. TRY
                * RESEEKING/RECALIBRATING FROM THIS TRACK
3df4 ad 78 04                   LDA          CURTRK                    ;PRESERVE DESTINATION TRACK
3df7 48                         PHA
3df8 98                         TYA
3df9 20 95 3e                   JSR          SETTRK
3dfc 68                         PLA
3dfd ce f8 04                   DEC          SEEKCNT                   ;SHOULD WE RESEEK?
3e00 d0 e5                      BNE          RESEEK                    ;=>YES, RESEEK
3e02 f0 ca                      BEQ          RECAL                     ;=>NO, RECALIBRATE!
                ***
3e04 68         DRVERR          PLA                                    ;REMOVE CURTRK.
3e05 a9 40                      LDA          #IBDERR                   ;BAD DRIVE ERROR
3e07 28         JMPTO1          PLP
3e08 4c 48 3e                   JMP          HNDLERR
3e0b f0 39      GALLDONE        BEQ          ALLDONE
3e0d 4c af 3e   FORMDSK         JMP          DSKFORM                   ;=>GO TO IT!
                *
                * DRIVE IS ON RIGHT TRACK, CHECK VOLUME MISMATCH
                *
3e10 a0 03      RTTRK           LDY          #3                        ;IS THE RIGHT DISK IN?
3e12 b1 48                      LDA          (IOBPL),Y                 ;GET DESIRED VOLUM
3e14 48                         PHA                                    ;PRESERVE DESIRED VOLUME#
3e15 a5 2f                      LDA          VOLUME                    ;GET ACTUAL VOLUME HERE
3e17 a0 0e                      LDY          #$0E                      ;TELL OPSYS WHAT VOLUME WAS THERE
3e19 91 48                      STA          (IOBPL),Y
3e1b 68                         PLA                                    ;GET DESIRED VOLUME BACK
3e1c f0 08                      BEQ          CORRECTVOL                ;DESIRED VOLUME 00 MATCHES ALL.
3e1e c5 2f                      CMP          VOLUME
3e20 f0 04                      BEQ          CORRECTVOL                ;YUP, IT WAS RIGHT
3e22 a9 20                      LDA          #IBVMME                   ;HE SWITCHED DISCS!
3e24 d0 e1                      BNE          JMPTO1                    ;ALWAYS TAKEN
                CORRECTVOL      EQU          *
3e26 a0 05                      LDY          #5                        ; TO ALLOW FOR INTERLEAVE
3e28 b1 48                      LDA          (IOBPL),Y                 ;GET REQUESTED (LOGICAL) SECTOR
3e2a a8                         TAY                                    ;MOVE TO INDEX REG
3e2b b9 b8 3f                   LDA          INTRLEAV,Y                ;COMPUTE PHYSICAL SECTOR
3e2e c5 2d                      CMP          SECT                      ;DID WE GET THE SECTOR?
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                BEQ          GOTSECT                   ;=>WE FOUND IT!
                ;;;                LDA          #TC5                      ;SAY 'LATENCY'
                ;;;                STA          TL5
                ;;;                LDA          SCOUNT                    ;ARE WE WAITING FOR FIRST SECTOR?
                ;;;                BEQ          NOLAT                     ;=>YES. LATENCY UNPREDICTABLE ANYWAY
                ;;;                INC          LCOUNT                    ;NO, COUNT SECTORS MISSED
                ;;;NOLAT           EQU          *
                ;;;                JMP          TRYADR2                   ;NOW..GET CORRECT SECTOR..
                ;;;                ELSE
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e30 d0 97                      BNE          TRYADR2                   ;NO, KEEP TRYING.
                ;;;                FIN
                *
                * HOORAY! WE GOT THE RIGHT SECTOR!
                *
                GOTSECT         EQU          *
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #SP                       ;SAY 'NO LATENCY'
                ;;;                STA          TL5
                ;;;                INC          SCOUNT                    ;BUMP 'SECTORS-ACCESSED' COUNT
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e32 28                         PLP
3e33 90 1c                      BCC          WRIT                      ;CARRY WAS SET FOR READ OPERATION,
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #TC9                      ;SAY 'READING'
                ;;;                STA          TL9
                ;;;                LDA          #SP                       ;SAY 'NO READ ERROR' (YET)
                ;;;                STA          TL10
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e35 20 dc 38                   JSR          READ16                    ;CLEARED FOR WRITE
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #SP                       ;READ FINISHED
                ;;;                STA          TL9
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e38 08                         PHP                                    ;SAVE STATUS OF READ OPERATION
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                BCC          GOODREAD                  ;NO ERROR
                ;;;                LDA          #TC10                     ;SAY 'READ ERROR'
                ;;;                STA          TL10
                ;;;                JMP          TRYADR2                   ;RETRY ON ERROR
                ;;;*
                ;;;GOODREAD        EQU          *
                ;;;                ELSE
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e39 b0 8e                      BCS          TRYADR2                   ;CARRY SET UPON RETURN IF BAD READ
                ;;;                FIN
3e3b 28                         PLP                                    ;CAREFUL OF STACK
3e3c a2 00                      LDX          #0                        ;SET TO POSTNIBLIZE
3e3e 86 26                      STX          T0                        ; ALL 256 BYTES OF THE SECTOR
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #TC11                     ;SAY 'POSTINIBBLIZING'
                ;;;                STA          TL11
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e40 20 c2 38                   JSR          POSTNB16                  ;DECODE INTO REAL WORLD DATA
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #SP                       ;POSTNIB COMPLETED
                ;;;                STA          TL11
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e43 ae f8 05                   LDX          SLOT                      ;RESTORE SLOTNUM INTO X
3e46 18         ALLDONE         CLC
3e47 24                         DFB          $24                       ;SKIP OVER NEXT BYTE WITH BIT OPCODE
3e48 38         HNDLERR         SEC                                    ;INDICATE AN ERROR
3e49 a0 0d                      LDY          #$0D                      ;GIVE HIM ERROR#
3e4b 91 48                      STA          (IOBPL),Y
3e4d bd 88 c0                   LDA          MOTOROFF,X                ;TURN IT OFF...
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;* AVERAGE LATENCY = LCOUNT/SCOUNT
                ;;;                LDA          LCOUNT                    ;GET TOTAL LATENCY
                ;;;                LDY          #0                        ;CLEAR QUOTIENT
                ;;;DIVIDE          EQU          *
                ;;;                CMP          SCOUNT                    ;DONE?
                ;;;                BCC          PRTLAT                    ;=>YES.PRINT IT
                ;;;                SBC          SCOUNT                    ;REMOVE SCOUNT
                ;;;                INY                                    ;INCREMENT QUOTIENT
                ;;;                BNE          DIVIDE
                ;;;*
                ;;;PRTLAT          TYA
                ;;;                AND          #$0F                      ;MAX LATENCY=15
                ;;;                ORA          #$B0                      ;MAKE ASCII
                ;;;                CMP          #$BA                      ;IS IT A-F?
                ;;;                BCC          PRTL2                     ;=>NO
                ;;;                ADC          #6                        ;ADD 7 (INCLUDES CARRY)
                ;;;PRTL2           STA          TL12                      ;STUFF LATENCY COUNT
                ;;;                LDA          #SP                       ;SAY 'RWTS NOT ACTIVE'
                ;;;                STA          TL1
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e50 60                         RTS
                WRIT            EQU          *
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #TC8                      ;SAY 'WRITING'
                ;;;                STA          TL8
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e51 20 2a 38                   JSR          WRITE16                   ;WRITE NYBBLES NOW
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #SP                       ;WRITE FINISHED
                ;;;                STA          TL8
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e54 90 f0                      BCC          ALLDONE                   ;IF NO ERRORS.
3e56 a9 10                      LDA          #IBWPER                   ;DISK IS WRITE PROTECTED!!
3e58 b0 ee                      BCS          HNDLERR                   ;ALWAYS TAKEN
                *
                * THIS IS THE 'SEEK' ROUTINE
                *  SEEKS TRACK 'N' IN SLOT #X/$10
                * IF DRIVNO IS NEGATIVE, ON DRIVE 1
                * IF DRIVNO IS POSITIVE, ON DRIVE 2
                *
3e5a 48         MYSEEK          PHA                                    ;AND PRESERVE A-REGISTER
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #TC3                      ;SAY 'SEEKING'
                ;;;                STA          TL3
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e5b a0 01                      LDY          #$01                      ;IS THIS A TWO-PHASE DISC?
3e5d b1 3c                      LDA          (DEVCTBL),Y
3e5f 6a                         ROR          A                         ;GET # OF PHASES INTO CARRY
3e60 68                         PLA
3e61 90 08                      BCC          MYSEEK2                   ;IF ONE PHASE PER TRACK
3e63 0a                         ASL          A
3e64 20 6b 3e                   JSR          MYSEEK2
3e67 4e 78 04                   LSR          CURTRK                    ;DIVIDE BACK DOWN
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE
                ;;;                LDA          #SP
                ;;;                STA          TL3                       ;SEEK DONE
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
3e6a 60                         RTS
3e6b 85 2a      MYSEEK2         STA          TRKN                      ;SAVE DESTINATION TRACK(*2)
3e6d 20 8e 3e                   JSR          XTOY                      ;SET Y=SLOT#
3e70 b9 78 04                   LDA          DRV1TRK,Y
3e73 24 35                      BIT          DRIVNO
3e75 30 03                      BMI          WASD0                     ;IS MINUS, ON DRIVE ZERO
3e77 b9 f8 04                   LDA          DRV2TRK,Y
3e7a 8d 78 04   WASD0           STA          CURTRK                    ;THIS IS WHERE I AM
3e7d a5 2a                      LDA          TRKN                      ;AND WHERE I'M GOING TO
3e7f 24 35                      BIT          DRIVNO                    ;NOW UPDATE SLOT DEPENDENT
3e81 30 05                      BMI          ISDRV1                    ;LOCATIONS WITH TRACK
3e83 99 f8 04                   STA          DRV2TRK,Y                 ;INFORMATION
3e86 10 03                      BPL          GOSEEK                    ;ALWAYS TAKEN
3e88 99 78 04   ISDRV1          STA          DRV1TRK,Y
3e8b 4c a0 39   GOSEEK          JMP          SEEK                      ;GO THERE!
3e8e 8a         XTOY            TXA
3e8f 4a                         LSR          A
3e90 4a                         LSR          A
3e91 4a                         LSR          A
3e92 4a                         LSR          A
3e93 a8                         TAY
3e94 60                         RTS
                *
                * THIS SUBROUTINE SETS THE SLOT DEPENDENT TRACK
                * LOCATION.
                *
3e95 48         SETTRK          PHA                                    ;PRESERVE DESTINATION TRACK
3e96 a0 02                      LDY          #$02
3e98 b1 48                      LDA          (IOBPL),Y
3e9a 6a                         ROR          A                         ;GET DRIVE # INTO CARRY
3e9b 66 35                      ROR          DRIVNO                    ;INTO (DRIVNO)
3e9d 20 8e 3e                   JSR          XTOY                      ;SET UP Y-REG
3ea0 68                         PLA
3ea1 0a                         ASL          A                         ;ASSUME TRACK IS HELD *2
3ea2 24 35      SETTRK2         BIT          DRIVNO
3ea4 30 05                      BMI          ONDRV1                    ;IF ON DRIVE 1(1), DRIVNO MINUS
3ea6 99 f8 04                   STA          DRV2TRK,Y
3ea9 10 03                      BPL          SETRTS
3eab 99 78 04   ONDRV1          STA          DRV1TRK,Y
3eae 60         SETRTS          RTS

                ;;;                SBTL         '16-SECTOR FORMATTER'
                ****************************
                *                          *
                *  FORMAT DISK AND RETURN  *
                *                          *
                ****************************
                *
                * EQUATES FOR FORMATTER
                *
                NSYNC           EQU          $45                       ;NUM GAP SELF-SYNC NIBLS
                *
                ;;;                REP          40
                DSKFORM         EQU          *
                ;;;                DO           DIAGMODE                  ;ELIMINATE FMTR FROM DIAG ASSEMBLY
                ;;;                LST          OFF
                ;;;                ELSE
3eaf a0 03                      LDY          #3
3eb1 b1 48                      LDA          (IOBPL),Y                 ;VOLUME NUMBER IN IOB.
3eb3 85 41                      STA          NVOL                      ;FOR FORMATTER.
3eb5 a9 aa                      LDA          #$AA                      ;SET Z-PAG LOC TO $AA FOR
3eb7 85 3e                      STA          AA                        ;TIME DEPENDENT REFERENCES.
3eb9 a0 56                      LDY          #$56
3ebb a9 00                      LDA          #0
3ebd 85 44                      STA          TRK                       ;TRACK NUMBER, 0 TO 34
3ebf 99 ff 3b   CLRNBUF2        STA          NBUF2-1,Y                 ;CLEAR NBUFS TO WRITE
3ec2 88                         DEY                                    ;ZERO SECTORS.
3ec3 d0 fa                      BNE          CLRNBUF2
3ec5 99 00 3b   CLRNBUF1        STA          NBUF1,Y
3ec8 88                         DEY
3ec9 d0 fa                      BNE          CLRNBUF1
3ecb a9 50                      LDA          #$50
3ecd 20 95 3e                   JSR          SETTRK                    ;FAKE LIKE ON TRACK 80.
3ed0 a9 28                      LDA          #$28
3ed2 85 45                      STA          NSYNC                     ;BEGIN WITH 40 SELF-SYNC NIBLS.
3ed4 a5 44      FORMTRK         LDA          TRK
3ed6 20 5a 3e                   JSR          MYSEEK                    ;GOTO NEXT TRACK.
3ed9 20 0d 3f                   JSR          WTRACK16                  ;WRITE AND VERIFY TRACK.
3edc a9 08      FORMERR1        LDA          #8                        ;'UNABLE TO FORMAT' ERR CODE.
3ede b0 24                      BCS          FORMERR                   ;CONTINUE IF NO ERROR.
3ee0 a9 30                      LDA          #$30                      ;UP TO 48 SECTOR RETRIES
3ee2 8d 78 05                   STA          RETRYCNT                  ;TO FIND SECTOR 0.
3ee5 38         FINDS0          SEC                                    ;ANTICIPATE 'UNABLE TO FORMAT'
3ee6 ce 78 05                   DEC          RETRYCNT                  ;DONE 48 RETRIES?
3ee9 f0 19                      BEQ          FORMERR                   ;IF SO, 'UNABLE TO FORMAT' ERR.
3eeb 20 44 39                   JSR          RDADR16                   ;READ ADR FIELD.
3eee b0 f5                      BCS          FINDS0                    ;RETRY IF ERR.
3ef0 a5 2d                      LDA          SECT                      ;CHECK SECTOR THAT WAS READ.
3ef2 d0 f1                      BNE          FINDS0                    ;CONTINUE SEARCHING IF NOT SECT 0.
3ef4 20 dc 38                   JSR          READ16                    ;NOW READ DATA FIELD.
3ef7 b0 ec                      BCS          FINDS0                    ;CONTINUE SEARCH IF ERR.
                *       (NOW POSITIONED PROPERLY FOR NEXT TRACK)
3ef9 e6 44                      INC          TRK                       ;INCREMENT TRACK NUMBER.
3efb a5 44                      LDA          TRK
3efd c9 23                      CMP          #$23                      ;CONTINUE IF LESS THAN 35.
3eff 90 d3                      BCC          FORMTRK
3f01 18                         CLC                                    ;CLEAR CARRY TO INDICATE 'NO ERR'
3f02 90 05                      BCC          FORMDONE                  ;ELSE TURN OFF MOTOR AND RETURN.
3f04 a0 0d      FORMERR         LDY          #$0D
3f06 91 48                      STA          (IOBPL),Y                 ;RETURN ERROR CODE.
3f08 38                         SEC                                    ;SET CARRY TO INDICATE ERR.
3f09 bd 88 c0   FORMDONE        LDA          MOTOROFF,X                ;TURN MOTOR OFF.
3f0c 60                         RTS                                    ;AND RETURN.
                ;;;                PAGE
                ******************************
                *                            *
                *   WRITE TRACK SUBROUTINE   *
                *                            *
                ******************************
3f0d a9 00      WTRACK16        LDA          #0
3f0f 85 3f                      STA          NSECT                     ;SECTOR NUMBER, 0 TO 15.
3f11 a0 80                      LDY          #128                      ;128 NIBS PRIOR SECTOR 0
3f13 d0 02                      BNE          WSECT0                    ; TO INSURE NO BLANK SPOT BETW 15 & 0
3f15 a4 45      WSECT           LDY          NSYNC                     ;CURRENT NUM OF GAP SELF-SYNC NIBLS.
                WSECT0          EQU          *
3f17 20 56 3c                   JSR          WADR16                    ;WRITE GAP AND ADR FIELD.
3f1a b0 6b                      BCS          WEXIT2                    ;ERR IF WRITE PROTECTED.
3f1c 20 2a 38                   JSR          WRITE16                   ;WRITE SECTOR FROM NBUF1, NBUF2.
3f1f b0 66                      BCS          WEXIT2                    ;ERR IF WRITE PROTECTED.
3f21 e6 3f                      INC          NSECT                     ;NEXT OF 16 SECTORS.
3f23 a5 3f                      LDA          NSECT
3f25 c9 10                      CMP          #$10
3f27 90 ec                      BCC          WSECT                     ;CONTINUE IF NOT DONE.
                ;;;                PAGE
                *****************************
                *                           *
                *     VERIFY ROUTINE        *
                *                           *
                *  VERIFIES THAT THE FIRST  *
                *  SECTOR ENCOUNTERED IS    *
                *  SECTOR 0, AND THAT ALL   *
                *  16 SECTORS ARE READABLE  *
                *  WITH MINIMAL RETRIES.    *
                *  (2 REVOLUTIONS MAXIMUM)  *
                *                           *
                *  IF FIRST SECTOR IS NOT   *
                *  SECTOR 0 THEN THE        *
                *  CURRENT NUMBER OF SELF-  *
                *  SYNC NIBLS IS DECR'D BY  *
                *  1 (IF ALREADY LESS THAN  *
                *  16) OR BY 2. THEN SECTOR *
                *  15 IS LOCATED SO AS TO   *
                *  POSITION THE NEW TRACK   *
                *  REWRITE.                 *
                *                           *
                *  IF UNABLE TO READ ANY    *
                *  SECTOR THEN THE ENTIRE   *
                *  TRACK IS REWRITTEN.      *
                *                           *
                *  AFTER VERIFYING TRACK 0, *
                *  THE NUMBER OF SELF-SYNC  *
                *  NIBLS, NSYNC, IS DECR'D  *
                *  BY 2 (IF STILL 16 OR     *
                *  GREATER).                *
                *                           *
                *****************************
                ;;;                PAGE
3f29 a0 0f      VTRACK          LDY          #$F
3f2b 84 3f                      STY          NSECT                     ;SET 16 BYTES OF
3f2d a9 30                      LDA          #$30                      ;SECTOR FOUND TABLE
3f2f 8d 78 05                   STA          RETRYCNT                  ;TO $30 (MARK THEM).
3f32 99 a8 3f   CLRFOUND        STA          FOUND,Y
3f35 88                         DEY
3f36 10 fa                      BPL          CLRFOUND
3f38 a4 45                      LDY          NSYNC                     ;DELAY 50 USEC FOR EVERY
3f3a 20 87 3f   S0DELAY         JSR          WEXIT2                    ;(12)  SELF-SYNC NIBL
3f3d 20 87 3f                   JSR          WEXIT2                    ;(12)  EXPECTED TO INSURE
3f40 20 87 3f                   JSR          WEXIT2                    ;(12)  PROPER GAP PRIOR SECTOR 0.
3f43 48                         PHA                                    ;(3)
3f44 68                         PLA                                    ;(4)
3f45 ea                         NOP                                    ;(2)
3f46 88                         DEY                                    ;(2)
3f47 d0 f1                      BNE          S0DELAY                   ;(3)
3f49 20 44 39                   JSR          RDADR16                   ;READ NEXT ADDRESS FIELD.
3f4c b0 23                      BCS          S15LOC                    ;ERR, LOCATE SECT 15 AND REWRITE TRK.
3f4e a5 2d                      LDA          SECT                      ;WAS IT SECTOR 0?
3f50 f0 15                      BEQ          VDATA                     ;YES, NOW VERIFY DATA FIELD.
3f52 a9 10                      LDA          #$10
3f54 c5 45                      CMP          NSYNC                     ;DECR NSYNC BY 1 IF LESS THAN
3f56 a5 45                      LDA          NSYNC                     ;16, BY 2 IF NOT LESS.
3f58 e9 01                      SBC          #1
3f5a 85 45                      STA          NSYNC
3f5c c9 05                      CMP          #5                        ;IF LESS THAN 5, UNRECOVERABLE
3f5e b0 11                      BCS          S15LOC                    ;ERR, ELSE REWRITE AFTER DATA FLD 15.
3f60 38         VERR            SEC                                    ;DRIVE EXTREMELY FAST OR
3f61 60                         RTS                                    ;OTHER SEVERE ERROR.
3f62 20 44 39   VSECT           JSR          RDADR16                   ;READ AN ADDRESS FIELD.
3f65 b0 05                      BCS          VERR1                     ;RETRY IF ERR.
3f67 20 dc 38   VDATA           JSR          READ16                    ;READ DATA FIELD.
3f6a 90 1c                      BCC          SECTOK                    ;(GOOD)
3f6c ce 78 05   VERR1           DEC          RETRYCNT                  ;NEXT OF 48 SECTOR TRIES.
3f6f d0 f1                      BNE          VSECT                     ;(KEEP TRYING)
3f71 20 44 39   S15LOC          JSR          RDADR16                   ;READ ADDRESS FIELD.
3f74 b0 0b                      BCS          NOTS15                    ;ERR, TRY UP TO 128 TIMES.
3f76 a5 2d                      LDA          SECT                      ;SECTOR THAT WAS READ.
3f78 c9 0f                      CMP          #$F                       ;SECTOR 15?
3f7a d0 05                      BNE          NOTS15                    ;NO, CONTINUE SEARCHING.
3f7c 20 dc 38                   JSR          READ16                    ;READ DATA FIELD.
3f7f 90 8c                      BCC          WTRACK16                  ;WRITE TRACK FROM HERE IF NO ERR.
3f81 ce 78 05   NOTS15          DEC          RETRYCNT                  ;$FF TO $7F, 128 TRIES.
3f84 d0 eb                      BNE          S15LOC                    ;TRY FOR SECT 15 AGAIN.
3f86 38                         SEC                                    ;SET CARRY TO INDICATE VERIFY ERR.
3f87 60         WEXIT2          RTS                                    ;AND RETURN TO FORMATTER.
3f88 a4 2d      SECTOK          LDY          SECT                      ;THIS IS SECTOR READ.
3f8a b9 a8 3f                   LDA          FOUND,Y                   ;ALREADY FOUND?
3f8d 30 dd                      BMI          VERR1                     ;YES, IGNORE IT.
3f8f a9 ff                      LDA          #$FF
3f91 99 a8 3f                   STA          FOUND,Y                   ;INDICATE THIS SECT NOW FOUND.
3f94 c6 3f                      DEC          NSECT                     ;FOUND 16 SECTORS?
3f96 10 ca                      BPL          VSECT                     ;NO, LOOK FOR NEXT.
3f98 a5 44                      LDA          TRK
3f9a d0 0a                      BNE          WEXIT1                    ;IF TRACK 0 AND NSYNC > 16
3f9c a5 45                      LDA          NSYNC                     ;(NUM GAP SYNC NIBLS)
3f9e c9 10                      CMP          #$10                      ;THEN SUBTRACT 2 FROM NSYNC
3fa0 90 e5                      BCC          WEXIT2                    ;TO AVOID RETRIES ON LATER TRKS.
3fa2 c6 45                      DEC          NSYNC
3fa4 c6 45                      DEC          NSYNC
3fa6 18         WEXIT1          CLC                                    ;INDICATE NO ERROR.
3fa7 60                         RTS                                    ;RETURN.
                ******************************
                AEC2            EQU          *                         ;TELL RELOCTR WHERE RWTS ENDS
                ******************************
3fa8 00 00 00   FOUND           DFB          0,0,0,0                   ;'SECTOR FOUND' TABLE.
3fab 00
3fac 00 00 00                   DFB          0,0,0,0
3faf 00
3fb0 00 00 00                   DFB          0,0,0,0
3fb3 00
3fb4 00 00 00                   DFB          0,0,0,0
3fb7 00
                ;;;                FIN
                ;;;                LST          ON
                ;;;                REP          40
                * THIS TABLE IS USED TO TRANSLATE
                *  LOGICAL (REQUESTED) SECTOR NUMBER
                *  TO PHYSICAL SECTOR NUMBER. THE
                *  DISKETTE IS FORMATTED WITH ALL
                *  SECTORS IN MONOTONICALLY INCREASING
                *  ORDER. THE TRANSLATION WILL ALLOW
                *  TIME BETWEEN SECTORS FOR READS.
                *
                ;;;                REP          40
                *
                * NOTE: THE CURRENT IMPLEMENTATION OF DOS
                *  USUALLY ACCESSES SECTORS IN DECREASING
                *  ORDER ON A TRACK. THUS WE WILL
                *  TRANSLATE IN REVERSE ORDER...
                *
                * THE INTERLEAVE IS THEN 9:1
                *
                * NOTE: WE MAP LOGICAL SECTOR 0
                *  INTO PHYSICAL SECTOR 0 SO THAT
                *  WRITING OF BOOT DURING 'INIT'
                *  IS CORRECT FOR SECTOR ZERO.
                *
                INTRLEAV        EQU          *
3fb8 00 0d 0b                   DFB          $00,$0D,$0B,$09
3fbb 09
3fbc 07 05 03                   DFB          $07,$05,$03,$01
3fbf 01
3fc0 0e 0c 0a                   DFB          $0E,$0C,$0A,$08
3fc3 08
3fc4 06 04 02                   DFB          $06,$04,$02,$0F
3fc7 0f

                ;;;                SBTL         "DOS PATCHES"
                ********************************
                *
                * DOS 3.2 PATCHES BY DICK HUSTON
                *
                ********************************
                * AFTER THE FACT PATCHES
                * CLRBYTE CALLED FROM DOS2 LABEL SOPTS +7 LINES
                * CLRSTS1 CALLED FROM DOS3 LABEL ERROR +2 LINES
                * ERROR9X CALLED FROM DOS5 LABEL ERROR9
                *
                *
                ;;;                REP          40
                *
                * DOS 3.3 REVISION B PATCH
                *
                ;;;                REP          40
                *****************************
                SDP1            EQU          *                         ;START OF DOS PATCHES
                RCPATCH         EQU          *
3fc8 20 93 fe                   JSR          SETVID
3fcb ad 81 c0                   LDA          $C081
3fce ad 81 c0                   LDA          $C081
3fd1 a9 00                      LDA          #0
3fd3 8d 00 e0                   STA          $E000
                ;;;                DO           DOS33B
3fd6 20 76 3a                   JSR          OFF80
3fd9 4c 44 37                   JMP          RCBACK
                ;;;                ELSE
                ;;;                JMP          RCBACK
                ;;;                DS           3,0
                ;;;                FIN
                ******************************
3fdc 8d 63 2a   CLRBYTE         STA          TEMP1A
3fdf 8d 70 2a                   STA          CB                        ;SET TYPE PARAM DEFAUTL=0
3fe2 8d 71 2a                   STA          CB+1
3fe5 60                         RTS
                ;;;                SKP          4
3fe6 20 5b 27   CLRSTS1         JSR          CLRSTS
3fe9 8c b7 2a                   STY          RSTATE                    ;PREVENTS FOREVER 'FILE NOT FOUND'
3fec 60                         RTS                                    ; IN APPLESOFT
                *****************************
3fed 20 7e 2e   ERROR9X         JSR          RTNFCB
3ff0 ae 9b 33                   LDX          ENTSTK                    ;GET STACK
3ff3 9a                         TXS                                    ;MESSY MESSY
3ff4 20 16 23                   JSR          CLALL                     ;GO CLOSE EVERYBODY
3ff7 ba                         TSX
3ff8 8e 9b 33                   STX          ENTSTK                    ;RESTORE SAVE STK
3ffb a9 09                      LDA          #9
3ffd 4c 85 33                   JMP          ERRORA                    ;AND BACK
                ******************************
                EDP1            EQU          *-1                       ;END OF DOS PATCHES FOR RELOCTR
                ENDOFDOS        EQU          *

                ;;;                FIN
